[[[EARLY AMERICAN
HISTORY]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

\

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
[[LESSON 1]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*Christopher Columbus*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Quōdam in oppīdō Ītaliae ōlim nātus est puer, quī Columbus appellābātur.
Diū in patris officīnā^[^1]^ labōrāvit. Sed prope erat mare, puerque
saepe ad lītus ībat, ut vidēret nāvēs, quae ē portū ad terrās exībant
dīversās. In nāvibus erant hominēs multī, et Columbus mare ipse trānsīre
saepe voluit; tum autem pecūniam nūllam habēbat. Sed posteā, cum iam
iuvenis esset, usque ad^[^2]^ Britanniam et Āfricam nāvigāvit.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Illīs temporibus^[^3]^ nautae timēbant mare Atlanticum, cursumque prope
lītus tenēbant. Interdum^[^4]^ autem secundum Āfricae ōram^[^5]^ longē
nāvigātum erat^[^6]^, quod Henrīcus, rēx Lūsitāniae, invenīre viam
volēbat, quā^[^7]^ nāvēs circum Āfricam prōgressae, ad Asiam pervenīre
possent^[^8]^.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

::: {about="#mwt4"}
:::

[[]{#c1_A_First_Latin_Reader_1.xhtml_pagename12}]{#c1_A_First_Latin_Reader_1.xhtml_id-2
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/12" about="#mwt15"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}[Quīdam]{about="#mwt16"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}^[^9]^[ tum crēdēbant terram esse
rotundam]{about="#mwt16"}^[^10]^[, Columbusque etiam spērāre coeperat se
trānsīre mare Atlanticum posse, et ita ad Asiam pervenīre; nēmō enim
intellegēbat terram tam magnam esse, nec]{about="#mwt16"}^[^11]^[
Columbus ipse suspicātus est Americam
interpōnī]{about="#mwt16"}^[^12]^[. ]{about="#mwt16"}
::::::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}

:::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
::::::: text
::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt19" lang="la"}
[[]{#c2_A_First_Latin_Reader_2.xhtml_pagename12-n40}]{#c2_A_First_Latin_Reader_2.xhtml_id-2-n39
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/12" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

[]{.mw-empty-elt about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
[[LESSON 2]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*Christopher Columbus (Continued)*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Interim Henrīcus rēx mortuus erat. Columbus tamen in Lūsitāniam
profectus est, ut rēgī tum ibi rēgnum obtinentī^[^13]^ cōnsilium suum
aperīret; sed pecūniam, quam petēbat, dare nōlēbat rēx. Ex Lūsitāniā
igitur in Hispāniam iter fēcit Columbus; ubi^[^14]^ rēx Ferdinandus
Isabellaque bellum cum Maurīs gerēbant, nec quisquam^[^15]^ advenam
libenter audiēbat. Itaque ille, ubi^[^16]^ cōgnōvit rēgem et rēgīnam
nōlle ea^[^17]^ facere quae spērāverat, ad Galliam versus profectus est;
cum autem montēs trānsīret, nūntius est cōnsecūtus, qui dīxit
velle^[^18]^ iam Isabellam parāre nāvēs pecūniamque dare. Quā rē audītā,
Columbus laetus^[^19]^ rediit, nautāsque validōs quaerere coepit; sed
paene omnēs, perīculum veritī^[^20]^, cum eō nāvigāre nōlēbant.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Postrēmō autem ē portū exiit tribus cum nāvibus parvīs, quae Pinta,
Nīna, Santaque Marīa appellābantur; cumque
[[]{#c2_A_First_Latin_Reader_2.xhtml_pagename13}]{#c2_A_First_Latin_Reader_2.xhtml_id-3
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/13"}paucōs diēs
nāvigāsset^[^21]^,ad īnsulās quāsdam pervēnit, in quibus inveniuntur
plūrimae^[^22]^ avēs, quārum cantus est pulcherrimus.Tum per īgnōtum
mare fortiter prōgressus est.
:::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
:::

[]{#c3_A_First_Latin_Reader_3.xhtml}

::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}
::: {.titulusHeaderBox about="#mwt1"}
:::

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}
:::

:::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
::::::: text
::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt18" lang="la"}
[[]{#c3_A_First_Latin_Reader_3.xhtml_pagename13-n64}]{#c3_A_First_Latin_Reader_3.xhtml_id-3-n63
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/13" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

[]{.mw-empty-elt about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
[[LESSON 3]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*Christopher Columbus (Continued)*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Cum multa mīlia passuum Columbus nāvigāsset neque^[^23]^ terram vīdisset
ūllam, nautae vehementer timēre coepērunt, quod multa^[^24]^ audīverant
dē nāvibus, quae longē per mare Atlanticum prōgressae domum numquam
posteā redierant; in Hispāniam igitur statim redīre volēbant, dux tamen
nōluit. Quārē illī prīmō habuērunt in animō Columbum etiam in mare
iacere; postrēmo autem eōrum animī īrātī ā duce mītigātī sunt^[^25]^.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Ōlim nauta quīdam crēdēbat sē terram vidēre, et omnēs gaudēbant;
nūbem^[^26]^ autem vīderat ille, nōn terram. Sed paucīs post
diēbus^[^27]^ rāmum invēnērunt et bācās in marī natantēs^[^28]^, ac
Columbus sēnsit sē iam^[^29]^ terrae appropinquāre. Mox noctū ignem
quoque in lītore vīdērunt, ac māne ad īnsulam pervēnērunt parvam, ubi
laetī in harēnam ēgressī paucōs diēs morāti sunt.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Inde profectus, Columbus aliās quoque īnsulās adiit, in quibus erat ea,
quae Cūba appellātur. Gazās tamen invenīre nōn potuit^[^30]^, quās
quaerēbat. Putābat enim sē iam ad
[[]{#c3_A_First_Latin_Reader_3.xhtml_pagename14}]{#c3_A_First_Latin_Reader_3.xhtml_id-4
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/14"}Asiam pervēnisse;
quārē incolās eārum īnsulārum, quās adierat, Indōs appellāvit.
:::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
:::

1.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c3_A_First_Latin_Reader_3.xhtml_cite_ref-1-n65){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}

    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"} cf. **nec**, [p. 2, l.
    4]( "A First Latin Reader/2"){.noteref
    xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink"}.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c3_A_First_Latin_Reader_3.xhtml_cite_note-1-n75}
2.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c3_A_First_Latin_Reader_3.xhtml_cite_ref-2-n66){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [[**multa:**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/multus#Latin "wiktionary:multus"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"} *many (stories).*]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c3_A_First_Latin_Reader_3.xhtml_cite_note-2-n76}

    [[**mītigātī
    sunt:**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/mitigo#Latin "wiktionary:mitigo"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"} *were calmed* (**mītigō,
    I**).]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c3_A_First_Latin_Reader_3.xhtml_cite_note-3-n77}
4.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c3_A_First_Latin_Reader_3.xhtml_cite_ref-4-n68){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [[**nūbem:**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/nubes#Latin "wiktionary:nubes"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"} **nūbēs, -is,** [f.]{.smallcaps},
    *cloud*.]{.mw-reference-text

    [**paucīs post diēbus:** *a few days later,* lit. *afterward by a
    few days* (abl. of degree of difference).]{.mw-reference-text

::::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
:::::::: text
:::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt21" lang="la"}
[[]{#c4_A_First_Latin_Reader_4.xhtml_pagename14-n84}]{#c4_A_First_Latin_Reader_4.xhtml_id-4-n83
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/14" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 4]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*Christopher Columbus (Concluded)*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Indī Columbum amābant; isque, cum ad Hispānīam reditūrus esset^[^31]^,
in īnsulā quādam colōniam parvam relīquit. Colōnī tamen iniūriās mox
Indīs fēcērunt ac brevī^[^32]^ ad ūnum^[^33]^ ab eīs interfectī sunt.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Interim Columbus ipse domum properābat; subitō autem, cum laetus^[^34]^
per mare nāvigāret, tempestāte maximā coortā, nāvēs fluctibus paene
complētae sunt. Tum ille scrīpsit litterās, quās in dōlia^[^35]^
conditās^[^36]^ in mare iēcit; crēdēbat enim nūllam iam esse spem,
putābatque dōlia posse ad lītus ventīs ferrī, cīvēsque suōs ita
certiōrēs fieri^[^37]^ dē eīs īnsulīs, quās ipse invēnerat. Sed maris
violentiam^[^38]^ nāvēs sustinuērunt, et Columbus in Hispāniam
incolumis^[^39]^ pervēnit; ubi^[^40]^ rēx et rēgīna eius rēbus
gestīs^[^41]^ gaudēbant, cumque fēcērunt insulārum praefectum.^[^42]^

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Posteā ad Americam Columbus semel atque iterum nāvigāvit. Rem autem haud
fēlīciter gessit, inopsque^[^43]^ postrēmō mortuus est. Etiam tum
terrās, quās invēnerat, Asiae partem esse crēdēbat.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

::: {about="#mwt4"}
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

::::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
:::::::: text
:::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt20" lang="la"}
[[]{#c5_A_First_Latin_Reader_5.xhtml_pagename15}]{#c5_A_First_Latin_Reader_5.xhtml_id-5
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/15" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 5]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*The Cabots*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Interim vir quīdam, nōmine Cabot, ā^[^44]^ Britanniā cum nāve parvā
nautīsque paucīs profectus est atque ad Americam pervēnit. Quī^[^45]^
nōn sōlum īnsulās adiit, sed etiam eam^[^46]^ terram, quae nunc Canada
appellātur. Posteā īdem cum fīliō ad Americam iterum nāvigāvit, ac multa
mīlia passuum secundum lītus prōgressus, Indōs vīdit multōs. Interim
nautae prope īnsulās quāsdam morābantur, ut piscīs caperent. Quī,
cum^[^47]^ domum incolumēs^[^48]^ redīssent, amīcīs suīs multa^[^49]^
nārrāvērunt dē rēbus mīrīs, quās vīderant; quīn etiam dīxērunt sē
ursās^[^50]^ vīdisse in mare prōgredientēs, ut piscīs raperent.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Cabot fīlius^[^51]^ posteā omnīs in partēs nāvigāvit, ac diū cōnātus est
viam invenīre, quā^[^52]^ circum Eurōpam nāvigāre atque ita ad Asiam
pervenīre posset; eam tamen viam numquam invēnit, neque^[^53]^ nunc nōta
est. Ōlim, cum iam esset senex neque ipse diūtius^[^54]^ nāvigāre
posset, dōna magna dīcitur^[^55]^ dedisse nautīs quibusdam, quōs forte
cōgnōverat parvā in nāve ad terrās īgnōtās profectūrōs esse^[^56]^; adeō
nāvīs nautāsque semper amāvit.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

::: {about="#mwt4"}
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

[]{#c6_A_First_Latin_Reader_6.xhtml}

::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}

:::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
::::::: text
::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt14" lang="la"}
[[]{#c6_A_First_Latin_Reader_6.xhtml_pagename16}]{#c6_A_First_Latin_Reader_6.xhtml_id-6
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/16" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

[]{.mw-empty-elt about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
[[LESSON 6]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*Captain John Smith*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Quod colōnī, quī ex Hispāniā in Americam dēductī erant, aurum multum et
argentum ibi inveniēbant, Britannī quoque colōnōs quōsdam mīsērunt, quī
castra pōnerent^[^57]^ eā^[^58]^ in terrā, quae Virginia appellātur.
Quōs^[^59]^ colōnōs Indī mox adortī sunt, sagittīsque occidērunt paucōs;
castra tamen prope rīpam posita erant, ac nautae ē nāvibus tēla plūrima
inmīsērunt in hostēs, quī sē celeriter in silvās recipere coāctī sunt.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Brevī autem erat perīculum etiam maius; nam paene omnis cōnsūmptus est
cibus, quem colōni ā Britanniā nāvibus^[^60]^ vēxerant. Statim igitur
eōrum dux, nōmine Faber, vir fortis, cum scaphā paucīsque mīlitibus
adversō flūmine^[^61]^ longē prōgressus est, ut frūmentum quaereret,
quod incolae libenter dabant prō nūgis^[^62]^ quās colōnī sēcum
ferēbant.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Posteā dux īdem, cum iterum profectus esset ut invenīret viam, quā ad
Asiam nāvēs pervenīre possent (omnēs^[^63]^ enim iam intellegēbant
Americam nōn esse Asiae partem), fortiter pugnāns ab Indīs captus est.
:::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}

    [**adversō flūmine**: *up stream;* lit. what?]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c6_A_First_Latin_Reader_6.xhtml_cite_note-5-n152}
6.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c6_A_First_Latin_Reader_6.xhtml_cite_ref-6-n146){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}

    *trifles*.]{.mw-reference-text

    noun use of the masc. pl. is very frequent.]{.mw-reference-text

[[]{#c7_A_First_Latin_Reader_7.xhtml_pagename16-n156}]{#c7_A_First_Latin_Reader_7.xhtml_id-6-n155
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/16" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

[]{.mw-empty-elt about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
[[LESSON 7]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*Captain John Smith* (Continued)
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Postrēmō tamen in colōniam incolumis reductus, Faber posteā per lītora
omnia iter fēcit; spērābat enim semper
[[]{#c7_A_First_Latin_Reader_7.xhtml_pagename17}]{#c7_A_First_Latin_Reader_7.xhtml_id-7
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/17"}sē flūmen esse
inventūrum^[^64]^, quō^[^65]^ Americam trānsīre et ita ad Asiam
pervenīre posset. In itineribus et dux et mīlitēs^[^66]^ noctū saepe
frīgora maxima^[^67]^ ferre cōgēbantur; tum^[^68]^, remōtō^[^69]^ ignī
et haud procul collocātō, humī^[^70]^ iacēre solēbant eōdem locō^[^71]^,
ubi ignis modo fuerat. Interdum^[^72]^ aquam dulcem^[^73]^ nōn habēbant,
eōrumque pānis^[^74]^ fluctibus corruptus est^[^75]^.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Ōlim in eōs, cum prope lītus quoddam nāvigārent, ab incolīs sagittae
subitō ex arboribus missae sunt; mīlitēs tamen, cum posteā in lītore
eōsdem Indōs corbulās^[^76]^ manibus^[^77]^ tenentēs vīdissent, incolās
velle frūmentum sibi dare crēdidērunt. Dux autem, īnsidiās veritus,
mīlitēs iussit hostēs prius sonō armōrum terrēre; tum, cum Indī
perterritī in silvās fūgissent, colōni ad lītus vēnērunt, et in harēnā
dōna posuērunt multa. Quae^[^78]^ cum Indī invēnissent, gaudēbant, ac
colōnis iam factī amīcī^[^79]^, frūmentum eīs libenter dedērunt.
:::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}

[]{#c8_A_First_Latin_Reader_8.xhtml}

:::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}
::: {.titulusHeaderBox about="#mwt1"}
:::

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}
:::

::::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
:::::::: text
:::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt33" lang="la"}
[[]{#c8_A_First_Latin_Reader_8.xhtml_pagename17-n192}]{#c8_A_First_Latin_Reader_8.xhtml_id-7-n191
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/17" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

[]{.mw-empty-elt about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
[[LESSON 8]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*Captain John Smith (Continued )*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Dum haec^[^80]^ fīunt^[^81]^, Indī, quī prope colōniam habitābant,
colōnōrum cōpiās saepe rapiēbant^[^82]^; quīn etiam interdum
[[]{#c8_A_First_Latin_Reader_8.xhtml_pagename18}]{#c8_A_First_Latin_Reader_8.xhtml_id-8
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/18"}arma quoque ē
colōniā rapta sunt, dōnec ūnus ex^[^83]^ Indīs, quī ea tractāre^[^84]^
nesciēbat, ita ipse paene sē^[^85]^ interfēcit.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Postrēmō ē Britanniā vēnērunt colōnī novī, quī Fabrō, dē quō suprā dīxī,
amīcī nōn erant. Ā quibus domum^[^86]^ redīre coāctus, numquam posteā
ille ad Virginiam revēnit^[^87]^. Sed per mare Atlanticum saepe
navigāvit, atque ōlim pervēnit usque ad^[^88]^ terram, quae nunc
Britannia Nova appellātur. Ibi nautae, locō^[^89]^ idōneō complūris diēs
morāti, piscēs cēpērunt multōs, quōs sāle condītōs^[^90]^ posteā in
Britanniam reportāvērunt. Interim dux parvā in scaphā multa mīlia
passuum secundum lītus prōgressus, frūmentum pellēsque^[^91]^ ab incolīs
emēbat.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Quī, cum^[^92]^ dēmum in Britanniam redīre vellet^[^93]^, Indōs
complūrīs in nāvēs accēpit^[^94]^ ac sēcum^[^95]^ domum redūxit.
Quō^[^96]^ ubi est perventum^[^97]^ omnēsque^[^98]^ iam ē nāvibus
ēgressī sunt, ūnus ē praepositīs^[^99]^ Indōs paucōs sē sequī nāvemque
iterum cōnscendere iussit; tum clam ad Hispāniam cum captīvīs miserīs
profectus est. Ibi autem cum Indōs vēndere cōnārētur, sacerdōtēs quīdam,
quī dē eius cōnsiliō certiōrēs factī erant^[^100]^, ad nāvem statim
properāvērunt; ā quibus captīvī servātī sunt.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

::: {about="#mwt4"}
:::
::::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}

:::

1.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c8_A_First_Latin_Reader_8.xhtml_cite_ref-1-n193){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [[**haec**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/hic#Latin "wiktionary:hic"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"}: *these things*.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c8_A_First_Latin_Reader_8.xhtml_cite_note-1-n216}
2.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c8_A_First_Latin_Reader_8.xhtml_cite_ref-2-n194){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [[**fīunt**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/fio#Latin "wiktionary:fio"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"}: in connection with **dum**, the pres.
    indic. is rendered as an imperfect.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c8_A_First_Latin_Reader_8.xhtml_cite_note-2-n217}
3.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c8_A_First_Latin_Reader_8.xhtml_cite_ref-3-n195){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [[**rapiēbant**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/rapio#Latin "wiktionary:rapio"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"}: *would steal;* a common meaning of the
    impf. indic.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c8_A_First_Latin_Reader_8.xhtml_cite_note-3-n218}
4.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c8_A_First_Latin_Reader_8.xhtml_cite_ref-4-n198){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [[**ex**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/ex#Latin "wiktionary:ex"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"}: *of.*]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c8_A_First_Latin_Reader_8.xhtml_cite_note-4-n219}

[]{#c9_A_First_Latin_Reader_9.xhtml}

:::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}
::: {.titulusHeaderBox about="#mwt1"}
:::

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}

::::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
:::::::: text
:::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt16" lang="la"}
[[]{#c9_A_First_Latin_Reader_9.xhtml_pagename20}]{#c9_A_First_Latin_Reader_9.xhtml_id-10
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/20" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 9]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*Captain John Smith (Concluded)*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Faber interim colōniam in Britanniam Novam dēdūcere parābat, brevīque
cum mīlitibus ac nautīs sēdecim ad Americam versus^[^101]^ profectus
est. Cum autem mare trānsīret, subitō tempestās magna est coorta, ac
nāvēs fluctibus paene frāctae sunt; quārē domum redīre coāctus est.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Sed paulō post^[^102]^ cum ūnā nāve parvā iterum profectus^[^103]^,
multōs diēs ad Americam versus fēlīciter nāvigāvit. Tum, pīrātīs procul
vīsīs, frūstrā effugere cōnātus est. Pīrātae tamen inventī sunt mīlitēs
esse^[^104]^, quōs ipse ōlim in Eurōpā^[^105]^ dūxerat; quī igitur ducem
suum veterem volēbant sēcum nāvigāre, is autem ad Americam cursum tenēre
māluit. Sed paucīs post diēbus Gallī quīdam, quī per maria omnia praedam
quaerēbant, eius nāvem cēpērunt, ipsumque suam nāvem longam coēgērunt
cōnscendere. Ibi cum morārētur^[^106]^, eius nautae, quī domum redīre
iam diū^[^107]^ volēbant, clam dedērunt vēla^[^108]^,
incolumēsque^[^109]^ in Britanniam pervēnērunt. Ubi^[^110]^ tamen poenās
posteā dedērunt cum dēmum redīsset Faber, quī cum Gallīs diū nāvigāre
coāctus erat. Numquam posteā ille colōniam dēdūcere cōnātus est.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

::: {about="#mwt4"}

[]{#c10_A_First_Latin_Reader_10.xhtml}

:::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}
::: {.titulusHeaderBox about="#mwt1"}
:::

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}
:::

::::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
:::::::: text
:::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt14" lang="la"}
[[]{#c10_A_First_Latin_Reader_10.xhtml_pagename21}]{#c10_A_First_Latin_Reader_10.xhtml_id-11
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/21" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 10]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*Pocahontas*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Prope colōniam, quam Britannī in Virginiam dēdūxerant, habitābat quīdam
rēx Indus, cui erat^[^111]^ fīlia pulchra. Puella, quae Pōcahonta
appellābātur, colōnōs amāvit, ōlimque servāverat eum ducem, dē quō suprā
multa^[^112]^ dīxī; nam trāditum est^[^113]^, cum ille ab Indīs captus
esset, hostēsque eum interficere vellent, rēgis filiam suum^[^114]^
corpus interposuisse. Id^[^115]^ tamen multī^[^116]^ crēdunt numquam
esse factum, Fabrumque posteā mentītum esse. Sed frūmentō certē et carne
Pōcahonta colōnōs saepe iūvit, et quondam ad oppidum nūntium mīsit, cum
hostēs oppidānōs occīdere parārent.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Interdum colōni, quōrum copiae semper parvae erant, fame paene
periērunt; quīn etiam ōlim, quamquam libenter equōs quoque edēbant,
hominēs multī mortuī sunt. Tum, impetum Indōrum timentēs, oppidānī ipsam
rapuērunt Pōcahontam mēnsēsque multōs prō^[^117]^ obside tenuērunt, ut
pater, filiā captā, amīcus esse cōgerētur. Puellam, dum in oppidō
morātur^[^118]^, ūnus ex colōnis amāre coepit. Quī, cum eam in
mātrimōnium dūxisset, ad Britanniam cum uxōre est profectus; ubi paulō
post Pōcahonta mortua est.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

::: {about="#mwt4"}
:::
::::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
:::

1.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c10_A_First_Latin_Reader_10.xhtml_cite_ref-1-n261){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**cui erat**: freely, *who had;* lit. what?]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c10_A_First_Latin_Reader_10.xhtml_cite_note-1-n269}
2.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c10_A_First_Latin_Reader_10.xhtml_cite_ref-2-n262){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [[**multa**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/multus#Latin "wiktionary:multus"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"}: *much;* cf. **multa**, [p. 5, l.
    9]( "A First Latin Reader/5"){.noteref
    xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink"}.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c10_A_First_Latin_Reader_10.xhtml_cite_note-2-n270}
3.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c10_A_First_Latin_Reader_10.xhtml_cite_ref-3-n263){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [[**trāditum
    est**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/trado#Latin "wiktionary:trado"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"}: *it is related* (trādo is short for
    trānsdo, lit. *hand over, pass along*).]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c10_A_First_Latin_Reader_10.xhtml_cite_note-3-n271}
4.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c10_A_First_Latin_Reader_10.xhtml_cite_ref-4-n264){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [[**suum**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/suus#Latin "wiktionary:suus"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"}: emphatic position, *her own*. When a
    possessive adj. is employed for clearness merely, it is apt to
    follow the modified noun; when it precedes the noun, it is often
    best rendered as **suum** here.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c10_A_First_Latin_Reader_10.xhtml_cite_note-4-n272}
5.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c10_A_First_Latin_Reader_10.xhtml_cite_ref-5-n265){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [[**id**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/is#Latin "wiktionary:is"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"}: *i.e.* the
    incident.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c10_A_First_Latin_Reader_10.xhtml_cite_note-5-n273}
6.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c10_A_First_Latin_Reader_10.xhtml_cite_ref-6-n266){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [[**multi**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/multus#Latin "wiktionary:multus"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"}: cf. the note on **quīdam**, [p. 2, l.
    1](#c1_A_First_Latin_Reader_1.xhtml_cite_note-9 "A First Latin Reader/1"){.noteref
    xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink"}.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c10_A_First_Latin_Reader_10.xhtml_cite_note-6-n274}
7.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c10_A_First_Latin_Reader_10.xhtml_cite_ref-7-n267){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [[**prō**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/pro#Latin "wiktionary:pro"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"}: *as*.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c10_A_First_Latin_Reader_10.xhtml_cite_note-7-n275}
8.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c10_A_First_Latin_Reader_10.xhtml_cite_ref-8-n268){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [[**morātur**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/moror#Latin "wiktionary:moror"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"}: for the force of the tense, see the
    note on **fīunt**, [p. 7, l. 16]( "A First Latin Reader/8"){.noteref
    xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink"}.]{.mw-reference-text

[]{#c11_A_First_Latin_Reader_11.xhtml}

:::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}
::: {.titulusHeaderBox about="#mwt1"}
:::

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}
:::

::::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
:::::::: text
:::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt14" lang="la"}
[[]{#c11_A_First_Latin_Reader_11.xhtml_pagename22}]{#c11_A_First_Latin_Reader_11.xhtml_id-12
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/22" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 11]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*Henry Hudson.*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Hōc ferē tempore^[^119]^ Batāvī, quī volēbant viam invenīre, quā circum
Eurōpam ad Asiam nāvigāri posset^[^120]^, parāvērunt nāvem, cui erat
nomen Lūna Dīmidia^[^121]^, et Hudsōnem, virum Britannicum, ducem
fēcērunt.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Ille prīmō circum Eurōpam nāvigāre frūstrā cōnātus, ad Americam deinde
profectus est, quod ibi audīverat esse freta, quibus nāvēs in Asiam
trānsīre possent. Quō^[^122]^ ubi perventum est, multa mīlia passuum
secundum lītus nāvigāvit; cumque loca multa explōrāsset^[^123]^,
postrēmō pervēnit ad īnsulam, ubi nunc est oppidum, quod Eborācum Novum
appellātur. Hīc Indī subitō adortī sunt nautās, quī cum scaphīs portum
explōrābant, sagittīsque hominem interfēcērunt ūnum.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Quō^[^124]^ factō, dux duōs Indōs rapuit nāvemque cōnscendere coēgit.
Tum īnsulā relictā, adversō flūmine^[^125]^ profectus est; cum autem
haud longē nāvigāsset, captīvī ē nāvī sē iēcērunt in aquam, et
nandō^[^126]^ ad rīpam incolumēs pervēnērunt. Interim nāvis lēniter
prōgrediēbātur, moxque in cōnspectū erant montēs, quōrum incolae
frūmentum cōpiāsque aliās nautīs libenter vēndidērunt.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

::: {about="#mwt4"}
:::
::::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}

1.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c11_A_First_Latin_Reader_11.xhtml_cite_ref-1-n279){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**hōc … tempore**: for syntax, cf. **illīs temporibus**, [p. 1, l.
    9]( "A First Latin Reader/1"){.noteref

    rel="mw:WikiLink"}.]{.mw-reference-text

    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"} **posset**: lit. *it could be sailed;*
    cf. the impersonal passive **nāvigātum erat**, [p. 1, l.

[]{#c12_A_First_Latin_Reader_12.xhtml}

:::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}
::: {.titulusHeaderBox about="#mwt1"}
:::

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}
:::

::::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
:::::::: text
:::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt19" lang="la"}
[[]{#c12_A_First_Latin_Reader_12.xhtml_pagename23}]{#c12_A_First_Latin_Reader_12.xhtml_id-13
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/23" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 12]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*Henry Hudson (Continued)*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Cum inde diēs paucōs flūmine adversō nāvigātum esset, dux ipse ē nāvi in
rīpam ēgressus incolās convēnit, quī libenter sagittās suās frēgērunt
omnīs, ut advenae intellegerent sē esse amīcōs. Ibi haud diū^[^127]^
morātus, Hudsō iterum lēniter prōgressus est; sed postrēmō flūmen
invēnit angustius^[^128]^ fierī, ac sēnsit sē hāc^[^129]^ ad Asiam
pervenīre nōn posse. Itaque ad mare rediit, brevīque domum profectus
est.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Paucīs post mēnsibus Batāvi nāvēs aliās et hominēs misērunt, quī cum
Indīs negōtiārentur^[^130]^; ac posterō annō dux īdem, cum ā Britanniā
ad Americam iterum profectus esset^[^131]^, mare^[^132]^ maximum^[^133]^
sub septentriōnibus^[^134]^ invēnit, quod nunc eius nōmine appellātur.
Ibi mēnsēs multōs hiemāre coāctus est. Tum dēmum, cum cibus iam omnis
cōnsūmptus esset, nautae scelerāti, duce in scaphā relictō, in
altum^[^135]^ vēla dedērunt.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Hudsōnem nēmō posteā vīdit; sed nautae, paucīs āmissīs^[^136]^,
incolumēs domum pervēnērunt:— quamquam primō fame omnēs paene perierant;
paucīs enim avibus exceptīs^[^137]^, nōn habēbant quod ēssent^[^138]^,
dōnec in cōnspectum vēnit nāvis, cuius magister eōs frūmentō aliīsque
rēbus iuvāre potuit.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

::: {about="#mwt4"}
:::
::::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
:::

1.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c12_A_First_Latin_Reader_12.xhtml_cite_ref-1-n297){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**haud diū**: freely, *but a short time*. ]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c12_A_First_Latin_Reader_12.xhtml_cite_note-1-n309}
2.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c12_A_First_Latin_Reader_12.xhtml_cite_ref-2-n298){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [[**angustius**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/angustior#Latin "wiktionary:angustior"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"}: predicate adj., agreeing with
    **flūmen**, l. 5.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c12_A_First_Latin_Reader_12.xhtml_cite_note-2-n310}
3.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c12_A_First_Latin_Reader_12.xhtml_cite_ref-3-n299){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [[**hāc**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/hic#Latin "wiktionary:hic"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"}: sc. **viā**; cf. the note on **quā**,
    [p. 5, l. 13]( "A First Latin Reader/5"){.noteref
    xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink"}.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c12_A_First_Latin_Reader_12.xhtml_cite_note-3-n311}
4.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c12_A_First_Latin_Reader_12.xhtml_cite_ref-4-n300){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [[**negōtiārentur**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/negotior#Latin "wiktionary:negotior"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"}: cf. the note on **possent**, [p. 1, l.
    13]( "A First Latin Reader/1"){.noteref
    xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink"}.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c12_A_First_Latin_Reader_12.xhtml_cite_note-4-n312}
5.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c12_A_First_Latin_Reader_12.xhtml_cite_ref-5-n301){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**cum … profectus esset**: cf. [p. 12, l.
    9](#c11_A_First_Latin_Reader_11.xhtml "A First Latin Reader/11"){.noteref
    xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops" rel="mw:WikiLink"}, [and
    the note]( "A First Latin Reader/11"){.noteref
    xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink"}.]{.mw-reference-text

6.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c12_A_First_Latin_Reader_12.xhtml_cite_ref-6-n302){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [[**mare**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/mare#Latin "wiktionary:mare"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"}: *bay*. ]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c12_A_First_Latin_Reader_12.xhtml_cite_note-6-n314}
7.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c12_A_First_Latin_Reader_12.xhtml_cite_ref-7-n303){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [[**maximum**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/maximus#Latin "wiktionary:maximus"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"}: *mighty;* absolute use of the
    superlative. In a similar way, comparatives may indicate a high
    degree in general, without distinctly comparing one thing with
    another.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c12_A_First_Latin_Reader_12.xhtml_cite_note-7-n315}
8.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c12_A_First_Latin_Reader_12.xhtml_cite_ref-8-n304){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**sub septentriōnibus**: i.e. toward the north
    ([**septentriōnēs**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/septentrio#Latin "wiktionary:septentrio"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"}, -um, [m.]{.smallcaps}, the “Great
    Bear”).]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c12_A_First_Latin_Reader_12.xhtml_cite_note-8-n316}
9.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c12_A_First_Latin_Reader_12.xhtml_cite_ref-9-n305){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [[**altum**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/altum#Latin "wiktionary:altum"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"}: *the deep (sea)*.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c12_A_First_Latin_Reader_12.xhtml_cite_note-9-n317}
10. [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c12_A_First_Latin_Reader_12.xhtml_cite_ref-10-n306){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [[**āmissīs**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/amitto#Latin "wiktionary:amitto"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"}: *i.e.* by death.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c12_A_First_Latin_Reader_12.xhtml_cite_note-10-n318}
11. [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c12_A_First_Latin_Reader_12.xhtml_cite_ref-11-n307){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**paucīs...exceptīs**: freely, *with the exception of a
    few*.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c12_A_First_Latin_Reader_12.xhtml_cite_note-11-n319}
12. [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c12_A_First_Latin_Reader_12.xhtml_cite_ref-12-n308){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**quod ēssent**: *(anything) to eat* (**ēssent** from
    [**edō**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/edo#Latin "wiktionary:edo"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"}). As antecedent for the relative,
    supply **id** (acc.).]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c12_A_First_Latin_Reader_12.xhtml_cite_note-12-n320}

::::::::::::

[]{#c13_A_First_Latin_Reader_13.xhtml}

::::::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}
::: {.titulusHeaderBox about="#mwt1"}
:::

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}
:::

:::::::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
::::::::::: text
::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt22" lang="la"}
[[]{#c13_A_First_Latin_Reader_13.xhtml_pagename24}]{#c13_A_First_Latin_Reader_13.xhtml_id-14
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/24" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 13.]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*Colonization in New England*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Paucīs post annīs Britannī complūrēs, quī apud Batāvōs diū habitāverant,
in Americam cum līberīs atque uxōribus^[^139]^ ēmigrāre cōnstituērunt.
Quī, cum^[^140]^ pervēnissent ad lītus eius terrae, quae nunc Britannia
Nova appellātur, impetum Indōrum veritī, lēgātum, nōmine Standisium, cum
mīlitibus paucīs mīsērunt, quī loca undique explōrāret^[^141]^. Illī
igitur multa mīlia passuum secundum lītus prōgressī sunt, cum
nāvigārent^[^142]^ interdiū, noctēsque autem in lītore agerent.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Prīmō terrae incolās rārō^[^143]^ vīdērunt; ōlim tamen, cum māne
proficīscī parārent ūnusque ex mīlitibus omnium^[^144]^ arma in scaphā
iam collocāvisset, Indī subitō ē silvā magnō clāmōre ērūpērunt,
sagittīsque vulnerāvērunt paucōs. Sed mīlitēs statim ad scapham
cucurrērunt, ut arma caperent^[^145]^, hostēsque celeriter fugere coāctī
sunt.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Postrēmō ad portum tūtum perventum est, ubi tribus ante annīs multī
habitāverant Indī; quī iam ad ūnum^[^146]^ morbō perierant. Quā dē
rē^[^147]^ certiōrēs factī, colōnī reliquī quoque ad eum locum vēnērunt,
ibique ē nāvī in lītus ēgressī, dīs^[^148]^ ēgērunt grātiās castraque
posuērunt. Est in lītore etiam nunc saxum, quod Americānī semper
coluērunt^[^149]^ colentque
[[]{#c13_A_First_Latin_Reader_13.xhtml_pagename26}]{#c13_A_First_Latin_Reader_13.xhtml_id-16
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/26"}semper, quod^[^150]^
hic demum ē nāvī ēgressi sunt Brītannī illī, quī posteā maiōrēs
peregrinantēs^[^151]^ appellātī sunt.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

\
:::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
:::

::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt27" lang="la"}
[[]{#c13_A_First_Latin_Reader_13.xhtml_pagename25}]{#c13_A_First_Latin_Reader_13.xhtml_id-15
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/25" about="#mwt24"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

[ ]{about="#mwt25" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

[ ]{about="#mwt25"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt25"}
[Iūnō, Rēgina Deōrum]{.smallcaps}
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt25"}

The chief deities worshiped by the Romans were twelve in number: namely,
Jupiter, Neptune, Vulcan, Mars, Mercury, Apollo, Juno, Minerva, Vesta,
Ceres, Venus, and Diana. Besides these, many minor divinities were
recognized.

[ ]{about="#mwt25"}

::: {about="#mwt25"}

:::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
::::::: text
::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt25" lang="la"}
[[]{#c14_A_First_Latin_Reader_14.xhtml_pagename26-n354}]{#c14_A_First_Latin_Reader_14.xhtml_id-16-n353
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/26" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 14]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*A Soldier’s Courtship*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Hieme proximā morbō aut fame colōni complūrēs periērunt, quōrum in
numerō^[^152]^ erat Standisī^[^153]^ quoque uxor. Ille, uxōre mortuā, in
mātrimōnium volēbat dūcere quandam puellam pulchram, cui erat nōmen
Prissilla; sed, cum^[^154]^ sē sentīret mīlitem asperum esse, rem ipse
tractāre nōluit, iuvenemque quendam mīsit, quī puellae patrem
convenīret.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Iuvenis, quī forte ipse quoque Prissillam amāre coeperat, amīcō tamen
deesse nōlēbat. Quārē maestus^[^155]^ profectus est, lēniterque per
lītus ad puellae domum^[^156]^ versus ambulāvit. Quō^[^157]^ cum
pervēnisset rēsque^[^158]^ esset prōposita, pater statim sē nōn
nōlle^[^159]^ dīxit. Cum autem iuvenis cum Prissillā^[^160]^ ipsā dē
virtūte lēgatī eiusque^[^161]^ rēbus gestīs^[^162]^ loquerētur, illa diū
tacitā audīvit, tum rīdēns: “Nōnne^[^163]^ prō tē,” inquit, “dictūrus
es?^[^164]^” Quā vōce ille vehementer commōtus domum ad lēgātum rediit.
Quī prīmō amīcum verbīs acerbīs
[[]{#c14_A_First_Latin_Reader_14.xhtml_pagename27}]{#c14_A_First_Latin_Reader_14.xhtml_id-17
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/27"}accēpit, postrēmō
tamen sēnsit nōn illīus culpā^[^165]^ rem^[^166]^ ita cecidisse. Itaque
paucīs post mēnsibus ā iuvene Prissilla in mātrimōnium ducta est,
Standisius autem sibi uxorem aliam sūmpsit.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}
:::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
:::

    nouns in **-ium**. Accent, **Standísī**.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c14_A_First_Latin_Reader_14.xhtml_cite_note-2-n373}

[]{#c15_A_First_Latin_Reader_15.xhtml}

::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}
::: {.titulusHeaderBox about="#mwt1"}

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}

:::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
::::::: text
::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt22" lang="la"}
[[]{#c15_A_First_Latin_Reader_15.xhtml_pagename27-n388}]{#c15_A_First_Latin_Reader_15.xhtml_id-17-n387
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/27" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 15]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*Unrest among the Indians*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Indī, quī prope colōniam habitābant, paene omnēs inimīcī erant, sed
vehementer timēbant lēgātum Standisium, dē quō suprā dīxī; nam is, dux
fortissimus, libentissimē bellum semper gessit, neque umquam^[^167]^
perīculum ūllum recūsāvit. Quī tamen nōn erat crūdēlis; ōlim enim, cum
ad oppidum Indōrum inimīcōrum profectus esset hostēsque vīcisset, trēs
Indōs vulnerātōs domum sēcum redūxit, ut eōrum vulnera ibi cūrārentur.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Hōc ferē tempore colōni aliī, ā Britanniā profectī, haud procul
condidērunt oppidum alterum. Tum dēmum Indī vehementer commōtī,
conciliō^[^168]^ convocātō, oppida ambō incendere colōnōsque ipsōs
interficere cōnstituērunt; sed rēx,quīdam, quī colōnōs amābat, ad
Standisium properāvit, eumque dē hostium cōnsiliō certiōrem fēcit.
Perīculō cōgnitō^[^169]^, lēgātus statim cum mīlitibus paucīs ad alterum
oppidum profectus est. Ibi Indī, cum vīdissent mīlitēs esse paucōs,
arbitrātī^[^170]^ sē facile Standisium terrēre posse, eī ostendērunt
[[]{#c15_A_First_Latin_Reader_15.xhtml_pagename28}]{#c15_A_First_Latin_Reader_15.xhtml_id-18
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/28"}sīcās, ac verbōrum
quoque contumēliās^[^171]^ adiūnxērunt^[^172]^. Sed paucīs post diēbus,
cum quīdam^[^173]^ Pecsuot cum lēgātō loquerētur, is^[^174]^, sīgnō
mīlitibus datō, Pecsuotis sīcam subitō rapuit, eāque^[^175]^
ipsum^[^176]^ interfēcit; simul mīlitēs, comitēs Pecsuotis adortī, eōs
omnes occīdērunt. Quō^[^177]^ factō, Indī reliquī perterritī fūgērunt,
nec diūtius^[^178]^ dē caede^[^179]^ colōnōrum cōgitābant ūllī.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}
:::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
:::

1.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c15_A_First_Latin_Reader_15.xhtml_cite_ref-1-n389){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**neque umquam**: and … never; cf. the rendering of **nec
    quisquam**, [p. 2, l. 11]( "A First Latin Reader/2"){.noteref
    xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops" rel="mw:WikiLink"}. In
    translation, **nec (neque)** should always, if possible, be resolved
    thus into connective and negative.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c15_A_First_Latin_Reader_15.xhtml_cite_note-1-n404}
2.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c15_A_First_Latin_Reader_15.xhtml_cite_ref-2-n390){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [[**conciliō**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/concilium#Latin "wiktionary:concilium"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"}: contrast
    [**cōnsiliō**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/consilium#Latin "wiktionary:consilium"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"}, l. 18.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c15_A_First_Latin_Reader_15.xhtml_cite_note-2-n405}
3.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c15_A_First_Latin_Reader_15.xhtml_cite_ref-3-n391){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [[**perīculō**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/periculum#Latin "wiktionary:periculum"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"}
    [**cōgnitō**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/cognosco#Latin "wiktionary:cognosco"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"}: freely, *having learned of the
    danger*. A literal rendering of **cōgnitus** in the abl. absol.
    construction would often be awkward.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c15_A_First_Latin_Reader_15.xhtml_cite_note-3-n406}
4.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c15_A_First_Latin_Reader_15.xhtml_cite_ref-4-n392){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [[**arbitrātī**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/arbitror#Latin "wiktionary:arbitror"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"}: cf. the use of
    [**veritī**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/vereor#Latin "wiktionary:vereor"){.extiw

    xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"

5.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c15_A_First_Latin_Reader_15.xhtml_cite_ref-5-n395){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}

8.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c15_A_First_Latin_Reader_15.xhtml_cite_ref-8-n398){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**is**: *i.e.* Standish. ]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c15_A_First_Latin_Reader_15.xhtml_cite_note-8-n411}
9.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c15_A_First_Latin_Reader_15.xhtml_cite_ref-9-n399){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [[**eā**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/is#Latin "wiktionary:is"){.extiw

    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"}: note the case.]{.mw-reference-text

10. [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c15_A_First_Latin_Reader_15.xhtml_cite_ref-10-n400){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [[**ipsum**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/ipse#Latin "wiktionary:ipse"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"}: *him*. The intensive pronoun points a
    contrast between Pecsuot and his companions
    ([**comitēs**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/comes#Latin "wiktionary:comes"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}

::::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
:::::::: text
:::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt21" lang="la"}
[[]{#c16_A_First_Latin_Reader_16.xhtml_pagename28-n418}]{#c16_A_First_Latin_Reader_16.xhtml_id-18-n417
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/28" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 16]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*Old Friends become Enemies*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Eī rēgī, ā quō colōnī dē suō perīculō cōnsilitīsque Indōrum certiōrēs
factī sunt, duo erant fīliī, quī quoque colōnīs diū amīcī erant. Patre
autem mortuō^[^180]^, iuvenēs suspicārī coepērunt bene ēmisse^[^181]^
colōnōs, quibus silvās Indī vēndiderant; tum^[^182]^ novam religiōnem
civēs suōs^[^183]^ amplectī haud libenter vīdērunt: itaque mox dē bellō
cōgitābant^[^184]^.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Quod^[^185]^ ubi cōgnitum est, ē colōniā mīlitēs missī sunt, quī frātrem
maiōrem, nōmine Alexandrum, prō obside in oppidum sēcum redūcerent. Ille
autem ibi morbō affectus est gravī^[^186]^; cumque posteā domum
redīsset, apud suōs^[^187]^ brevī mortuus est. Quō factō, Alexandrum
venēnō periisse arbitrātī, Indī sīcās secūrēsque suās acuere^[^188]^
statim coepērunt.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

::: {about="#mwt4"}
:::

[[]{#c16_A_First_Latin_Reader_16.xhtml_pagename30}]{#c16_A_First_Latin_Reader_16.xhtml_id-20
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/30"}Tum dēmum oppidānī
alterum frātrem, quī Philippus appellābātur, ad colōniam dēdūxērunt,
eumque coēgērunt arma omnia trādere, quae ipse comitēsque ferēbant; nec
vērō dīmīsērunt hominem^[^189]^, dōnec pollicitus est sē reliqua quoque
arma trāditūrum^[^190]^, quae domī^[^191]^ Indī habēbant.

[ ]{about="#mwt15"}

::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}
::: {.titulusHeaderBox about="#mwt1"}

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}

:::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
::::::: text
::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt22" lang="la"}
[[]{#c17_A_First_Latin_Reader_17.xhtml_pagename30-n446}]{#c17_A_First_Latin_Reader_17.xhtml_id-20-n445
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/30" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 17]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*The Outbreak of King Philip’s War*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Philippus, quī patre et frātre mortuīs iam ipse rēx erat, irātus domum
profectus, Indōs ad arma vocāvit. Quī eum libenter secūtī sunt; quīn
etiam ōlim quendam cīvem suum^[^192]^ interfēcērunt, quod rēgis cōnsilia
colōnīs prōdiderat.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Complūra iam erant colōnōrum oppida; sed Indī prīmō tantum vīllīs
admōvērunt ignīs bovēsque rapuērunt: nam, ā sacerdōtibus monitī,
hominem^[^193]^ occīdere nūllum ausī sunt, dōnec ā colōnīs ūnus ex
ipsōrum^[^194]^ numerō vulnerātus est. Tum dēmum, omnibus oppidīs
oppugnātīs, caedēs maxima est facta, ac colōnī miserī, aliī^[^195]^
cum^[^196]^ aquam peterent, aliī cum ā vīllīs in oppida fugerent,
undique occīsī sunt.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Ōlim hostēs, cum^[^197]^ in^[^198]^ castellum quoddam impetum fēcissent
sagittāsque ārdentēs mīsissent in tēctum, postrēmō ipsī^[^199]^ quoque
castellō ignem admovēre cōnātī sunt. Quā rē^[^200]^ animadversā, colōnī,
quī sē fortiter multās hōrās
[[]{#c17_A_First_Latin_Reader_17.xhtml_pagename31}]{#c17_A_First_Latin_Reader_17.xhtml_id-21
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/31"}dēfenderant, omnem
salūtis spem iam dēpōnēbant^[^201]^; sed subitō imber^[^202]^ coortus
est maximus, quo ignēs sunt extīnctī. Quārē Indī cōnātū
dēsistere^[^203]^ coāctī sunt.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}
:::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
:::

1.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c17_A_First_Latin_Reader_17.xhtml_cite_ref-1-n447){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [[**suum**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/suus#Latin "wiktionary:suus"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"}: *of theirs*.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c17_A_First_Latin_Reader_17.xhtml_cite_note-1-n461}
2.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c17_A_First_Latin_Reader_17.xhtml_cite_ref-2-n448){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [[**hominem**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/homo#Latin "wiktionary:homo"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"}: standing in contrast to **villīs** and
    **bovēs** of the preceding clause.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c17_A_First_Latin_Reader_17.xhtml_cite_note-2-n462}
3.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c17_A_First_Latin_Reader_17.xhtml_cite_ref-3-n449){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**ipsōrum**: *their own*.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c17_A_First_Latin_Reader_17.xhtml_cite_note-3-n463}
4.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c17_A_First_Latin_Reader_17.xhtml_cite_ref-4-n450){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**aliī … aliī**: *some … others*. ]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c17_A_First_Latin_Reader_17.xhtml_cite_note-4-n464}
5.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c17_A_First_Latin_Reader_17.xhtml_cite_ref-5-n451){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [[**cum**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/cum#Latin "wiktionary:cum"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"}: *as*.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c17_A_First_Latin_Reader_17.xhtml_cite_note-5-n465}
6.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c17_A_First_Latin_Reader_17.xhtml_cite_ref-6-n452){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [[**hostēs**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/hostis#Latin "wiktionary:hostis"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"}, **cum**: *when the enemy*. Note the
    changed order of the English. ]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c17_A_First_Latin_Reader_17.xhtml_cite_note-6-n466}
7.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c17_A_First_Latin_Reader_17.xhtml_cite_ref-7-n453){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [[**in**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/in#Latin "wiktionary:in"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"}: **upon**.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c17_A_First_Latin_Reader_17.xhtml_cite_note-7-n467}
8.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c17_A_First_Latin_Reader_17.xhtml_cite_ref-8-n454){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**ipsī**: modifying
    [**castellō**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/castellum#Latin "wiktionary:castellum"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"}. ]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c17_A_First_Latin_Reader_17.xhtml_cite_note-8-n468}
9.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c17_A_First_Latin_Reader_17.xhtml_cite_ref-9-n455){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**quā rē**: *this*.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c17_A_First_Latin_Reader_17.xhtml_cite_note-9-n469}

:::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
::::::: text
::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt17" lang="la"}
[[]{#c18_A_First_Latin_Reader_18.xhtml_pagename31-n474}]{#c18_A_First_Latin_Reader_18.xhtml_id-21-n473
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/31" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 18]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*A Remarkable Deliverance*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Hōc ferē tempore aliō in oppidō latēbat imperātor quīdam, quī ē
Britanniā paulō ante fūgerat, quod rēx Britannōrum eum volēbat
interficere. Homō^[^204]^ scīlicet nōlēbat oppidānōs cōgnōscere sē ibi
latēre. Sed ōlim, cum colōnī in templō adessent omnēs, tūtō sē ē
latebrīs exīre posse crēdēbat; itaque ē fenestrā prōspēxit. Prīmō
nēminem vīdit; tum subitō animadvertit multōs Indōs per agrōs clam
properantēs, ut oppidum oppugnārent.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Quibus ille rēbus^[^205]^ vehementer commōtus, ex aedibus statim ērūpit
ac colōnōs ad arma vocāvit. Quī cum^[^206]^ celeriter ē templō
cucurrissent, advenā duce^[^207]^ cum Indīs fortiter pugnāvērunt,
hostēsque postrēmō in silvās fugere coāctī sunt.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Imperātor interim, postquam Indōs fugere intellēxit, ad latebrās statim
sē recēpit, nec posteā ā colōnīs invenīrī^[^208]^ potuit^[^209]^.
Quī^[^210]^ igitur crēdidērunt ducem^[^211]^ ē caelō ā dīs missum esse,
quī sē adiuvāret, sīcut multīs ante annīs Castor et Pollūx ōlim subitō
adfuērunt in aciē auxiliumque Rōmānīs
[[]{#c18_A_First_Latin_Reader_18.xhtml_pagename32}]{#c18_A_First_Latin_Reader_18.xhtml_id-22
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/32"}tulērunt, cum illī
hōrās multās pugnāssent cum hostibus, neque eōs in fugam dare
potuissent.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}
:::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
:::

1.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c18_A_First_Latin_Reader_18.xhtml_cite_ref-1-n475){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [[**homō**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/homo#Latin "wiktionary:homo"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"}: cf. *hominem*, [p. 20, l.
    4](#c16_A_First_Latin_Reader_16.xhtml_cite_note-10 "A First Latin Reader/16"){.noteref
    xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink"}.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c18_A_First_Latin_Reader_18.xhtml_cite_note-1-n485}

    [**quībus … rébus**: transl. as singular (cf. **quā rē**, \[\[A
    First Latin Reader/17#cite_note-9\|p. 20, l.
    19).]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c18_A_First_Latin_Reader_18.xhtml_cite_note-2-n486}

4.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c18_A_First_Latin_Reader_18.xhtml_cite_ref-4-n478){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}

6.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c18_A_First_Latin_Reader_18.xhtml_cite_ref-6-n480){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}

    **possent**, [p. 1, l. 13]( "A First Latin Reader/1"){.noteref

::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}

:::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
::::::: text
::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt24" lang="la"}
[[]{#c19_A_First_Latin_Reader_19.xhtml_pagename32-n494}]{#c19_A_First_Latin_Reader_19.xhtml_id-22-n493
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/32" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 19]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*Philip finds Allies*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Dum^[^212]^ haec geruntur, Indī quīdam longinquī, quibus erat castellum
maximum, armīs aliīsque rēbus Philippum iuvāre coepērunt. Quō^[^213]^
cōgnitō^[^214]^, colōnī, quamquam iam hiems erat, id castellum statim
oppugnāre cōnstituērunt; nam putābant hanc quoque gentem prīmā^[^215]^
aestāte bellum gerere parāre, cōnsiliaque hostium ipsī^[^216]^
praeoccupāre volēbant.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Itaque viā^[^217]^ nivālī^[^218]^ cum exercitū validō profectī, per
silvās ad castellum iter fēcērunt. Ibi ācerrimē est pugnātum^[^219]^, ac
colōni multī interfectī sunt; castellum tamen expugnātum est, Indōrumque
cōpiae omnēs ignī sunt cōnsūmptae: quibus rēbus factīs, colōnī
vulnerātōs^[^220]^ sēcum ferentēs^[^221]^ domum lēniter sē recēpērunt.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Hōc dētrīmentō vehementer commōtī, Indī iam undique convēnērunt,
oppidaque colōnōrum oppugnāre coepērunt singula^[^222]^. Subitō
veniēbant^[^223]^ in cōnspectum; tum, colōnīs occīsīs vīllīsque
incēnsīs, celeriter in silvās sē recipiēbant, cum^[^224]^ interim
mīlitēs, quī arma graviōra ferēbant, nūllō modō cōnsequī^[^225]^
poterant. Itaque diū colōnī miserī undique
[[]{#c19_A_First_Latin_Reader_19.xhtml_pagename33}]{#c19_A_First_Latin_Reader_19.xhtml_id-23
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/33"}interfectī sunt;
Standisius enim iam prīdem mortuus erat: sed postrēmō dux alius inventus
est, quī fēlīciter cum Indīs bellum gerere^[^226]^ sciēbat.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}
:::::

[]{#c20_A_First_Latin_Reader_20.xhtml}

::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}

:::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
::::::: text
::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt28" lang="la"}
[[]{#c20_A_First_Latin_Reader_20.xhtml_pagename33-n528}]{#c20_A_First_Latin_Reader_20.xhtml_id-23-n527
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/33" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 20]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*Captain Church*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Cercās^[^227]^, quī iam dux colōnōrum factus est, nōn modo^[^228]^ cum
hostibus fēliciter bellum gerere sciēbat, sed etiam^[^229]^ Indōs
interdum sociōs^[^230]^ sibi ascīscere potuit. Quō cōnsiliō^[^231]^ ōlim
profectus, ad quandam gentem pervēnit haud longinquam, cuius
rēgīnae^[^232]^ diū fuerat ipse^[^233]^ amīcus; quārē spērābat
eius^[^234]^ cīvibus facile sē persuādēre^[^235]^ posse^[^236]^, ut
colōnōs adiuvārent. Ibi tamen ab Indīs impetus ācerrimus in Cercam
eiusque comitēs facta est; quī igitur in palūde coāctī sunt latēre,
dōnec in scaphā vēnērunt mīlitēs complūrēs, quī eōs ex perīculō
ēriperent.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Cercās, quamquam^[^237]^ cōnsilium tum perficere nōn potuerat,
convenīre^[^238]^ tamen rēginam iterum cōnārī cōnstituit. Itaque paucīs
post mēnsibus ūnō cum mīlite Indīsque tribus profectus, in eiusdem
gentis fīnēs dēnuō^[^239]^ iter fēcit; quō^[^240]^ ubi est perventum,
comitibus in scaphā relictīs, ad rēgīnam ipse prōgressus est.
Cum^[^241]^ eā dum loquitur, Indī multī, quī per^[^242]^
[[]{#c20_A_First_Latin_Reader_20.xhtml_pagename34}]{#c20_A_First_Latin_Reader_20.xhtml_id-24
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/34"}herbam latuerant,
subitō armātī exsiluērunt. Quī tamen, cum^[^243]^ intellēxissent Cercam
minimē esse territum, humī^[^244]^ tum^[^245]^ sēdērunt conciliōque
habitō pollicitī sunt sē colōnōs adiūtūrōs in bellō, quod illī cum
Philippō gerēbant.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}
:::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}

::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt24" lang="la"}
[[]{#c21_A_First_Latin_Reader_21.xhtml_pagename34-n570}]{#c21_A_First_Latin_Reader_21.xhtml_id-24-n569
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/34" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 21]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*The Death of Philip*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Cercās cum hīs sociīs suīsque^[^246]^ mīlitibus iam omnēs in partīs iter
fēcit per silvās, et undique hostēs in fugam dedit. Quārē postrēmō
Philippus ipse paucīs cum comitibus per vallīs multa mīlia passuum in
palūdēs longinquās fugere coāctus est; numquam enim colōnīs sē dēdere
cōnstituerat: quīn etiam ōlim, cum quīdam^[^247]^ ex eius amīcīs dīcere
ausus esset pācem cum eīs faciendam esse, rēx īrātus hominem^[^248]^
suā^[^249]^ manū occīdit. Cuius reī^[^250]^ acerbitāte^[^251]^ commōtus,
frāter mortuī^[^252]^ statim ad colōnōs perfūgit eōsque certiōrēs fēcit
de palūde, ubi Philippus tum latēbat.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Itaque dux colōnōrum, quī multōs diēs frūstrā quaesīverat rēgem
modoque^[^253]^ domum redierat ut uxōrem cōnsōlārētur, iterum celeriter
profectus est, mīlitēsque suōs prope illam palūdem sine morā īnstrūxit.
Quā rē^[^254]^ animadversā, Philippus eiusque comitēs per vallēs longius
fugere cōnātī sunt; rēx vērō^[^255]^ īnfēlix^[^256]^, interceptus ā
mīlitibus quī in silvā collocātī
[[]{#c21_A_First_Latin_Reader_21.xhtml_pagename35}]{#c21_A_First_Latin_Reader_21.xhtml_id-25
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/35"}erant, ā frātre
eiusdem Indī interfectus est, quem ipse occīderat. Caput Philippī secūrī
abscīsum^[^257]^ colōnī sēcum domum tulērunt; ubi suprā^[^258]^ portam
positum est, ut omnēs vidērent rēgem rē vērā^[^259]^ mortuum esse.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}
:::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}

    the note.]{.mw-reference-text

    *ill-starred*.]{.mw-reference-text

12. [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c21_A_First_Latin_Reader_21.xhtml_cite_ref-12-n584){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}

    [**rē vērā**: *in very fact* (**verus, -a, -um,** lit. *true,* or
    *actual*).]{.mw-reference-text

[]{#c22_A_First_Latin_Reader_22.xhtml}

::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}
::: {.titulusHeaderBox about="#mwt1"}
:::

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}
:::

:::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
::::::: text
::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt28" lang="la"}
[[]{#c22_A_First_Latin_Reader_22.xhtml_pagename35-n602}]{#c22_A_First_Latin_Reader_22.xhtml_id-25-n601
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/35" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 22]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*End of the War*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Quō dētrīmentō perterritus lēgātus^[^260]^ Philippī, quī paucīs cum
comitibus ē palūde effūgerat, in silvīs procul latēbat. Quem^[^261]^
Cercās diū frūstra quaesīvit; sed postrēmō Indum senem^[^262]^ cēpit et
puellam, quōs viam ostendere coēgit: quō modō in lēgātī castra subitō
perventum est.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Ibi Cercās, quamquam comitēs perpaucōs^[^263]^ sēcum habēbat, arma
Indōrum, quae humī collocāta erant, audācter rapuit. Quō factō, lēgātus
magnā^[^264]^ vōce: “Captus sum,” inquit. Cercās vērō^[^265]^: “Ubi est
cēna? nam vēnī ut vobīscum cēnārem.” Tum lēgātus: “Equīnam^[^266]^
carnem māvīs^[^267]^,” inquit, “an^[^268]^ būbulam^[^269]^?” Quō auditō,
Cercās scīlicet dīxit se mālle būbulam.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Carne sine morā cōnsūmptā, reliquī (noctū enim impetus factus erat) mox
humī iacēbant sōpītī; sed Cercās et lēgātus diū vigilābant. Postrēmō
Indus^[^270]^ surrēxit et silentiō^[^271]^
[[]{#c22_A_First_Latin_Reader_22.xhtml_pagename36}]{#c22_A_First_Latin_Reader_22.xhtml_id-26
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/36"}ēgressus est; quārē
alter^[^272]^ crēdēbat eum exīsse ut arma alia sūmeret. Brevī autem
aderat^[^273]^ lēgātus manibus^[^274]^ ferēns insīgnia^[^275]^ quae
quondam Philippus gesserat^[^276]^. “Haec nunc tua^[^277]^ sunt,”
inquit, īnsīgniaque ante Cercae pedēs humī posuit. Ita bellum cōnfectum
est.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

:::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
::::::: text
::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt31" lang="la"}
[[]{#c23_A_First_Latin_Reader_23.xhtml_pagename36-n642}]{#c23_A_First_Latin_Reader_23.xhtml_id-26-n641
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/36" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 23]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*William Penn and the Friends*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Dum haec^[^278]^ in Britanniā Novā geruntur, in aliās Americae partēs ex
Eurōpā veniēbant^[^279]^ colōnī multī; in^[^280]^ quibus erant
complūrēs, quī sē Amīcōs appellābant. Cuidam virō clārō, quī hanc
religiōnem erat amplexus, rēx Britannōrum tum magnam^[^281]^ pecūniam
dēbēbat^[^282]^; quod^[^283]^ aes aliēnum ut^[^284]^ solveret, in
Americā prōvinciam novam hōc ferē tempore cōnstituit^[^285]^, virumque
illum lēgātum^[^286]^ fēcit; quae prōvincia ē^[^287]^ nōmine lēgātī
Pennsylvēnia appellāta est.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Lēgātus, quod religiō Amicōrum gentibus Eurōpae grāta^[^288]^ nōn erat,
colōnōs plūrimōs statim ad Pennsylvēniam praemīsit, paucīsque post
mēnsibus in prōvinciam ipse profectus est; ubi^[^289]^ urbem condidit,
quae Philadelphia appellātur. Propter religiōnem Amīcī crēdunt bellum
gerere nefās^[^290]^ esse, atque omnibus cum hominibus cōmiter vīvere
volunt; itaque

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

[[]{#c23_A_First_Latin_Reader_23.xhtml_pagename37}]{#c23_A_First_Latin_Reader_23.xhtml_id-27
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/37"}per^[^291]^ multōs
annōs continuōs^[^292]^ in prōvinciā erat pāx, etiam cum^[^293]^ lēgātus
ille mortuus esset.

[ ]{about="#mwt19"}

Dē cōmitāte lēgāti multa^[^294]^ nārrantur; quīn etiam trāditum
est^[^295]^ illum, cum ōlim per prōvinciam iter faceret, parvam puellam
vīdisse ad templum euntem^[^296]^, eamque^[^297]^ in ipsīus^[^298]^ equō
positam^[^299]^ ad templum ita dēdūxisse.

[ ]{about="#mwt19"}

\
:::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}

20. [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c23_A_First_Latin_Reader_23.xhtml_cite_ref-20-n664){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [[**eam**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/is#Latin "wiktionary:is"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"}: *her*.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c23_A_First_Latin_Reader_23.xhtml_cite_note-20-n686}
21. [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c23_A_First_Latin_Reader_23.xhtml_cite_ref-21-n665){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [[**ipsius**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/ipse#Latin "wiktionary:ipse"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"}: *his own*.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c23_A_First_Latin_Reader_23.xhtml_cite_note-21-n687}
22. [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c23_A_First_Latin_Reader_23.xhtml_cite_ref-22){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [[**positam**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/pono#Latin "wiktionary:pono"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"}: part. (from **pōnō**), agreeing with
    **eam**.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c23_A_First_Latin_Reader_23.xhtml_cite_note-22}

[]{#c24_A_First_Latin_Reader_24.xhtml}

::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}
::: {.titulusHeaderBox about="#mwt1"}
:::

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}
:::

:::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
::::::: text
::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt25" lang="la"}
[[]{#c24_A_First_Latin_Reader_24.xhtml_pagename37-n690}]{#c24_A_First_Latin_Reader_24.xhtml_id-27-n689
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/37" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 24]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*Nathaniel Bacon in Virginia*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Dum in Britanniā Novā bellum gerit Philippus, in Virginiā quoque Indī
impetūs saepe in colōnōs faciēbant, multōsque agricolās, quī procul ab
oppidīs habitābant, cum cruciātū occīdērunt. Quō perīculō commōtī,
colōnī multa mīlia passuum nūntiōs ad caput^[^300]^ prōvinciae mīsērunt,
quī lēgātum ōrārent, ut mitteret mīlitēs, quī hostīs coercērent. Lēgātō
autem nūllō modō persuādērī potuit^[^301]^ ut colōnōs adiuvāret, quod
cum Indīs ipse negōtiābātur nec quaestum dīmittere volēbat^[^302]^; quīn
etiam iuvenis quīdam, nōmine Bēcō, quī ā Britanniā tribus ante annīs in
prōvinciam vēnerat, cum^[^303]^ dīxisset sē velle in Indōrum fīnīs
dūcere colōnōs paucōs, quī iam ipsī^[^304]^ arma cēperant, ā lēgātō domī
est iussus manēre.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Iuvenis autem, sine morā ad castra colōnōrum clam
[[]{#c24_A_First_Latin_Reader_24.xhtml_pagename38}]{#c24_A_First_Latin_Reader_24.xhtml_id-28
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/38"}fectus, cum
prīmum^[^305]^ in cōrum cönspectum vēnit summō assēnsū omnium^[^306]^
dux factus est. Quī^[^307]^ igitur, quamquam sciēbat lēgātum posteā
īrātum^[^308]^ sē fortasse^[^309]^ interfectūrum^[^310]^, in fīnīs tamen
Indōrum cōpiās^[^311]^ dūxit, hostēsque in fugam undique dedit.
Quod^[^312]^ ubi est audītum, lēgātus ex oppidō celeriter profectus est,
ut Bēcōnem caperet suppliciumque^[^313]^ dē^[^314]^ eō sūmeret, quod
iniussū suō bellum cum Indīs gereret.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

\
:::::

[]{#c25_A_First_Latin_Reader_25.xhtml}

::::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}
::: {.titulusHeaderBox about="#mwt1"}
:::

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}

:::::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
::::::::: text
::::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt26" lang="la"}
[[]{#c25_A_First_Latin_Reader_25.xhtml_pagename38-n724}]{#c25_A_First_Latin_Reader_25.xhtml_id-28-n723
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/38" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 25]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*Nathaniel Bacon (Continued)*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Brevī autem ad caput prōvinciae lēgātus celeriter redīre est coāctus;
nūntiātum enim est oppidānōs, quōs domī relīquerat quīque iuvenī^[^315]^
ducī amīcissimī erant, rēs novās^[^316]^ ibi agitāre^[^317]^.
Quibuscum^[^318]^ lēgātus tum pācem fēcit; postquam vērō Bēcō dēmum ē
bellō longinquō domum rediit, colōnī, lēgātum adhūc esse īrātum
arbitrātī^[^319]^, noctēs diēsque^[^320]^ ducis cārī aedēs custōdiēbant;
eumque, cum paulō post decuriō^[^321]^ factus esset, multī comitēs
armātī ad oppidum secūti sunt. Ibi tamen lēgātus, quī quoque cōpiās
coēgerat^[^322]^, Bēcōnem statim rapuit, mox autem ab oppidānīs īrātīs
dīmittere coāctus est. Sed iuvenis, paucīs post diēbus certior factus
[[]{#c25_A_First_Latin_Reader_25.xhtml_pagename39}]{#c25_A_First_Latin_Reader_25.xhtml_id-29
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/39"}

[ ]{about="#mwt15" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

<figure class="mw-halign-center" typeof="mw:File" about="#mwt15">
<a href="https://la.wikisource.org/wiki/Fasciculus:Ballista_Romana.jpg"
class="mw-file-description"><img
src="images/c137_jpg_500px_Ballista_Romana.jpg_utm_source_la.wikisource.org_utm_campaign_parser_utm_content_thumbnail"
class="mw-file-element" style="width:350px; height:223px; "
resource="./Fasciculus:Ballista_Romana.jpg" decoding="async"
data-file-type="bitmap"
data-title="Ballista_Romana.jpg-500px-Ballista_Romana.jpg?utm_source=la.wikisource.org&amp;utm_campaign=parser&amp;utm_content=thumbnail" /></a>
</figure>

[ ]{about="#mwt15"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt15"}
[Ballista]{.smallcaps}
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt15"}

Ancient “artillery” was not very formidable, as may be seen from the
above illustration, which gives a modern artist’s conception of an
attack upon a walled town. Roman “cannon” were simply huge catapults,
some of which threw stones or masses of metal, others projected heavy
darts.

[ ]{about="#mwt15"}

::: {about="#mwt15"}
:::

[[]{#c25_A_First_Latin_Reader_25.xhtml_pagename40}]{#c25_A_First_Latin_Reader_25.xhtml_id-30
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/40"}lēgātum parāre sē
iterum in custōdiam dare, clam noctū fūgit ex oppidō, nec posterō diē ab
inimīcīs suīs invenīrī^[^323]^ potuit.

[ ]{about="#mwt17"}

Colōnī scīlicet undique libenter convēnērunt, ut ducem cārum adiuvārent;
isque iam mēnsēs multōs, modo^[^324]^ cum Indīs modo cum lēgātō,
fēlīciter bellum gessit. Ōlim, cum obsidēret urbem, quod^[^325]^ erat
caput prōvinciae, ballistāsque circum mūrōs collocāre vellet, uxōrēs
inimīcōrum ē praediīs proximīs dēductās ante mīlitēs suōs posuisse
dīcitur^[^326]^, ut sine perīculō suōrum^[^327]^ opus perficerētur.

[ ]{about="#mwt17"}
:::::::

    note.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c25_A_First_Latin_Reader_25.xhtml_cite_note-12-n753}
13. [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c25_A_First_Latin_Reader_25.xhtml_cite_ref-13-n741){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [[**suōrum**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/suus#Latin "wiktionary:suus"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"}: *to* (lit. *of*) *his
    men.*]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c25_A_First_Latin_Reader_25.xhtml_cite_note-13-n754}

[]{#c26_A_First_Latin_Reader_26.xhtml}

:::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}
::: {.titulusHeaderBox about="#mwt1"}

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}
