::::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
:::::::: text
:::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt18" lang="la"}
[[]{#c26_A_First_Latin_Reader_26.xhtml_pagename40-n756}]{#c26_A_First_Latin_Reader_26.xhtml_id-30-n755
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/40" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 26]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*Nathaniel Bacon (Concluded)*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Lēgātus^[^328]^, cum eā in urbe multōs diēs obsessus esset, postrēmō cum
comitibus omnibus nāvis cōnscendit, quae in flūmine propinquō ad ancoram
cōnsistēbant, ac sine morā profectus est, ut auxilium peteret. Quō
factō, Bēcō, quī sentiēbat lēgātum mox cum sociīs esse reditūrum, urbem
statim incendit; ipse autem, labōribus perīculīsque frāctus, paulō post
mortuus est.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Tum eius comitēs, cum intellegerent^[^329]^ lēgātum solēre^[^330]^
inimīcōs etiam mortuōs^[^331]^ contumēliīs afficere, corpus ducis cāri
tulērunt ad flūmen et in aquam mersērunt^[^332]^; quārē lēgātus, cum
redīsset ad urbem amīcōsque Bēcōnis multōs^[^333]^ interfēcisset, ipsīus
iuvenis corpus invenīre nōn potuit.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

::: {about="#mwt4"}
:::

[[]{#c26_A_First_Latin_Reader_26.xhtml_pagename41}]{#c26_A_First_Latin_Reader_26.xhtml_id-31
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/41"}Paucīs post annīs
ille lēgātus pessimus quoque poenās dedit; nam ā rēge domum revocātus,
summā ignōminiā affectus ibi mortuus est. Interim Virginia reliquaeque
prōvinciae paulātim validiōrēs fīēbant^[^334]^. Sed antequam dē bellō
loquor, quod posteā ā colōnīs cum Britannīs gestum est, quaedam^[^335]^
dicenda sunt de puerō, quī imperātor summus Americanōrum futūrus
erat^[^336]^.

[ ]{about="#mwt12"}
::::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}

::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}

:::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
::::::: text
::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt23" lang="la"}
[[]{#c27_A_First_Latin_Reader_27.xhtml_pagename41-n778}]{#c27_A_First_Latin_Reader_27.xhtml_id-31-n777
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/41" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 27]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*The Boyhood of George Washington*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Hīc puer, quī Vasingtō appellābātur, in Virginiā nātus est^[^337]^
sexāgintā ferē annīs post^[^338]^ bellum, quod cum lēgātō eius
prōvinciae gesserat Bēcō ille, dē quō modo dīxī. Puerō erat frāter
maior, quī tribūnus mīlitum factus ad bellum abierat, quod Britannī cum
Hispānīs tum gerēbant eīs in īnsulīs, ad quās Columbus prīmum nāvēs
appulit.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Vasingtō, postquam frāter ad exercitum profectus est, dē bellō saepe
cōgitābat; cumque lūdēbant puerī ac simulābant sē esse mīlitēs, semper
erat ille imperātor^[^339]^. Posteā vērō^[^340]^, puer magnus et^[^341]^
validus factus^[^342]^, celerrimē dicitur^[^343]^ currere potuisse neque
equum timuisse ūllum.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Frāter iam volēbat Vasingtōnem nautam fierī, māter autem nōluit; itaque
ille domī aliquamdiū mānsit et didicit omnia^[^344]^, quae ibi in
lūdō^[^345]^ trādēbantur^[^346]^. Sed paucīs post
[[]{#c27_A_First_Latin_Reader_27.xhtml_pagename42}]{#c27_A_First_Latin_Reader_27.xhtml_id-32
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/42"}annīs vir quīdam,
cuī erat maximum praedium longinquum, hōminem condūcere voluit, quī
terminōs^[^347]^ praediī suī cōnstitueret; ac Vasingtō, quī hanc quōque
artem^[^348]^ didicerat, ab eō conductus in praedium missus est.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

\
:::::

::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}

:::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}

::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt23" lang="la"}
[[]{#c28_A_First_Latin_Reader_28.xhtml_pagename42-n806}]{#c28_A_First_Latin_Reader_28.xhtml_id-32-n805
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/42" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 28]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*Experiences on the Frontier*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

In praediō, quod īnstar prōvinciae erat, habitābant agricolae paucī, at
multī Indī. Hīc^[^349]^ Vasingtō mēnsēs multōs per silvās et montēs
longē iter fēcit, ac saepe equō vectus rīvōs et flūmina trānsiit; noctū
autem^[^350]^ solēbat sub caelō prope ignem humī^[^351]^ iacēre, quod
casās colōnōrum nōn amābat^[^352]^. Ōlim cum ita sōpitus iacēret, subitō
ignis in foenum^[^353]^ cecidit, ex quō^[^354]^ lectus eius factus erat;
quō ex perīculō^[^355]^ ipse tamen servātus est ab agricolā quōdam, quī
tum vigilābat.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Trēs annōs in praediō morātus est Vasingtō, ibique mōrēs Indōrum
cōgnōscere coepit; quārē, ubi domum ūndēvīgintī annōs nātus^[^356]^
rediit, ā lēgātō Virginiae tribūnus mīlitum^[^357]^ factus est: nam
Virginiā tōtā^[^358]^ reliquīsque prōvinciīs colōni arbitrābantur bellum
cum Gallīs mox gerendum esse. Britannī enim multī iam trānsierant montēs
cōnsederantque in vallibus, quae a Gallīs prius explōrātae erant; quibus
rēbus
[[]{#c28_A_First_Latin_Reader_28.xhtml_pagename43}]{#c28_A_First_Latin_Reader_28.xhtml_id-33
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/43"}Gallī commōti, cum
hanc regiōnem dīmittere nōllent^[^359]^, castella complūra ibi
pōnēbant^[^360]^, quae Britannōs arcērent^[^361]^.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}
:::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
:::

    [[**hīc**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/hic#Latin "wiktionary:hic"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"}: the adverb.]{.mw-reference-text

    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"}: *moreover*.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c28_A_First_Latin_Reader_28.xhtml_cite_note-2-n823}

    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"}: cf. p. 7, l. 4.]{.mw-reference-text

    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"}: *fancy;* for other meanings of this
    word, see the Vocab.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c28_A_First_Latin_Reader_28.xhtml_cite_note-4-n825}
5.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c28_A_First_Latin_Reader_28.xhtml_cite_ref-5-n811){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}

    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"}: **foenum, -i,** [n.]{.smallcaps},
    *straw*.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c28_A_First_Latin_Reader_28.xhtml_cite_note-5-n826}
6.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c28_A_First_Latin_Reader_28.xhtml_cite_ref-6-n812){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**ex quō**: *(out) of which*.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c28_A_First_Latin_Reader_28.xhtml_cite_note-6-n827}
7.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c28_A_First_Latin_Reader_28.xhtml_cite_ref-7-n813){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**quō ex periculō**: for word order, cf. **eā in terrā**, p. 6, l.
    3.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c28_A_First_Latin_Reader_28.xhtml_cite_note-7-n828}
8.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c28_A_First_Latin_Reader_28.xhtml_cite_ref-8-n814){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**ūndēvīgintī annōs nātus**: *at nineteen years of age,* lit.
    *having been born nineteen years*.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c28_A_First_Latin_Reader_28.xhtml_cite_note-8-n829}
9.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c28_A_First_Latin_Reader_28.xhtml_cite_ref-9-n815){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**tribūnus mīlitum**: *a major*.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c28_A_First_Latin_Reader_28.xhtml_cite_note-9-n830}
10. [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c28_A_First_Latin_Reader_28.xhtml_cite_ref-10-n816){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**Virginiā tōtā**: *throughout all Virginia*. The prep. in is often
    omitted when the abl. is modified by **tōtus**.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c28_A_First_Latin_Reader_28.xhtml_cite_note-10-n831}
11. [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c28_A_First_Latin_Reader_28.xhtml_cite_ref-11-n819){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**cum … nōllent**: translate by a participial
    phrase.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c28_A_First_Latin_Reader_28.xhtml_cite_note-11-n832}
12. [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c28_A_First_Latin_Reader_28.xhtml_cite_ref-12-n820){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [[**ponēbant**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/pono#Latin "wiktionary:pono"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"}: note the tense.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c28_A_First_Latin_Reader_28.xhtml_cite_note-12-n833}
13. [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c28_A_First_Latin_Reader_28.xhtml_cite_ref-13-n821){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [[**arcērent**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/arceo#Latin "wiktionary:arceo"){.extiw

[]{#c29_A_First_Latin_Reader_29.xhtml}

::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}
::: {.titulusHeaderBox about="#mwt1"}
:::

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}
:::

:::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
::::::: text
::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt23" lang="la"}
[[]{#c29_A_First_Latin_Reader_29.xhtml_pagename43-n836}]{#c29_A_First_Latin_Reader_29.xhtml_id-33-n835
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/43" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 29]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*A Dangerous Mission*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Quamquam spēs pācis iam paene sublāta erat, lēgātus Virginiae cōnstituit
tamen nūntium mittere, sī^[^362]^ ūllō modō rēs sine bellō
compōnī^[^363]^ possent. Itaque Vasingtō, sine morā dēlēctus quī hanc
rem difficilem tractāret^[^364]^, paucīs cum comitibus per silvās
fortiter profectus est; cumque montēs quoque trānsīsset, Indīs^[^365]^
quibusdam ad concilium vocātis^[^366]^ persuāsit ut ad Gallōrum castra
sē sequerentur.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Quō ubi perventum est, Gallī nūntium cōmiter accēpērunt, respondērunt
tamen sē numquam nisi^[^367]^ bellō coāctōs ex illīs fīnibus
discessūrōs. Quārē Vasingtō, qui Gallōrum cōpias^[^368]^ maximās summā
sollicitūdine^[^369]^ animadverterat, domum statim properāre coepit; cum
vērō^[^370]^ ad montēs perventum esset, impedīmentīs relictīs, ūnō cum
comite et duce^[^371]^ Indō etiam celerius prōgressus est.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Via scīlicet erat ipsa perīculōsa (nam hiems iam erat): alterum^[^372]^
autem fuit perīculum maius; colōnīs^[^373]^ enim inimīcus erat dux. Quī
ōlim, cum advesperāsceret, tēlum subitō
[[]{#c29_A_First_Latin_Reader_29.xhtml_pagename44}]{#c29_A_First_Latin_Reader_29.xhtml_id-34
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/44"}in^[^374]^
Vasingtōnem mīsit. Quō factō, colōnus alter Indum interficere volēbat.
At Vasingtō, quī tēlō vulnerātus nōn erat, hominem discēdere incolumem
passus est; iam autem nōn sōlum interdiū sed noctū quoque iter faciendum
arbitrābātur, quod perīculum sentiēbat maximum esse.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}
:::::

[]{#c30_A_First_Latin_Reader_30.xhtml}

::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}
::: {.titulusHeaderBox about="#mwt1"}
:::

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}
:::

:::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
::::::: text
::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt21" lang="la"}
[[]{#c30_A_First_Latin_Reader_30.xhtml_pagename44-n866}]{#c30_A_First_Latin_Reader_30.xhtml_id-34-n865
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/44" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 30]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*A Dangerous Mission (Continued)*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Paulō post ad flūmen magnum perventum est; quod cum rate^[^375]^
trānsīrent, Vasingtō forte in aquam frīgidam cecīdit, ūnāque cum comite
in īnsulā parvā morārī coāctus est, dōnec diēs postera illūxit: tum
dēmum per glaciem, quae in^[^376]^ flūmine natābat, summō cum perīculō
ad rīpam alteram ambō vēnērunt. Deinde, equō ab^[^377]^ Indīs emptō,
facilius^[^378]^ fēcērunt iter, et postrēmō incolumēs domum pervēnērunt.
Ubi^[^379]^ lēgātus, cum dē pertināciā Gallōrum certior factus esset,
molestē ferēns illōs tam audācter respondisse^[^380]^, Vasingtōnem
iussit mīlitēs trāns montēs dūcere ad castella eīsdem in locīs
pōnenda^[^381]^, ē quī^[^382]^ ipse modo redierat.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Interim colōnī aliī, ē prōvinciā clam per montēs profectī, in illīs
regiōnibus longinquīs locum quendam, castrīs maximē idōneum, audācter
occupāvērunt. Quī vērō brevī ā Gallīs sē dēdere coāctī sunt; nam
Vasingtō, quamquam iam cōgēbat cōpiās atque intellegēbat omnia
sibi^[^383]^ esse facienda
[[]{#c30_A_First_Latin_Reader_30.xhtml_pagename45}]{#c30_A_First_Latin_Reader_30.xhtml_id-35
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/45"}ut hīc locus
dēfenderētur, cīvibus tamen suīs^[^384]^ satis mātūrē auxilium ferre nōn
potuit.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}
:::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
:::

    *raft;* for syntax, cf. **navibus**, p. 6, l.
    10.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c30_A_First_Latin_Reader_30.xhtml_cite_note-1-n879}
2.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c30_A_First_Latin_Reader_30.xhtml_cite_ref-2-n868){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}

    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"}: *upon the surface of.*
    [[——]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}\

    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"}, p. 3, l. 15.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c30_A_First_Latin_Reader_30.xhtml_cite_note-2-n880}
3.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c30_A_First_Latin_Reader_30.xhtml_cite_ref-3-n869){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [[**ab**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/ab#Latin "wiktionary:ab"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"}: *from.*]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c30_A_First_Latin_Reader_30.xhtml_cite_note-3-n881}
4.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c30_A_First_Latin_Reader_30.xhtml_cite_ref-4-n870){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}

    14.]{.mw-reference-text

    [**illōs … respondisse**: *that they had
    replied.*]{.mw-reference-text

    [**ad castella … pōnenda**: *to establish

    [[**sibi**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/sibi#Latin "wiktionary:sibi"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"}: dat. case, this being the regular

    [**suīs**: modifier of civibus]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c30_A_First_Latin_Reader_30.xhtml_cite_note-10-n888}

:::::::::::

[]{#c31_A_First_Latin_Reader_31.xhtml}

::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}
::: {.titulusHeaderBox about="#mwt1"}
:::

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}
:::

:::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
::::::: text
::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt17" lang="la"}
[[]{#c31_A_First_Latin_Reader_31.xhtml_pagename45-n890}]{#c31_A_First_Latin_Reader_31.xhtml_id-35-n889
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/45" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 31]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*The Beginning of the French and Indian War*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

At paucīs post diēbus, per loca aspera summō labōre prōgressus, in
hostium finēs pervēnit Vasingtō, castraque ibi parva posuit. Deinde
paulō longius profectus explorātōrēs cēpit paucōs; tum autem certior
factus Gallōs Indōsque adesse plūrimōs, iterum sē in castra recēpit. Quō
factō Gallī, cum sociīs Indīs^[^385]^ celeriter cōnsecūtī, in castra
impetum fēcērunt ācerrimum; sed postrēmō, colōnīs multās hōrās frūstrā
oppugnātīs, ē castrīs Vasingtōnem cum armīs eā condiciōne^[^386]^ exīre
passī sunt, ut exercitum ex hīs fīnibus statim redūceret. Ille igitur
invītus^[^387]^ domum iter facere coāctus est.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Posterō autem annō ē Britanniā legiōnēs complūrēs missae sunt ad Gallōs
expellendōs^[^388]^ ex eīs locīs, unde illī modo Vasingtōnem discēdere
coēgerant. Imperātor factus erat vir Britannicus, nōmine Braddoc, dux
fortis, quī tamen cum Indīs bellum gerere^[^389]^ nesciēbat. Crēdēbat
vērō sē omnia scīre, neque ā Vasingtōne aut reliquīs colōnīs sē monērī
volēbat; quārē, cum ad bellum profectus esset, quamquam multa mīlia
passuum per viās perīculōsās silvāsque maximās iter legiōnibus^[^390]^
erat faciendum, explōrātōrēs praemittere
[[]{#c31_A_First_Latin_Reader_31.xhtml_pagename46}]{#c31_A_First_Latin_Reader_31.xhtml_id-36
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/46"}nōluit, nec grātiās
colōnis ēgit, quī operam suam ultrō pollicitī sunt: nam nē cōnspectum
quidem legiōnum suārum putābat Indōs esse lātūrōs.
:::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
:::

1.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c31_A_First_Latin_Reader_31.xhtml_cite_ref-1-n891){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**Indīs**: here as adj.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c31_A_First_Latin_Reader_31.xhtml_cite_note-1-n899}
2.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c31_A_First_Latin_Reader_31.xhtml_cite_ref-2-n892){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**eā condiciōne** … ut: *on those terms, that*.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c31_A_First_Latin_Reader_31.xhtml_cite_note-2-n900}
3.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c31_A_First_Latin_Reader_31.xhtml_cite_ref-3-n893){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**invītus**: cf. the note on **laetus**, p. 2 l.
    16]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c31_A_First_Latin_Reader_31.xhtml_cite_note-3-n901}
4.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c31_A_First_Latin_Reader_31.xhtml_cite_ref-4-n894){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**ad Gallōs expellendōs**: purpose clause; cf. the similar phrase
    on p. 34 l. 15]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c31_A_First_Latin_Reader_31.xhtml_cite_note-4-n902}
5.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c31_A_First_Latin_Reader_31.xhtml_cite_ref-5-n895){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**gerere**: cf. the infinitive with **nesciēbat**, p.8 l. 2
    [[——]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
    **sē**: omit in translation.
    [[——]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
    **omnia**: *all (about the subject)*.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c31_A_First_Latin_Reader_31.xhtml_cite_note-5-n903}
6.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c31_A_First_Latin_Reader_31.xhtml_cite_ref-6-n896){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**legiōnibus**: for syntax, cf. **sibi**, p. 34, l.
    21.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c31_A_First_Latin_Reader_31.xhtml_cite_note-6-n904}
:::::::

[]{#c32_A_First_Latin_Reader_32.xhtml}

::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}
::: {.titulusHeaderBox about="#mwt1"}
:::

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}
:::

:::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
::::::: text
::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt22" lang="la"}
[[]{#c32_A_First_Latin_Reader_32.xhtml_pagename46-n906}]{#c32_A_First_Latin_Reader_32.xhtml_id-36-n905
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/46" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 32]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*Braddock’s Defeat*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Postrēmō vērō, cum in fīnēs hostium longē iter factum esset, subitō in
silvīs Indōrum ululātus est audītus; tum tēla plūrima inmissa sunt, ac
mīlitēs Britannicī, quī hostem nūllum vidēbant,^[^391]^ undique cadere
coepērunt. Colōnī interim in silvam celeriter inrūpērunt, arboribusque
interpositīs^[^392]^ cum Indīs ācriter pugnābant; at imperātor legiōnēs
in viā habēbat^[^393]^ instrūctās, nec suōs locō cēdere passus est,
quamquam caedem maximam fierī sentiēbat. Itaque illī paene omnēs aut
interfectī sunt aut^[^394]^ vulnerātī, ac Braddoc ipse vulnus accēpit,
ex quō paulō post mortuus est. Vasingtō mīlitēs perterritōs primō
cohortārī cōnātus, imperātōre vulnerātō^[^395]^ exercitūs reliquiās ad
castra redūxit, ubi impedimenta maxima relicta erant. Ibi, conciliō
convocātō, tribūnī centuriōnēsque celeriter ē fīnibus hostium sibi
discēdendum esse^[^396]^ statuērunt.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Quō proeliō admoneor ut^[^397]^ dīcam dē incommodō maximō, quod ā
Romanīs acceptum est apud lacum Trasumennum,^[^398]^
[[]{#c32_A_First_Latin_Reader_32.xhtml_pagename47}]{#c32_A_First_Latin_Reader_32.xhtml_id-37
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/47"}cum Hannibal, dux
Poenōrum, ibi īnsidiās clam fēcisset. Secundum lītus est via angusta,
tum agrī apertī. In locō apertō^[^399]^ Hannibal castra posuit, mīlitēs
autem multōs in latebrīs prope viam collocāvit. Tum, cum Rōmānī temerē
viā angustā^[^400]^ ad Hannibalis castra versus iter facerent, subitō
Poenī ē latebrīs ērūpērunt et hostīs perterritōs in lacum compulērunt.
:::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
:::

1.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c32_A_First_Latin_Reader_32.xhtml_cite_ref-1-n907){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**vidēbant**: we would say “*could* see”.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c32_A_First_Latin_Reader_32.xhtml_cite_note-1-n919}
2.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c32_A_First_Latin_Reader_32.xhtml_cite_ref-2-n908){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**arboribusque interpositīs**: freely, *getting behind trees*; lit.
    what?]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c32_A_First_Latin_Reader_32.xhtml_cite_note-2-n920}
3.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c32_A_First_Latin_Reader_32.xhtml_cite_ref-3-n909){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**habēbat**: *kept*
    [[——]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
    **suōs**: cf. **suōrum**, page 30. l. 9
    [[——]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
    locō: *from their places*; cf. the note on p. 7, l.
    4]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c32_A_First_Latin_Reader_32.xhtml_cite_note-3-n921}
4.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c32_A_First_Latin_Reader_32.xhtml_cite_ref-4-n910){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**aut … aut**: *either … or*.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c32_A_First_Latin_Reader_32.xhtml_cite_note-4-n922}
5.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c32_A_First_Latin_Reader_32.xhtml_cite_ref-5-n911){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**imperātōre vulnerātō**: translate by a phrase introduced by
    “after”.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c32_A_First_Latin_Reader_32.xhtml_cite_note-5-n923}
6.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c32_A_First_Latin_Reader_32.xhtml_cite_ref-6-n912){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**discēdendum esse**: impersonal use of the
    gerundive.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c32_A_First_Latin_Reader_32.xhtml_cite_note-6-n924}
7.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c32_A_First_Latin_Reader_32.xhtml_cite_ref-7-n913){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**ut**: *to*.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c32_A_First_Latin_Reader_32.xhtml_cite_note-7-n925}
8.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c32_A_First_Latin_Reader_32.xhtml_cite_ref-8-n914){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**apud**: *at*.
    [[——]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
    **lacum Trasumennum**: in north central Italy.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c32_A_First_Latin_Reader_32.xhtml_cite_note-8-n926}
9.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c32_A_First_Latin_Reader_32.xhtml_cite_ref-9-n917){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**in locō apertō**: freely, *in the open*; lit.
    what?]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c32_A_First_Latin_Reader_32.xhtml_cite_note-9-n927}
10. [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c32_A_First_Latin_Reader_32.xhtml_cite_ref-10-n918){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**viā angustā**: for syntax, cf. the note on **quā** p. 5 l. 13;
    here the abl. may be rendered “along’]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c32_A_First_Latin_Reader_32.xhtml_cite_note-10-n928}

::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt18" lang="la"}
[[]{#c33_A_First_Latin_Reader_33.xhtml_pagename47-n930}]{#c33_A_First_Latin_Reader_33.xhtml_id-37-n929
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/47" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 33]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*Later Events of the War*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Etsī in proeliō, dē quō suprā dīxī, Gallī victōriam erant adeptī^[^401]^
Britannīque ex illīs regiōnibus celerrimē sē recēperant, Vasingtōnis
tamen virtūtem omnēs laudābant. Quem^[^402]^ igitur colōnī, cōpiīs tōtā
ex prōvinciā coāctīs, summum fēcērunt ducem et in montēs cum exercitū ad
hostīs arcendōs misērunt; ubi bellum cum Gallīs eōrumque sociīs mēnsēs
multōs fēlīciter gessit: tribusque post annīs, cum iam imperātōrēs
complūrēs ē Britanniā ad Americam missī essent, ūnā cum legātīs aliīs
legiōnēs quāsdam ille ē Pennsylvēniā trāns montēs dūxit atque hostēs ex
eīs locīs discēdere coēgit, ubi illī quondam Britannīs^[^403]^ tantum
dētrīmentum intulerant.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Quō incommodō acceptō, Gallī tamen minimē animō dēmissī^[^404]^ bellum
alibī ācriter gessērunt; nam Indī, quī erant paene omnēs amīcī, eos
omnibus modīs adiuvābant. Sed
[[]{#c33_A_First_Latin_Reader_33.xhtml_pagename48}]{#c33_A_First_Latin_Reader_33.xhtml_id-38
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/48"}postrēmō, multīs
dētrimentīs frāctī, pācem petiērunt;^[^405]^ quam mox adeptī
sunt,^[^406]^ Canadā aliīsque regiōnibus Britannīs^[^407]^ trāditīs.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Vasingtō interim ab exercitū domum redierat, ubi in mātrimōnium dūxit
mātrōnam quandam, quae Marta appellabātur; tum annōs paucōs in praediō
suō mānsit ōtiōsus.^[^408]^
:::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
:::

1.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c33_A_First_Latin_Reader_33.xhtml_cite_ref-1-n931){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**erant adeptī**: **adipīscor**, 3. **adeptus sum**, *gain*, or
    *secure*.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c33_A_First_Latin_Reader_33.xhtml_cite_note-1-n941}
2.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c33_A_First_Latin_Reader_33.xhtml_cite_ref-2-n932){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**quem**: not relative in the Engish
    translation.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c33_A_First_Latin_Reader_33.xhtml_cite_note-2-n942}
3.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c33_A_First_Latin_Reader_33.xhtml_cite_ref-3-n933){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**Britannīs**: dat. case; translate “upon”.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c33_A_First_Latin_Reader_33.xhtml_cite_note-3-n943}
4.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c33_A_First_Latin_Reader_33.xhtml_cite_ref-4-n934){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**animō dēmissī**: lit. *cast down in mind*, i.e. *discouraged*.
    The ablative case here expresses specification.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c33_A_First_Latin_Reader_33.xhtml_cite_note-4-n944}
5.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c33_A_First_Latin_Reader_33.xhtml_cite_ref-5-n937){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**petiērunt**: *i.e.* **petivērunt**.
    [[——]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
    quam: *this* (noun).]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c33_A_First_Latin_Reader_33.xhtml_cite_note-5-n945}
6.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c33_A_First_Latin_Reader_33.xhtml_cite_ref-6-n938){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**adeptī sunt**: c.f. the note on p37 l. 8]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c33_A_First_Latin_Reader_33.xhtml_cite_note-6-n946}
7.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c33_A_First_Latin_Reader_33.xhtml_cite_ref-7-n939){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**Britannīs**: dat. case]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c33_A_First_Latin_Reader_33.xhtml_cite_note-7-n947}
8.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c33_A_First_Latin_Reader_33.xhtml_cite_ref-8-n940){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**ōtiōsus**: translate by another part of
    speech.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c33_A_First_Latin_Reader_33.xhtml_cite_note-8-n948}
:::::::
::::::::
:::::::::::

[]{#c34_A_First_Latin_Reader_34.xhtml}

::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}
::: {.titulusHeaderBox about="#mwt1"}
:::

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}
:::

:::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
::::::: text
::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt27" lang="la"}
[[]{#c34_A_First_Latin_Reader_34.xhtml_pagename48-n950}]{#c34_A_First_Latin_Reader_34.xhtml_id-38-n949
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/48" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 34]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*The Outbreak of the Revolution*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Nunc mihi dīcendum est dē bellō, quod colōnī paucīs post annīs cum
Britannīs ipsīs gessērunt. Diū rēx senātusque Britannōrum ā prōvinciīs
vectīgālia^[^409]^ quaedam exigere erant cōnātī, etsī hae lēgēs^[^410]^
lātae erant in conciliō, in quō suffrāgium ferre^[^411]^ Americānō nūllī
licēbat. Id^[^412]^ colōnī molestē ferēbant; ac postrēmō, cum iam tanta
iniūria nōn diūtius ferenda^[^413]^ vidērētur, omnibus ex prōvinciīs in
unum locum^[^414]^ virī dēlēctī, in eīs Vasingtō, ad cōnsilium commūne
capiendum convocātī sunt. Hī, conciliō habitō, litterās^[^415]^ ad rēgem
Britannōrum mīsērunt, quibus^[^416]^ postulābant ut colōnīs iūra eadem
concēderentur, quae domī cīvēs reliquī obtinēbant.^[^417]^ Quibus
litterīs acceptīs, rēx īrātus nōn sōlum iūra concēdere
[[]{#c34_A_First_Latin_Reader_34.xhtml_pagename49}]{#c34_A_First_Latin_Reader_34.xhtml_id-39
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/49"}nōluit, sed etiam in
Americam mīsit mīlitēs multōs, quī ā colōnīs audāciae^[^418]^ poenās
repeterent.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Apud^[^419]^ oppidum parvum, nōmine Lexingtōnem, prīmum^[^420]^ pugnātum
est, magnā cum caede Britannōrum; nam agricolae, murīs interpositīs,
tēla plūrima inmīsērunt in hostēs, quī ita^[^421]^ sex milia passuum sē
recipere coāctī sunt ad urbem, unde paulō ante profectī erant. Quibus
rēbus factīs, concilium^[^422]^ idem, quod ad rēgem litterās mīserat,
quaerere coepit imperātōrem, quī omnīs copiās Americānās dūceret. Cīvēs
scīlicet memoriā tenēbant^[^423]^ rēs gestās Vasingtōnis in bellō, quod
paucīs ante annīs cum Gallīs Indīsque gestum erat; quārē ille summō
assēnsū omnium dux brevī factus est.
:::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
:::

1.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c34_A_First_Latin_Reader_34.xhtml_cite_ref-1-n951){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**vectīgālia**: **vectīgālia, -ium**, [n.]{.smallcaps},
    *taxes*.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c34_A_First_Latin_Reader_34.xhtml_cite_note-1-n968}
2.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c34_A_First_Latin_Reader_34.xhtml_cite_ref-2-n952){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**lēgēs**: lēx, lēgis, [f.]{.smallcaps}, *measure*, or
    *law*.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c34_A_First_Latin_Reader_34.xhtml_cite_note-2-n969}
3.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c34_A_First_Latin_Reader_34.xhtml_cite_ref-3-n953){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**suffrāgium ferre**: *cast a vote* (**suffrāgium, -ī,
    [n]{.smallcaps}.).**]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c34_A_First_Latin_Reader_34.xhtml_cite_note-3-n970}
4.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c34_A_First_Latin_Reader_34.xhtml_cite_ref-4-n954){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**id**: *this (state of affairs)*.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c34_A_First_Latin_Reader_34.xhtml_cite_note-4-n971}
5.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c34_A_First_Latin_Reader_34.xhtml_cite_ref-5-n955){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**ferenda**: *bearable*: lit. what?]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c34_A_First_Latin_Reader_34.xhtml_cite_note-5-n972}
6.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c34_A_First_Latin_Reader_34.xhtml_cite_ref-6-n956){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**in unum locum**: with **convocātī sunt**.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c34_A_First_Latin_Reader_34.xhtml_cite_note-6-n973}
7.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c34_A_First_Latin_Reader_34.xhtml_cite_ref-7-n957){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**litterās**: for the force of the plural, see the
    Vocab.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c34_A_First_Latin_Reader_34.xhtml_cite_note-7-n974}
8.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c34_A_First_Latin_Reader_34.xhtml_cite_ref-8-n958){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**quibus**: *in which*; strictly, abl of means.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c34_A_First_Latin_Reader_34.xhtml_cite_note-8-n975}
9.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c34_A_First_Latin_Reader_34.xhtml_cite_ref-9-n959){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**obtinēbant**: freely, *enjoyed*]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c34_A_First_Latin_Reader_34.xhtml_cite_note-9-n976}
10. [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c34_A_First_Latin_Reader_34.xhtml_cite_ref-10-n962){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [[**audāciae**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/audacia#Latin "wiktionary:audacia"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"}: *for* (lit. *of*) *their
    insubordination*.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c34_A_First_Latin_Reader_34.xhtml_cite_note-10-n977}
11. [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c34_A_First_Latin_Reader_34.xhtml_cite_ref-11-n963){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [[**apud**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/apud#Latin "wiktionary:apud"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"}: *near*.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c34_A_First_Latin_Reader_34.xhtml_cite_note-11-n978}
12. [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c34_A_First_Latin_Reader_34.xhtml_cite_ref-12-n964){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [[**prīmum**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/primum#Latin "wiktionary:primum"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"}: the adverb.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c34_A_First_Latin_Reader_34.xhtml_cite_note-12-n979}
13. [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c34_A_First_Latin_Reader_34.xhtml_cite_ref-13-n965){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [[**ita**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/ita#Latin "wiktionary:ita"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"}:, *i.e.* under a hot
    fire.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c34_A_First_Latin_Reader_34.xhtml_cite_note-13-n980}
14. [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c34_A_First_Latin_Reader_34.xhtml_cite_ref-14-n966){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}

[]{#c35_A_First_Latin_Reader_35.xhtml}

::::::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}
::: {.titulusHeaderBox about="#mwt1"}
:::

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}
:::

:::::::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
::::::::::: text
::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt26" lang="la"}
[[]{#c35_A_First_Latin_Reader_35.xhtml_pagename49-n984}]{#c35_A_First_Latin_Reader_35.xhtml_id-39-n983
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/49" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 35]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*Operations about Boston*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Sed antequam Vasingtō in Britanniam Novam pervenīre potuit, iterum
ācriter pugnātum est in quōdam colle, ubi posteā Americānī
columnam^[^424]^ maximam eōrum nōmine^[^425]^ statuērunt,^[^426]^ quī
ibī prō lībertāte vītam^[^427]^ suam largītī sunt. Eō^[^428]^ in proeliō
Britannī vīcērunt; sed nē hostēs quidem satis laudāre poterant virtūtem
colōnōrum, quī impetum veterānōrum tam audācter excēperant.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Vasingtō, postquam^[^429]^ illūc^[^430]^ pervēnit, hostīs mēnsēs multōs
[[]{#c35_A_First_Latin_Reader_35.xhtml_pagename51}]{#c35_A_First_Latin_Reader_35.xhtml_id-41
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/51"}intrā mūnītiōnēs
Bostōnis continuit. Tum, cum eius cōpiae maiōrēs factae essent, subitō
noctū prope urbem clam collem quendam occupāvit, atque ibi vāllum summā
celeritāte exstrūxit; quīn etiam ubi diēs illūxit duxque hostium
mūnītiōnēs novās animadvertit, vehementer commōtus ille: “Hī colōnī ūnā
nocte,” inquit, “tanta opera perfēcērunt, quanta^[^431]^ meus exercitus
mēnse tōtō perficere nōn potest.”^[^432]^ Hōc vāllō^[^433]^ exstrūctō,
cum cotīdiē tēla plūrima ballistīs^[^434]^ Americanōrum in urbem
mitterentur, hostēs brevī nāvēs cōnscendere atque ē portū fugere coāctī
sunt.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Colōnī adhūc bellum gesserant ut iūra cīvium Britannicōrum sibi
concēderentur; iam vērō, cum^[^435]^ neque rēx neque^[^436]^ senātus eōs
audīre vellet, dē^[^437]^ Britanniā dēscīscere^[^438]^ novamque condere
rem pūblicam^[^439]^ cōnstituērunt.
:::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
:::

::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt33" lang="la"}
[[]{#c35_A_First_Latin_Reader_35.xhtml_pagename50}]{#c35_A_First_Latin_Reader_35.xhtml_id-40
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/50" about="#mwt28"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

<figure class="mw-halign-center" typeof="mw:File" about="#mwt29">
<a href="https://la.wikisource.org/wiki/Fasciculus:Columna_in_Rome.jpg"
class="mw-file-description"><img
src="images/c138_jpg_500px_Columna_in_Rome.jpg_utm_source_la.wikisource.org_utm_campaign_parser_utm_content_thumbnail"
class="mw-file-element" style="width:500px; height:386px; "
resource="./Fasciculus:Columna_in_Rome.jpg" decoding="async"
data-file-type="bitmap"
data-title="Columna_in_Rome.jpg-500px-Columna_in_Rome.jpg?utm_source=la.wikisource.org&amp;utm_campaign=parser&amp;utm_content=thumbnail" /></a>
</figure>

[ ]{about="#mwt29"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt29"}
[Columna]{.smallcaps}
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt29"}

In the picture is shown a monument about a hundred feet in height,
erected at Rome in 104 [a.d.,]{.smallcaps} in honor of the emperor
Trajan. On its sides are sculptured scenes descriptive of one of
Trajan’s important campaigns, a fact which makes this column a very
important source of information about the details of Roman military
life.

[ ]{about="#mwt29"}

::: {about="#mwt29"}
:::

::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt18" lang="la"}
[[]{#c36_A_First_Latin_Reader_36.xhtml_pagename51-n1022}]{#c36_A_First_Latin_Reader_36.xhtml_id-41-n1021
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/51" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 36]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*The Battles of Long Island and Trenton*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Interim Britannī Novum Eborācum terrā marīque^[^440]^ oppugnāre
parābant. Haud procul est magna īnsula, quae Longa appellatur. Ibi ē
nāvibus ēgressī hostēs cum Americānīs ācriter pugnāvērunt. Quō proeliō
victus Vasingtō nōn sōlum ex īnsulā discēdere sed etiam Novum Eborācum
dīmittere coāctus est. Hīs rēbus factīs, colōnī omnēs animō^[^441]^
[[]{#c36_A_First_Latin_Reader_36.xhtml_pagename52}]{#c36_A_First_Latin_Reader_36.xhtml_id-42
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/52"}vehementer erant
dēmissī: quārē Vasingtō, quamquam tōtō cum exercitū Britannicō in
aciē^[^442]^ pugnāre nōn audēbat, putāvit tamen aliquid sibi faciendum
esse, quod spem cīvibus suīs adferret^[^443]^. Quam facultātem^[^444]^
mox nactus est. Nam Britannī, quī invītī^[^445]^ cum Americānīs
ipsī^[^446]^ pugnābant, multōs Germānōs condūxerant, quī in exercitū
stīpendia facerent; quōrum Germānōrum pars quaedam haud procul ā Novō
Eborācō in hībernīs iam collocāta erat. Quō cōgnitō, Vasingtō noctū
profectus, etsī erat^[^447]^ tempestās maxima flūmenque quoddam
trānseundum erat, ad eōrum castra versus audācter iter fēcit; quō in
itinere duo hominēs frīgore periērunt. Hostēs, quī nihil suspicābantur
diemque fēstum^[^448]^ celebrābant, ab Americānīs facillimē captī sunt.
Tum dēmum colōnī iterum spem magnam habēre coepērunt.
:::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
:::

1.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c36_A_First_Latin_Reader_36.xhtml_cite_ref-1-n1023){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**terrā marīque**: *by land and sea*, the abl. expressing place
    where.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c36_A_First_Latin_Reader_36.xhtml_cite_note-1-n1034}
2.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c36_A_First_Latin_Reader_36.xhtml_cite_ref-2-n1024){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**animō … dēmisssī**: cf. the note on this same phrase, [p.37 l.
    20]( "A First Latin Reader/33"){.noteref
    xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink"}.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c36_A_First_Latin_Reader_36.xhtml_cite_note-2-n1035}
3.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c36_A_First_Latin_Reader_36.xhtml_cite_ref-3-n1027){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [[**aciē:**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/acies#Latin "wiktionary:acies"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"} *regular
    engagement*.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c36_A_First_Latin_Reader_36.xhtml_cite_note-3-n1036}
4.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c36_A_First_Latin_Reader_36.xhtml_cite_ref-4-n1028){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [[**adferret:**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/adfero#Latin "wiktionary:adfero"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"} note the mood. ]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c36_A_First_Latin_Reader_36.xhtml_cite_note-4-n1037}
5.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c36_A_First_Latin_Reader_36.xhtml_cite_ref-5-n1029){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**quam facultátem:** freely, *an opportunity for
    which*.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c36_A_First_Latin_Reader_36.xhtml_cite_note-5-n1038}
6.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c36_A_First_Latin_Reader_36.xhtml_cite_ref-6-n1030){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [[**invītī:**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/invitus:#Latin "wiktionary:invitus:"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"} *with reluctance.*]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c36_A_First_Latin_Reader_36.xhtml_cite_note-6-n1039}
7.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c36_A_First_Latin_Reader_36.xhtml_cite_ref-7-n1031){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**ipsī:** *in person*.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c36_A_First_Latin_Reader_36.xhtml_cite_note-7-n1040}
8.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c36_A_First_Latin_Reader_36.xhtml_cite_ref-8-n1032){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [[**erat**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/sum#Latin "wiktionary:sum"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"} *there was*.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c36_A_First_Latin_Reader_36.xhtml_cite_note-8-n1041}
9.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c36_A_First_Latin_Reader_36.xhtml_cite_ref-9-n1033){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**diem … féstum:** a holiday
    ([**fēstus**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/festus#Latin "wiktionary:festus"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"}, **-a, -um**).]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c36_A_First_Latin_Reader_36.xhtml_cite_note-9-n1042}
:::::::
::::::::
:::::::::::

[]{#c37_A_First_Latin_Reader_37.xhtml}

:::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}
::: {.titulusHeaderBox about="#mwt1"}
:::

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}
:::

::::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
:::::::: text
:::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt24" lang="la"}
[[]{#c37_A_First_Latin_Reader_37.xhtml_pagename52-n1044}]{#c37_A_First_Latin_Reader_37.xhtml_id-42-n1043
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/52" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 37]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*The Retreat from Trenton*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Paulō post Vasingtō, cum ausus esset iterum prōgredi ad eundem locum ubi
Germānōs illōs^[^449]^ cēperat, perīculum adiit maximum. Nam subitō
aderant Britannī plūrimī, nec propter natantem glaciem flūmen trānsīre
Americānī poterant. Tum imperātor Britannicus, quī Cornivallis
appellābātur, cum Vasingtōnem crēderet^[^450]^ iam dēmum circumventum
esse, glōriāns, “Cras^[^451]^,” inquit, “ā mē iste vulpēs^[^452]^
capiētur.”

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

::: {about="#mwt4"}
:::

[[]{#c37_A_First_Latin_Reader_37.xhtml_pagename53}]{#c37_A_First_Latin_Reader_37.xhtml_id-43
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/53" about="#mwt10"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}[At Vasingtō suōs iussit sub vesperum in
castrīs ignīs facere, ut]{about="#mwt11"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}^[^453]^[ cotīdiē
solēbant]{about="#mwt11"}^[^454]^[, cum interim
paucī]{about="#mwt11"}^[^455]^[ maximō cum strepitū circum
vāllum]{about="#mwt11"}^[^456]^[ opus
fēstīnārent]{about="#mwt11"}^[^457]^[; quod]{about="#mwt11"}^[^458]^[ eō
cōnsiliō]{about="#mwt11"}^[^459]^[ iussit, ut Britannī arbitrārentur ibi
impetum hostium excipere Americānōs parāre. Nocte tamen intempestā
colōnī, sine strepitū ūllō ex castrīs ēgressī, viīs dēviīs iter fēcērunt
circum exercitum Britannicum, atque in agrōs apertōs incolumēs
pervēnērunt. Itaque māne imperātor Britannōrum “vulpem istum” invenīre
nōn potuit; Vasingtō enim etiam tum oppidum
oppugnābat]{about="#mwt11"}^[^460]^[ alterum, ubi quidam Britannī aliī
castra posuerant. Quārē Cornivallis, cum sentīret sē ēlūsum esse,
celeriter sē recēpit, ut impedīmenta cōnservāret sua, quae ad
pugnam]{about="#mwt11"}^[^461]^[ profectus post tergum longē relīquerat.
]{about="#mwt11"}
::::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}

1.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c37_A_First_Latin_Reader_37.xhtml_cite_ref-1-n1045){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**illōs:** *i.e*. those mentioned in Lesson 36.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c37_A_First_Latin_Reader_37.xhtml_cite_note-1-n1060}
2.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c37_A_First_Latin_Reader_37.xhtml_cite_ref-2-n1046){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**cum … crēderet**: translate by a participial phrase; so also on
    the next page, l. 11. In Latin the pres. part. is used much less
    freely than in English.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c37_A_First_Latin_Reader_37.xhtml_cite_note-2-n1061}
3.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c37_A_First_Latin_Reader_37.xhtml_cite_ref-3-n1047){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}

    .reference-text}]{#c37_A_First_Latin_Reader_37.xhtml_cite_note-5-n1064}

    [**solebant[ ]{typeof="mw:DisplaySpace"}:** sc.
    **facere.**]{.mw-reference-text

7.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c37_A_First_Latin_Reader_37.xhtml_cite_ref-7-n1053){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}

    camp.]{.mw-reference-text

9.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c37_A_First_Latin_Reader_37.xhtml_cite_ref-9-n1055){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}

    [**ad pugnam:** **for a battle (merely), i.e.** not for a campaign.

[[]{#c38_A_First_Latin_Reader_38.xhtml_pagename53-n1074}]{#c38_A_First_Latin_Reader_38.xhtml_id-43-n1073
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/53" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 38]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*Burgoyne’s Campaign*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Posterō annō alius imperātor Britannicus ex Canadā per prōvinciam
Noveborācēnsem legiōnēs quāsdam dūcere cōnātus est. Cui^[^462]^
omnia^[^463]^ prīmō fēlīciter ēvēnērunt; Taeconderōga enim capta est ūnā
cum cōpiīs omnibus, quās eō^[^464]^ Americānī comportāverant. Cum autem
Germānī multī ē Britannicō exercitū in proximam prōvinciam missī essent
ut equōs aliāsque cōpiās colōnōrum raperent,
[[]{#c38_A_First_Latin_Reader_38.xhtml_pagename54}]{#c38_A_First_Latin_Reader_38.xhtml_id-44
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/54"}agricolae, quī ā
pueritiā arma ferre solitī erant, undique statim convenērunt;
Germānīsque magnō cum dētrīmentō ex illā prōvinciā discēdere coāctīs,
imperātōrem ipsum mox ācerrimē adortī sunt Americānī, quōrum in
diēs^[^465]^ cōpiae maiōrēs fīēbant.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Quō proeliō victī hostēs, quī iam omnibus ex partibus^[^466]^
obsidēbantur, in Canadam redīre prīmō frūstrā cōnātī, postrēmō
Americānīs^[^467]^ in dēditiōnem vēnērunt. Tum scīlicet colōnī omnēs
ecfrēnātē gaudēbant, quod^[^468]^ perīculum maximum effūgisse
vidēbantur^[^469]^. Sed alibī hostēs ācriter gerēbant^[^470]^ bellum;
cuius ēventus adhūc maximē dubius^[^471]^ erat.
:::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
:::

1.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c38_A_First_Latin_Reader_38.xhtml_cite_ref-1-n1075){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**cui:** for whom.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c38_A_First_Latin_Reader_38.xhtml_cite_note-1-n1087}
2.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c38_A_First_Latin_Reader_38.xhtml_cite_ref-2-n1076){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**omnia:** note the gender.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c38_A_First_Latin_Reader_38.xhtml_cite_note-2-n1088}
3.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c38_A_First_Latin_Reader_38.xhtml_cite_ref-3-n1077){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**eō:** *there,* lit. *thither;* cf. the note on **quō**, [p. 8, l.
    14](#c8_A_First_Latin_Reader_8.xhtml_cite_ref-17 "A First Latin Reader/8"){.noteref
    xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink"}.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c38_A_First_Latin_Reader_38.xhtml_cite_note-3-n1089}
4.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c38_A_First_Latin_Reader_38.xhtml_cite_ref-4-n1080){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**in diēs:** *from day to day*.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c38_A_First_Latin_Reader_38.xhtml_cite_note-4-n1090}
5.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c38_A_First_Latin_Reader_38.xhtml_cite_ref-5-n1081){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**omnibus ex partibus:** *on all sides.*]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c38_A_First_Latin_Reader_38.xhtml_cite_note-5-n1091}
6.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c38_A_First_Latin_Reader_38.xhtml_cite_ref-6-n1082){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [[**Americānīs:**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/americanus#Latin "wiktionary:americanus"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"} dat. case.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c38_A_First_Latin_Reader_38.xhtml_cite_note-6-n1092}
7.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c38_A_First_Latin_Reader_38.xhtml_cite_ref-7-n1083){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**quod:** conjunction.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c38_A_First_Latin_Reader_38.xhtml_cite_note-7-n1093}
8.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c38_A_First_Latin_Reader_38.xhtml_cite_ref-8-n1084){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**vidēbantur:** sc. **sibi**, *i.e. they seemed to themselves;
    freely, they thought that they,* etc.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c38_A_First_Latin_Reader_38.xhtml_cite_note-8-n1094}
9.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c38_A_First_Latin_Reader_38.xhtml_cite_ref-9-n1085){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**gerēbant:** note the tense.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c38_A_First_Latin_Reader_38.xhtml_cite_note-9-n1095}
10. [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c38_A_First_Latin_Reader_38.xhtml_cite_ref-10-n1086){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**maximē dubius:** by the prefixing of
    [**maximē**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/maxime#Latin "wiktionary:maxime"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"}, an adj. (or adv.) is raised to the
    superlative degree.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c38_A_First_Latin_Reader_38.xhtml_cite_note-10-n1096}

[]{#c39_A_First_Latin_Reader_39.xhtml}

::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}
::: {.titulusHeaderBox about="#mwt1"}

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}

:::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
::::::: text
::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt28" lang="la"}
[[]{#c39_A_First_Latin_Reader_39.xhtml_pagename54-n1098}]{#c39_A_First_Latin_Reader_39.xhtml_id-44-n1097
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/54" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 39]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*Valley Forge*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Dum geruntur haec^[^472]^, dē quibus modo dixī, Britannī Philadelphiam
oppugnāre parābant, quae urbs^[^473]^ tum erat caput reī publicae
Americānae. Unde Vasingtō, cuius cōpiae numerō^[^474]^ erant
multō^[^475]^ īnferiōrēs, hostēs nūllō modō arcēre poterat; quārē
senātus ad aliud oppidum sē recēpit, ac Philadelphia nūllō^[^476]^
dēfendente^[^477]^ ā Britannīs capta est.
[[]{#c39_A_First_Latin_Reader_39.xhtml_pagename55}]{#c39_A_First_Latin_Reader_39.xhtml_id-45
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/55"}Paucīs post diēbus
circiter quīnque mīlibus passuum^[^478]^ ab^[^479]^ eādem urbe ācriter
pugnātum est^[^480]^, sed tum quoque Vasingtō discessit īnferior. Quī
igitur, cum^[^481]^ hiems iam adesset, mīlitēs suōs in hībernīs
collocāvit in quādam valle, ubi mēnsēs multōs summā cum^[^482]^ inopiā
omnium rērum necessāriārum miserrimē^[^483]^ vīctum est^[^484]^. Nam nōn
sōlum in aerāriō^[^485]^ nūlla erat pecūnia, sed in castrīs mox
frūmentum quoque dēficere coepit; mīlitēsque miserī, quibus^[^486]^
erant saga nūlla, saepe noctēs tōtās prope ignem vigilāre coāctī sunt.
Quīn etiam trāditum est, cum agmen in hīberna iter faceret,
multōrum^[^487]^ pedēs nūdōs in nive vestīgia cruenta fēcisse.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Sed iam dēmum ex Eurōpā sociī Americānīs^[^488]^ auxilium ferre
parābant; multī enim etiam aliīs ex gentibus^[^489]^ molestē ferēbant
Britannōs iūra cīvium colōnīs concēdere nōluisse.
:::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
:::

1.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c39_A_First_Latin_Reader_39.xhtml_cite_ref-1-n1099){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**haec:** neut. pl.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c39_A_First_Latin_Reader_39.xhtml_cite_note-1-n1119}
2.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c39_A_First_Latin_Reader_39.xhtml_cite_ref-2-n1100){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**quae urbs:** *the city which;* lit. what?]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c39_A_First_Latin_Reader_39.xhtml_cite_note-2-n1120}
3.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c39_A_First_Latin_Reader_39.xhtml_cite_ref-3-n1101){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**numerō:** for syntax, cf. **animō**, [p. 37, l.
    20]( "A First Latin Reader/33"){.noteref
    xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink"}.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c39_A_First_Latin_Reader_39.xhtml_cite_note-3-n1121}
4.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c39_A_First_Latin_Reader_39.xhtml_cite_ref-4-n1102){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**multō:** *(by) much.*]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c39_A_First_Latin_Reader_39.xhtml_cite_note-4-n1122}
5.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c39_A_First_Latin_Reader_39.xhtml_cite_ref-5-n1103){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [[**nūllō:**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/nullus#Latin "wiktionary:nullus"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"} supplying the missing abl. of
    [**nēmō**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/nemo#Latin "wiktionary:nemo"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"}. ]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c39_A_First_Latin_Reader_39.xhtml_cite_note-5-n1123}
6.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c39_A_First_Latin_Reader_39.xhtml_cite_ref-6-n1104){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [[**dēfendente:**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/defendens#Latin "wiktionary:defendens"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"} sc. **eam** (i.e. **Philadelphiam**).
    For the pres. part. being active in meaning, may take an object even
    when used, as here, in the abl. absol.
    construction.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c39_A_First_Latin_Reader_39.xhtml_cite_note-6-n1124}
7.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c39_A_First_Latin_Reader_39.xhtml_cite_ref-7-n1107){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**quinque milibus passuum:** abl. of degree of
    difference.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c39_A_First_Latin_Reader_39.xhtml_cite_note-7-n1125}
8.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c39_A_First_Latin_Reader_39.xhtml_cite_ref-8-n1108){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**ab:** *(away) from*.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c39_A_First_Latin_Reader_39.xhtml_cite_note-8-n1126}
9.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c39_A_First_Latin_Reader_39.xhtml_cite_ref-9-n1109){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [[**pugnātum
    est**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/pugno#Latin "wiktionary:pugno"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"}: a battle was fought; lit.
    what?]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c39_A_First_Latin_Reader_39.xhtml_cite_note-9-n1127}
10. [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c39_A_First_Latin_Reader_39.xhtml_cite_ref-10-n1110){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [[**cum:**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/cum#Latin "wiktionary:cum"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"} *as,* or *since*.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c39_A_First_Latin_Reader_39.xhtml_cite_note-10-n1128}
11. [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c39_A_First_Latin_Reader_39.xhtml_cite_ref-11-n1111){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [[**cum:**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/cum#Latin "wiktionary:cum"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"} freely, under the stress
    of.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c39_A_First_Latin_Reader_39.xhtml_cite_note-11-n1129}
12. [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c39_A_First_Latin_Reader_39.xhtml_cite_ref-12-n1112){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [[**miserrimē**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/misere#Latin "wiktionary:misere"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"}: miserē (adv.), wretchedly.
    ]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c39_A_First_Latin_Reader_39.xhtml_cite_note-12-n1130}
13. [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c39_A_First_Latin_Reader_39.xhtml_cite_ref-13-n1113){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [[**vīctum
    est:**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/vivo#Latin "wiktionary:vivo"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"} impersonal pass. (from
    vīvō).]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c39_A_First_Latin_Reader_39.xhtml_cite_note-13-n1131}
14. [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c39_A_First_Latin_Reader_39.xhtml_cite_ref-14-n1114){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [[**aerāriō:**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/aerarium#Latin "wiktionary:aerarium"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"} **aerārium, -rī,** [n.]{.smallcaps},
    *public treasury*.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c39_A_First_Latin_Reader_39.xhtml_cite_note-14-n1132}
15. [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c39_A_First_Latin_Reader_39.xhtml_cite_ref-15-n1115){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**quibus:** dat. case; cf. **cui**, p. 11, l.
    2.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c39_A_First_Latin_Reader_39.xhtml_cite_note-15-n1133}
16. [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c39_A_First_Latin_Reader_39.xhtml_cite_ref-16-n1116){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**multōrum:** as (masc.) noun; cf. **multī**, l.
    13.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c39_A_First_Latin_Reader_39.xhtml_cite_note-16-n1134}
17. [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c39_A_First_Latin_Reader_39.xhtml_cite_ref-17-n1117){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**Americānīs:** indirect obj. with **auxilium
    ferre**.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c39_A_First_Latin_Reader_39.xhtml_cite_note-17-n1135}
18. [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c39_A_First_Latin_Reader_39.xhtml_cite_ref-18-n1118){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**aliīs ex gentibus:** *i.e. of other
    nationalities*.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c39_A_First_Latin_Reader_39.xhtml_cite_note-18-n1136}

[]{#c40_A_First_Latin_Reader_40.xhtml}

::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}
::: {.titulusHeaderBox about="#mwt1"}
:::

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}
:::

:::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
::::::: text
::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt28" lang="la"}
[[]{#c40_A_First_Latin_Reader_40.xhtml_pagename55-n1138}]{#c40_A_First_Latin_Reader_40.xhtml_id-45-n1137
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/55" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 40]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*Help from France*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Ita hōc ferē tempore factum erat^[^490]^ ut Gallī, quī Britannōs minimē
amābant, cum^[^491]^ Americānīs facerent foedus^[^492]^ atque trāns mare
imperātōrem cum classe mitterent, quī colōnōs
[[]{#c40_A_First_Latin_Reader_40.xhtml_pagename56}]{#c40_A_First_Latin_Reader_40.xhtml_id-46
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/56"}adiuvāret. Quibus
rēbus^[^493]^ cōgnitīs, Britannī illī, quī Philadelphiae^[^494]^
cōnsedērant, cum sentīrent flūmine classe obsessō ^[^495]^ sē undique
oppugnārī^[^496]^ posse^[^497]^, celeriter sēsē^[^498]^ coniūnxērunt cum
cōpiīs aliīs, quae in prōvinciā proximā collocātae erant. Ita
Philadelphia rursus in Americānōrum potestātem pervēnit.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Adhūc Britannī crēdiderant colōnōs facile vincī posse: sed iam dēmum
sensērunt sē rem difficillimam tractāre; cumque^[^499]^ in prōvinciīs,
quae ad merīdiem spectant, colōnī rārī multīs cum servīs in praediīs
maximīs habitārent, in eās^[^500]^ cōnstituērunt exercitūs suōs mittere,
sī^[^501]^ ibi rem gerere fēlīcius possent. Nec vērō^[^502]^ eōs
cōnsilium fefellit; nam Gorgia ūnā cum aliīs quibusdam prōvinciīs brevī
est occupāta, et ubicumque^[^503]^ in aciē pugnatum est, Americānī victī
sunt. Quibus dētrīmentīs minimē animō dēmissī, colōnī iam manūs^[^504]^
parvās coēgērunt, quae in silvīs palūdibusque latēbant^[^505]^, dōnec
occāsiōnem reī bene gerendae^[^506]^ nancīscerentur^[^507]^; tum subitō
impetū factō aut capiēbant Britannōs aut eōs in fugam dabant.
:::::

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}

::::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
:::::::: text
:::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt29" lang="la"}
[[]{#c41_A_First_Latin_Reader_41.xhtml_pagename56-n1178}]{#c41_A_First_Latin_Reader_41.xhtml_id-46-n1177
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/56" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 41]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*Benedict Arnold*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Dum haec geruntur, in prōvinciā Noveborācēnsī quīdam imperātor
Americānus, nōmine Arnoldius, dux audāx ac
[[]{#c41_A_First_Latin_Reader_41.xhtml_pagename57}]{#c41_A_First_Latin_Reader_41.xhtml_id-47
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/57"}strēnuus, Britannīs
parābat prōdere castra^[^508]^, quae colōnī in rīpā flūminīs Hudsōnis
posuerant, quōque^[^509]^ ab Americānīs comportāta erant omnia^[^510]^,
quae ad^[^511]^ bellum necessāria erant; nam castra nātūrā^[^512]^ locī
mūnitissima erant, ac fūnis^[^513]^ quōque ferreus^[^514]^ ibi trāns
flūmen ductus erat^[^515]^, nē nāvēs hostium longius adversō flūmine
nāvigāre possent.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Britannī, cum iam diēs prōditiōnis^[^516]^ appropinquāret, nūntium
mīsērunt, quī ducem convenīret Americānum, litterāsque ab eō reportāret.
Incolumis ad Arnoldium pervēnit nūntius; sed cum ad Britannōs redīret,
ab Americānīs tribus captus est: quī captīvum sine morā in castra
proxima dēdūxērunt, quamquam ille miser^[^517]^ omnibus modīs ab eīs
salūtem impetrāre cōnātus est. Quā dē rē certior factus, Arnoldius ad
Britannōs quam celerrimē^[^518]^ perfūgit; quōrum in exercitū^[^519]^
imperātor brevī factus est.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Nūntius interim, causā cōgnitā^[^520]^, capitis^[^521]^ est damnātus;
litterās enim, quās manū^[^522]^ ducis Americānī scrīptās ferēbat,
dēlēre nōn potuerat, antequam in castrā ā colōnīs tribus ductus est.
Arnoldius, cum contrā suōs^[^523]^ cīvēs ācerrimē bellum
gessisset^[^524]^, postrēmō apud Britannōs mortuus est, etiam eīs
ipsīs^[^525]^ invīsus quōs tantā perfidiā adiuvāre cōnātus erat.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

::: {about="#mwt4"}
:::
::::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
:::

    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"} note the case.]{.mw-reference-text

    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"

    ]{.mw-reference-text

    erat:**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/duco#Latin "wiktionary:duco"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"} *had been
    stretched*.]{.mw-reference-text

9.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c41_A_First_Latin_Reader_41.xhtml_cite_ref-9-n1189){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [[**prōditiōnis:**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/proditio#Latin "wiktionary:proditio"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"} **prōditiō, -ōnis,** [f.]{.smallcaps},
    *betrayal;* cf. the verb
    [**prōdō**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/prodo#Latin "wiktionary:prodo"){.extiw

    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"}, l. 1. ]{.mw-reference-text

10. [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c41_A_First_Latin_Reader_41.xhtml_cite_ref-10-n1190){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**ille miser:** *he, poor fellow.* ]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c41_A_First_Latin_Reader_41.xhtml_cite_note-10-n1208}
11. [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c41_A_First_Latin_Reader_41.xhtml_cite_ref-11-n1191){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**quam celerrimē:** as quickly as possible.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c41_A_First_Latin_Reader_41.xhtml_cite_note-11-n1209}
12. [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c41_A_First_Latin_Reader_41.xhtml_cite_ref-12-n1192){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**quōrum in exercitū**: *and in their army*.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c41_A_First_Latin_Reader_41.xhtml_cite_note-12-n1210}
13. [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c41_A_First_Latin_Reader_41.xhtml_cite_ref-13-n1193){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**cōgnitā:** *tried*. ]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c41_A_First_Latin_Reader_41.xhtml_cite_note-13-n1211}
14. [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c41_A_First_Latin_Reader_41.xhtml_cite_ref-14-n1194){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [[**capitis:**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/caput#Latin "wiktionary:caput"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"} *i.e. to death*. The charge or (less
    often) the penalty may be expressed, as here, by the
    genitive.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c41_A_First_Latin_Reader_41.xhtml_cite_note-14-n1212}
15. [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c41_A_First_Latin_Reader_41.xhtml_cite_ref-15-n1195){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**manu:** abl. of means with **scrīptās**.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c41_A_First_Latin_Reader_41.xhtml_cite_note-15-n1213}
16. [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c41_A_First_Latin_Reader_41.xhtml_cite_ref-16-n1196){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**suōs:** observe the emphatic position (cf. the note on
    [**suum**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/suum#Latin "wiktionary:suum"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"}, p. 11, l. 6). ]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c41_A_First_Latin_Reader_41.xhtml_cite_note-16-n1214}
17. [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c41_A_First_Latin_Reader_41.xhtml_cite_ref-17-n1197){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**cum … gessisset:** *after waging*.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c41_A_First_Latin_Reader_41.xhtml_cite_note-17-n1215}
18. [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c41_A_First_Latin_Reader_41.xhtml_cite_ref-18-n1198){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**eīs ipsīs:** dat. case; construe with
    **invīsus**.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c41_A_First_Latin_Reader_41.xhtml_cite_note-18-n1216}

[]{#c42_A_First_Latin_Reader_42.xhtml}

::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}
::: {.titulusHeaderBox about="#mwt1"}
:::

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}
:::

:::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
::::::: text
::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt27" lang="la"}
[[]{#c42_A_First_Latin_Reader_42.xhtml_pagename58}]{#c42_A_First_Latin_Reader_42.xhtml_id-48
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/58" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 42]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*A Roman who fought against his Country*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Quibus rēbus admoneor ut pauca^[^526]^ dīcam dē Coriolānō, clārō duce
Rōmānō; quī^[^527]^ imperātor fortissimus, ā cīvibus iniūriā^[^528]^
damnātus, ab urbe^[^529]^ discessit sēque coniūnxit cum hostibus, quī
anteā bellum Rōmānīs^[^530]^ saepe intulerant.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Dēnuō^[^531]^ mox bellō indictō, hostibus prīmō rēs undique fēlīciter
ēvēnērunt, Rōmānīque lēgātōs pācis petendae causā^[^532]^ ad Coriolānum
mittere coāctī sunt. Quī autem, propter iniūriam ā cīvibus inlātam adhūc
irātus, asperius^[^533]^ respondit lēgātōsque^[^534]^
maestissimōs^[^535]^ domum dīmīsit; quīn etiam īdem^[^536]^ nūntiī ā
senātū iterum missī nē in castra receptī quidem sunt.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Quibus rēbus cōgnitīs, Rōmānī graviter permōtī etiam sacerdōtēs mittere
cōnstituērunt, sī ab eīs saltem Coriolānī animus ferōx^[^537]^
flectī^[^538]^ posset; cum
vērō[**vērō:**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/vero#Latin "wiktionary:vero"){.extiw
rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"} *and*. nē hī quidem quicquam^[^539]^
impetrāre potuissent, tum māter ipsa uxorque Coriolānī ūnā cum aliīs
mātrōnīs complūribus ad hostium castra maestae^[^540]^ profectae sunt.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Quō ubi perventum est, mātris verbis vehementer commōtus Coriolānus
pollicitus est sē sine morā cum exercitū ē fīnibus Rōmānōrum
discessūrum. Posteā apud hostīs
[[]{#c42_A_First_Latin_Reader_42.xhtml_pagename59}]{#c42_A_First_Latin_Reader_42.xhtml_id-49
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/59"}multōs annōs
vīxit^[^541]^, nec libenter^[^542]^; nam trāditum est eum esse solitum
dīcere senī^[^543]^ miserrimum esse exsilium.
:::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
