:::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt20" lang="la"}
[[]{#c43_A_First_Latin_Reader_43.xhtml_pagename59-n1258}]{#c43_A_First_Latin_Reader_43.xhtml_id-49-n1257
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/59" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 43]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*The Surrender of Cornwallis*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Sed ut ad Americānōs redeāmus^[^544]^, ab eīs diū ac variā fortūnā
bellum cum Britannīs gestum est. At paulātim oppida prōvinciārum, quae
ad merīdiem spectant, rursus in potestātem Americānōrum venērunt, ac
Cornivallis, quī iam ibi^[^545]^ bellum gerēbat, in Virginiam postrēmō
sē recipere coāctus est; quā in prōvinciā summā cum licentiā^[^546]^
rapere et agere^[^547]^ coepit omnia.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Vasingtō autem iam aderat cum exercitū sociīsque Gallicīs; et
Cornivallis in urbe mūnītissimā^[^548]^, quae Eborācopolis appellātur,
undique obsessus, oppugnātiōnem duōs mēnsēs aegrē sustinuit. Tum
hostēs^[^549]^, cum frūstrā ērumpere cōnātī essent parsque mūnītiōnum ab
Americānīs esset expugnāta, sē suaque omnia Vasingtōnī dēdidērunt.
Cornivallis autem ipse, nē suis^[^550]^ oculīs īgnōminiam exercitūs
vidēret^[^551]^, eō diē sē esse aegrum simulābat, atque in tabernāculō,
dōnec dēditiō est facta, maestus morātus est.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Hāc victōriā nūntiātā, Americānī ecfrēnātē gaudēbant; ac senātus in
templum convocātus dīs^[^552]^ grātiās maximās ēgit.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

::: {about="#mwt4"}
:::

[[]{#c43_A_First_Latin_Reader_43.xhtml_pagename61}]{#c43_A_First_Latin_Reader_43.xhtml_id-51
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/61" about="#mwt15"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}[Omnēs enim sentiēbant
Britannīs]{about="#mwt16" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}^[^553]^[ pācem iam
demum esse petendam. ]{about="#mwt16"}
::::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
:::

1.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c43_A_First_Latin_Reader_43.xhtml_cite_ref-1-n1259){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**ut … redeāmus:** *to return*.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c43_A_First_Latin_Reader_43.xhtml_cite_note-1-n1271}
2.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c43_A_First_Latin_Reader_43.xhtml_cite_ref-2-n1260){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [[**ibī:**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/ibi#Latin "wiktionary:ibi"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"} in that region.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c43_A_First_Latin_Reader_43.xhtml_cite_note-2-n1272}
3.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c43_A_First_Latin_Reader_43.xhtml_cite_ref-3-n1261){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [[**licentiā:**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/licentia#Latin "wiktionary:licentia"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"} **licentia, -ae,** [f.]{.smallcaps},
    *lawlessness*.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c43_A_First_Latin_Reader_43.xhtml_cite_note-3-n1273}
4.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c43_A_First_Latin_Reader_43.xhtml_cite_ref-4-n1262){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**rapere et agere:** freely, *rob and plunder*; strictly, *steal*
    (goods) *and drive off* (livestock).]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c43_A_First_Latin_Reader_43.xhtml_cite_note-4-n1274}
5.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c43_A_First_Latin_Reader_43.xhtml_cite_ref-5-n1263){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**mūnītissimā:** strongly fortified.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c43_A_First_Latin_Reader_43.xhtml_cite_note-5-n1275}
6.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c43_A_First_Latin_Reader_43.xhtml_cite_ref-6-n1264){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [[**hostēs:**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/hostis#Latin "wiktionary:hostis"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"} *i.e.* the English.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c43_A_First_Latin_Reader_43.xhtml_cite_note-6-n1276}
7.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c43_A_First_Latin_Reader_43.xhtml_cite_ref-7-n1265){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**suīs:** cf. again **suum**, p. 11, l. 6.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c43_A_First_Latin_Reader_43.xhtml_cite_note-7-n1277}
8.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c43_A_First_Latin_Reader_43.xhtml_cite_ref-8-n1266){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**nē … vidēret:** freely, *in order to avoid
    seeing*.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c43_A_First_Latin_Reader_43.xhtml_cite_note-8-n1278}
9.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c43_A_First_Latin_Reader_43.xhtml_cite_ref-9-n1267){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [[**dīs:**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/dives#Latin "wiktionary:dives"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"} cf. p. 14, l. 19.]{.mw-reference-text

10. [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c43_A_First_Latin_Reader_43.xhtml_cite_ref-10-n1270){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**Britannīs:** cf. the note on **sībi**, p. 34, l.
    21.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c43_A_First_Latin_Reader_43.xhtml_cite_note-10-n1280}

[]{#c44_A_First_Latin_Reader_44.xhtml}

:::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}
::: {.titulusHeaderBox about="#mwt1"}
:::

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}
:::

::::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
:::::::: text
:::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt20" lang="la"}
[[]{#c44_A_First_Latin_Reader_44.xhtml_pagename61-n1282}]{#c44_A_First_Latin_Reader_44.xhtml_id-51-n1281
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/61" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 44]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*Washington retires to Private Life*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Pāce factā, Carletō, dux Britannicus, quī tum Eborācum Novum praesidiō
tenēbat, cum exercitū nāvēs cōnscendere domumque redīre ā rēge iussus
est.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Illam in urbem Vasingtō lēgātōs^[^554]^ suōs paulō post convocāvit.
Cumque pauca locūtus eōs valēre iussisset^[^555]^, lēgātī, quī eō
duce^[^556]^ annōs circiter^[^557]^ octō stīpendia fēcerant^[^558]^,
lacrimās nōn potuērunt diūtius continēre, sed flentēs imperātōrem dextrā
tenuērunt. Lēgātīs dīmissīs, Vasingtō, ut^[^559]^ imperium suum
dēpōneret, ad urbem statim profectus est, ubi senātus^[^560]^ tum
habēbātur.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Cum^[^561]^ iter faceret, multitūdinēs maximae ex oppidīs omnibus
ēgressae flōrēs in viā sparsērunt^[^562]^; et inter fausta^[^563]^
nōmina etiam pater patriae est appellātus. Sic prōgressus est usque ad
urbem, ubi eum senātus exspectābat^[^564]^; tum imperiō dēpositō, domum
sine morā contendit, arbitrātus^[^565]^ sē iam in praediō iūre^[^566]^
ōtiōsum^[^567]^ vīvere posse, sīcut fēcerat, antequam bellum indictum
est.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

::: {about="#mwt4"}
:::
::::::

::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt32" lang="la"}
[[]{#c45_A_First_Latin_Reader_45.xhtml_pagename62}]{#c45_A_First_Latin_Reader_45.xhtml_id-52
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/62" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 45]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*The Father of his Country*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Laus^[^568]^ maxima Vasingtōnī tribuenda est^[^569]^, quod^[^570]^ sē
rēgem facere nōluit. Sed eius nōmen manet semperque mānsūrum est^[^571]^
in animīs hominum, in aeternitāte^[^572]^ tempōrum^[^573]^, neque
aliud^[^574]^ umquam ab Americānīs aequē^[^575]^ amābitur. Quod^[^576]^
ille pater patriae appellātus est, hīc est^[^577]^ honor, quī
paucīs^[^578]^ contigit^[^579]^. Nam abhinc multōs annōs Cicerō ita est
vocātus, cum vīcisset cīvīs pessimōs, quī rem pūblicam perdere^[^580]^
voluerant; et antīquitus hoc idem cōgnōmen^[^581]^ Camillō ā cīvibus
grātīs^[^582]^ iūre datum est.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Nam ille vir Rōmānus, dux fortis clārusque, iniūriā in iūs vocātus,
abierat in exsilium, vīvēbatque apud Ardeātēs^[^583]^, cum Gallī^[^584]^
plūrimī trāns montēs in Ītaliam subitō profectī, proeliō ācrī vīcērunt
Rōmānōs, urbemque^[^585]^ ipsam incendērunt. Tum Camillus, conciliō
convocātō, Ardeātēs hortātus est ut audācter fīnēs dēfenderent suōs,
Rōmānīsque fortiter auxilium ferrent. Itaque, illō duce, oppidānī noctū
clam profectī, in quōsdam Gallōs, quī sine custōdiīs in agrō apertō
[[]{#c45_A_First_Latin_Reader_45.xhtml_pagename63}]{#c45_A_First_Latin_Reader_45.xhtml_id-53
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/63"}humī iacēbant
sōpītī, maximō clāmōre fēcērunt impetum, eōsque in fugam dedērunt. Ac
paulō post reliquī quoque hostēs, quī in castrīs ad Rōmam^[^586]^ morātī
erant, ā Camillō paene ad ūnum^[^587]^ occīsī sunt.
:::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}

[[]{#c46_A_First_Latin_Reader_46.xhtml_pagename63-n1356}]{#c46_A_First_Latin_Reader_46.xhtml_id-53-n1355

typeof="mw:Transclusion"}[]{about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[]{#c46_A_First_Latin_Reader_46.xhtml_pagename64}]{#c46_A_First_Latin_Reader_46.xhtml_id-54
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/64" about="#mwt5"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

[]{.mw-empty-elt about="#mwt6" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt6"}
[[[TALES OF LAND AND
SEA]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt6"}
[[LESSON 45]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt6"}
*The Settler’s Daughter*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt6"}

In Britanniā Novā quondam agricolae, quī semper impetūs timēbant
Indōrum, in agrōs cotīdiē sēcum arma ferre solēbant; ac prope quendam
vīcum in colle ēditō ^[^588]^ castellum quoque positum erat,
quō^[^589]^, sī quandō^[^590]^ opus esset^[^591]^, colōnī līberōs
uxōrēsque statim dēdūcerent. Quō ex castellō ōlim signum subitō datum
est Indōs adesse. Hōc audītō, agricolae, equīs in agrīs sine
morā^[^592]^ relictīs, ad villās cucurrērunt, et mulierēs ac līberōs
quam celerrimē^[^593]^ in castellum dēdūcere coepērunt.

[ ]{about="#mwt6"}

At vir quīdam, cui erat fīlia tantum, ad castellum cum eā pervenīre nōn
potuit, priusquam^[^594]^ Indī in cōnspectum vēnērunt; itaque puellam
parvam in arbore cavā collocāvit, nē hostēs eam invenīre possent,
ipseque, ut auxilium cīvibus suīs ferret, per agrōs fortiter contendit.

[ ]{about="#mwt6"}

In proeliō, quod est ibi commissum^[^595]^, ab Indīs captī, in silvās
longinquās dēductī sunt agricolae paucī, in eīs^[^596]^ ille vir, dē quō
modo dīxī. Oppidānī scīlicet crēdidērunt fīliam ūnā cum patre captam
esse: sed ille multīs post mēnsibus
[[]{#c46_A_First_Latin_Reader_46.xhtml_pagename65}]{#c46_A_First_Latin_Reader_46.xhtml_id-55
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/65"}ex Indōrum vīcō clam
effūgit; cumque postrēmō domum pervēnisset neque in oppidō fīliam
potuisset invenīre, cīvīs suōs ad arborem cavam dēdūxit. Ibi reperta
sunt ossa^[^597]^ tantum et sagitta ūna.
::::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}

    high.]{.mw-reference-text

:::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
::::::: text
::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt24" lang="la"}
[[]{#c47_A_First_Latin_Reader_47.xhtml_pagename65-n1382}]{#c47_A_First_Latin_Reader_47.xhtml_id-55-n1381
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/65" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 47]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*The Trials of War*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Ab hostibus trānsmarīnīs^[^598]^ quī ōlim bellum cum colōnīs Americānīs
multōs annōs gessērunt, facinora atrōcia^[^599]^ facta esse
dīcuntur^[^600]^ plūrima. Nam cuidam colōnō erant duo equī pulcherrimī,
quōs ille maximā dīligentiā cūrābat; at imperātor hostium, quī hoc
oppidum praesidiō tenēbat, quīque^[^601]^ erat omnibus oppidānīs^[^602]^
superbiā^[^603]^ maximē invīsus, illōs equōs quondam ad sē dūcī iussit,
quod nūntium cum litterīs ad castra longinqua mittere vellet^[^604]^.
Sed ūnum ex equīs nēmō posteā vīdit, alterque paucīs post hōrīs in viā
moribundus haud procul repertus est.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Praedam quoque ē villīs undique rapere solēbant hostēs; sed eōs quondam
duo servī Āfrī callidē^[^605]^ ēlūsērunt; postquam enim mīlitēs
appropinquāre nūntiātum est, hī servī fidēlēs, tabulā^[^606]^ abreptā,
argentum dominī celeriter sub aedibus condidērunt. Ūnus autem ex eīs sub
aedibus argentum vix ab alterō accēperat, cum subitō hostēs in
cōnspectum vēnērunt. Itaque ille^[^607]^, quī suprā stābat,
tabulam^[^608]^
[[]{#c47_A_First_Latin_Reader_47.xhtml_pagename66}]{#c47_A_First_Latin_Reader_47.xhtml_id-56
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/66"}statim
dēmīsit^[^609]^, ne quid^[^610]^ hostēs suspicārentur; ac servus alter,
quī nūllō modō ēvādere poterat, trīs diēs noctēsque sub aedibus
dīcitur^[^611]^ sine aquā cibōve mānsisse.
:::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}

[[]{#c48_A_First_Latin_Reader_48.xhtml_pagename66-n1414}]{#c48_A_First_Latin_Reader_48.xhtml_id-56-n1413

typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 48]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*The Attempt to surprise Detroit*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Postquam bellum, quod^[^612]^ ā Britannīs cum Gallīs Indīsque gerēbātur,
paene cōnfectum est, multaque castella longinqua in potestātem
Britannōrum vēnērunt, quīdam rēx Indōrum, nōmine Pontiac, dux fortis et
ācer, castella illa recipere^[^613]^ Britannōsque ita ex eīs regiōnibus
expellere sē posse^[^614]^ sperāre coepit; quāre, conciliīs undique
convocātis, Indōs hortātus est ut sē^[^615]^ fortiter sequerentur atque
hostīs invīsōs ad ūnum interficerent.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Cum iam ad caedem faciendam Indī omnia expedīrent, ē castellō quōdam
mulier forte ēgressa barbarōs in tabernānaculīs arma parāre
animadvertit. Quā rē^[^616]^ nūntiātā, lēgātus Britannicus, quī ibi
praeerat, nihil tamen verēbātur^[^617]^, dōnec puella Inda, quae eum
amābat, castellum maesta intrāvit, cōnsiliumque tōtum Indōrum ostendit.
Tum vērō castellum custōdiīs maiōribus fīrmātum est, nec nimis^[^618]^
mātūrē; nam posterā nocte procul in silvīs audīrī^[^619]^ poterat
cantus^[^620]^
[[]{#c48_A_First_Latin_Reader_48.xhtml_pagename67}]{#c48_A_First_Latin_Reader_48.xhtml_id-57
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/67"}hostium, quī circum
ignēs saltābant: sīc enim Indī sē ad caedem^[^621]^ incitāre solēbant.
:::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
:::

    War.]{.mw-reference-text

    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"

    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"}. This and the following infin. depend
    on **posse**, l. 9. ]{.mw-reference-text

    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"} *could*.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c48_A_First_Latin_Reader_48.xhtml_cite_note-3-n1429}
4.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c48_A_First_Latin_Reader_48.xhtml_cite_ref-4-n1418){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [ **sē:** *him*.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c48_A_First_Latin_Reader_48.xhtml_cite_note-4-n1430}
5.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c48_A_First_Latin_Reader_48.xhtml_cite_ref-5-n1419){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**quā rē:** *this observation*. ]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c48_A_First_Latin_Reader_48.xhtml_cite_note-5-n1431}
6.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c48_A_First_Latin_Reader_48.xhtml_cite_ref-6-n1420){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**nihil … verēbātur:** freely, *felt no concern;* lit. what?
    ]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c48_A_First_Latin_Reader_48.xhtml_cite_note-6-n1432}
7.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c48_A_First_Latin_Reader_48.xhtml_cite_ref-7-n1421){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}

    rendered freely *and none too soon*. ]{.mw-reference-text

    [[**caedem:**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/caedes#Latin "wiktionary:caedes"){.extiw

[]{#c49_A_First_Latin_Reader_49.xhtml}

:::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}
::: {.titulusHeaderBox about="#mwt1"}
:::

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}
:::

::::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
:::::::: text
:::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt27" lang="la"}
[[]{#c49_A_First_Latin_Reader_49.xhtml_pagename67-n1438}]{#c49_A_First_Latin_Reader_49.xhtml_id-57-n1437
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/67" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 49]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*The Attempt to surprise Detroit (Continued)*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Māne ad castellum cum comitibus circiter sexāgintā vēnit Pontiac,
conciliumque postulāvit. Haud magnō intervāllō^[^622]^ sequēbātur
reliqua multitūdō Indōrum, quī simulābant sē extrā mūnītiōnēs
pilā^[^623]^ lūsūrōs^[^624]^.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Portīs castellī patefactīs, Pontiac, quī nihil suspicābātur, ūnā cum
comitibus, quī omnēs^[^625]^ arma vestīmentīs^[^626]^ tēcta ferēbant,
sine morā intrāvit; deinde autem vehementer permōtus mīlitēs omnēs et
complūrēs negōtiātōrēs cum armīs^[^627]^ circumstāre^[^628]^
animadvertit. Postquam vērō ad prīncipia^[^629]^ dēductus est ac vīdit
duōs trēsve tantum adesse centuriōnēs, audācter cum lēgātō loquī coepit.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Priusquam ad castellum perventum est, comitēs rēx monuerat sē, cum
pauca^[^630]^ prius dē pāce locūtus esset, lēgātō zōnam^[^631]^
datūrum^[^632]^; quō sīgnō^[^633]^ impetum statim in lēgātum
centuriōnēsque faciendum esse, cum interim Indī cēterī^[^634]^, quī
extrā mūnitiōnēs relictī erant, per portās inrumperent praesidiumque
adorīrentur.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

::: {about="#mwt4"}
:::

[[]{#c49_A_First_Latin_Reader_49.xhtml_pagename68}]{#c49_A_First_Latin_Reader_49.xhtml_id-58
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/68"}Cum vērō porrigere
zōnam^[^635]^ ille cōnārētur, lēgātus sīgnum dedit^[^636]^, et subitō
prīncipia^[^637]^ sonō armōrum complēta sunt. Tum dēmum barbarī, quī iam
plānē sentiēbant omnia cōnsilia sua patefacta esse, vultū dēmissō ē
castellō silentiō sunt ēgressī, atque in silvās properāvērunt; ubi ē
cōnspectū Britannōrum mox āmissī sunt.

[ ]{about="#mwt21"}
::::::

:::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt32" lang="la"}
[[]{#c50_A_First_Latin_Reader_50.xhtml_pagename68-n1474}]{#c50_A_First_Latin_Reader_50.xhtml_id-58-n1473
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/68" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 50]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*A Successful Ruse*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Colōnī, cum bellum gererent, hostīs saepe fallāciīs^[^638]^ ēlūsērunt.
Sīcut^[^639]^ dux quīdam Americānus, quī mēnsēs multōs cum exercitū
fuerat, uxōris conveniendae causā^[^640]^ ōlim clam domum profectus est.
Cuius adventū cōgnitō, oppidānī^[^641]^, quī paucī^[^642]^ hostibus
favēbant, certiōrem fēcērunt lēgātum Britannicum, quī castrīs
praeerat^[^643]^ proximīs, ducem illum in oppidō latēre.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Itaque sine morā cum legiōne^[^644]^ noctū profectus, lēgātus ad oppidum
celeriter contendit; ubi statim aedibus Americānī^[^645]^ ignēs^[^646]^
admotī sunt. Quō^[^647]^ animadversō, ille scīlicet crēdēbat spem omnem
iam esse sublātam: sed fīlia ex aedibus fortiter ēgressa lēgātō, “Māter
mea,” inquit, “aegra est. Dā mihi, obsecrō^[^648]^, salūtem eius saltem
miserae.”^[^649]^

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

::: {about="#mwt4"}
:::

[[]{#c50_A_First_Latin_Reader_50.xhtml_pagename69}]{#c50_A_First_Latin_Reader_50.xhtml_id-59
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/69" about="#mwt18"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}[Quā rē]{about="#mwt19"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}^[^650]^[ impetrātā, mulier cum lectō lēniter
ēlāta est;]{about="#mwt19"}^[^651]^[ mīlitēs autem, nē dux ipse ullō
modō effugere posset, aedēs interim omnibus ex
partibus]{about="#mwt19"}^[^652]^[ circumstābant quīn etiam haūd procul
sunt morātī, dōnec aedēs tōtae]{about="#mwt19"}^[^653]^[ ignī cōnsūmptae
sunt. Tum laetī ad castra sā recēpērunt, inter
sē]{about="#mwt19"}^[^654]^[ glōriantēs ūnum saltem Americānum
scelerātum poenās dedisse. At incolumis erat ille; nam, cum uxor
efferrētur, sub lectō manibus genibusque]{about="#mwt19"}^[^655]^[
ambulāverat, neque eum vīderat quisquam.]{about="#mwt19"}^[^656]^[ Sīc
astūtiā]{about="#mwt19"}^[^657]^[ fīliae servātus mox ad exercitum tūtō
rediit. ]{about="#mwt19"}
::::::

:::::::::: text
::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt33" lang="la"}
[[]{#c51_A_First_Latin_Reader_51.xhtml_pagename69-n1518}]{#c51_A_First_Latin_Reader_51.xhtml_id-59-n1517
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/69" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 51]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*How the Town was Saved*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Multīs post annīs, quam^[^658]^ ea,^[^659]^ quae modo dīxī, facta sunt,
duae puellae Americānae, quae aliō in oppidō prope mare habitābant,
facinus^[^660]^ memorābile ausae sunt. Ōlim enim, cum pater eārum longē
abesset, in cōnspectum subitō vēnit nāvis longa Britannica; ex quā, cum
in portum pervēnisset, mīlitēs multī scaphīs vectī ad lītus celeriter
contendērunt atque Americānōrum coepērunt incendere nāvigia, quae tum
forte in portū ad ancoram cōnsistēbant.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Fugam iam parābant^[^661]^ oppidānī ceterī; at puellae illae,
[[]{#c51_A_First_Latin_Reader_51.xhtml_pagename71}]{#c51_A_First_Latin_Reader_51.xhtml_id-61
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/71"}tībiā^[^662]^
tympanōque^[^663]^ arreptīs, secundum lītus clam properāvērunt, ac colle
parvō interpositō^[^664]^ clārae^[^665]^ canere coepērunt. Quō sonō
audītō, Britannī vehementer commōtī armātōs plūrimōs appropinquāre
arbitrābantur (nam Americānī multaeque gentēs aliae tībiā
tympanōque^[^666]^ canere solent, cum in proelium prōgrediuntur). Quārē,
veritī nē^[^667]^ interciperentur, hostēs, nāvigiīs oppidānōrum
relictīs, celerrimē sē ad suam^[^668]^ nāvem longam recēpērunt; nam nōn
diūtius de iniūriīs inferendīs^[^669]^ cōgitābant, sed sine morā nāvem
solvērunt ^[^670]^ atque in mare apertum prōgressī sunt. Ita ā puellīs
duābus oppidum servātum est.
:::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}

[ ]{about="#mwt36"}[ ]{about="#mwt36"}

\

[ ]{about="#mwt36"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt36"}
[Musical Instruments]{.smallcaps}
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt36"}

Among the ancients, music was a comparatively undeveloped art. The
scantiness of the music of the stage is indicated by the above scene
from a comedy, where the actor in the foreground is manipulating a
tambourine (*tympanum*), while another in the rear plays upon double
pipes (*tibiae*).

[ ]{about="#mwt36"}

In the Roman army, music was not employed as an accompaniment for the
march; but various trumpets were used for sounding signals. In the
picture below may be seen the long straight trumpet (*tuba*) used by the
infantry.

[ ]{about="#mwt36"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*An Example of Fortitude*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Indī Americānī summum cruciātum sine gemitū patī possunt, atque Indī
Asiāticī nūdī^[^671]^ dīcuntur inter nivēs vītam^[^672]^ agere, neque
ēdere^[^673]^ gemitum, etsī ^[^674]^ ignēs^[^675]^ admoveantur.^[^676]^
Illī tamen cruciātū fortiter ferendō^[^677]^ Rōmānōs nūllō modō
superant. Nam olim, cum diū neque fēlīciter ^[^678]^ bellum cum rēge
[[]{#c52_A_First_Latin_Reader_52.xhtml_pagename72}]{#c52_A_First_Latin_Reader_52.xhtml_id-62
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/72"}Porsinnā^[^679]^
gestum esset, C.^[^680]^ Mūcius, clārus iuvenis Romānus, Tiberim^[^681]^
cōnstituit sōlus trānsīre rēgemque hostium, sī^[^682]^ posset,
interficere. Itaque tēlō veste ^[^683]^ tēctō profectus est; cumque
flūmen clam trānsīsset, in castra hostium incolumis pervenit. Ibi tamen
rēgem a comitibus internōscere^[^684]^ nōn potuit, ac prō Porsinnā
scrībam^[^685]^ occīdit; deinde frūstrā effugere cōnātus ad^[^686]^
rēgem ipsum dēductus est. Quī^[^687]^ cum vellet^[^688]^ penitus^[^689]^
cōgnōscere cōnsilia, quae in ^[^690]^ sē inita erant,^[^691]^ ignēs
iussit admovērī, ut iuvenis omnia^[^692]^ prōdere cōgerētur. Ille autem
ultrō dextram in ignem porrēxit, cruciātumque sine gemitū passus est.
Quō^[^693]^ vīsō rex, tantam fortitūdinem admīrātus, captīvum incolumem
dīmīsit, ac paulō post ā Rōmānīs pācis condiciōnēs petīvit, quod^[^694]^
cum gente, ex quā erant iuvenēs^[^695]^ tantae virtūtis,^[^696]^ diūtius
bellum gerere nōllet.
:::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
:::

    [[**Quī**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/qui#Latin "wiktionary:qui"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"}: *the king*.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c52_A_First_Latin_Reader_52.xhtml_cite_note-17-n1595}
18. [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c52_A_First_Latin_Reader_52.xhtml_cite_ref-18-n1570){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [[**cum
    vellet**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/volo#Latin "wiktionary:volo"){.extiw

::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt31" lang="la"}
[[]{#c53_A_First_Latin_Reader_53.xhtml_pagename72-n1606}]{#c53_A_First_Latin_Reader_53.xhtml_id-62-n1605
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/72" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 53]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*A Hasty Leave-Taking*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Prīmō bellō, ^[^697]^ quod Britannī cum Americānīs gessērunt, per
prōvinciam Noveborācēnsem
[[]{#c53_A_First_Latin_Reader_53.xhtml_pagename73}]{#c53_A_First_Latin_Reader_53.xhtml_id-63
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/73"}ad mare iter facere
cōnābantur, ā sociīs Indīs^[^698]^ multum adiūtī sunt; barbarī enim
paulum ante exercitum prōgressī, villīs undique incēnsīs, colōnōs summā
crūdēlitāte occīdēbant.^[^699]^ Quārē agricolārum omnium suspēnsī erant
animī.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Dum rēs^[^700]^ ita sē habent, in praediō quōdam servus Āfer ōlim subitō
ex hortō perterritus fūgit, dominumque certiōrem fēcit sē Indum in herbā
latentem vīdisse. Quō audītō, dominus statim ad frātris vīllam^[^701]^
profectus est, ut cum eō cōnsilium commūnicāret;^[^702]^ interim uxor
fīlium iussit equōs candrrumque parāre. Tum, postquam rediit pater,
pauca^[^703]^ in carrum imposuērunt, aedibusque ac bōbus^[^704]^
relictīs, ad rīpam flūminis satis^[^705]^ magnī, quod prope fluēbat,
sine morā prōgressī sunt. Id cum trānsissent, celeriter inde per agrōs
contendērunt ūnā cum colōnīs aliīs,^[^706]^ quī in hīs regiōnibus
diūtius morārī nōn audēbant. At nē sīc quidem sine labōribus
perīculīsque effūgērunt; nam in itinere, tempestāte subitō coortā, māter
līberīque sub caelō noctem agere^[^707]^ coāctī sunt: sed postrēmō in
prōvinciam proximam incolumaes pervēnērunt.
:::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}

6.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c53_A_First_Latin_Reader_53.xhtml_cite_ref-6-n1614){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}

::::::: text
::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt35" lang="la"}
[[]{#c54_A_First_Latin_Reader_54.xhtml_pagename73-n1632}]{#c54_A_First_Latin_Reader_54.xhtml_id-63-n1631
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/73" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 54]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*The Capture of a Man-of-War*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Ōlim multī armātī^[^708]^ Americānī ad Canadam versus iter faciēbant, ut
ibi cum Gallīs pugnārent. Quī postrēmō pervēnērunt ad lacum, quī
transeundus erat, sī longius
[[]{#c54_A_First_Latin_Reader_54.xhtml_pagename74}]{#c54_A_First_Latin_Reader_54.xhtml_id-64
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/74"}prōgredī vellent; in
lacū autem ultrō^[^709]^ citrōque nāvis longa Gallica nāvigābat, nē
quis^[^710]^ ibi scaphīs transīre posset.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Americānī scīlicet nāvem longam sibi statim capiendam esse
intellēxērunt. Conciliōque convocātō, cum variae sententiae^[^711]^
dictae essent, subitō lēgātus quīdam, maximae virtūtis vir, imperātōrī
“Ego,” inquit, “sī mihi mīlitēs sex et cuneōs complūrīs dabis, celeriter
rem cōnficiam.” Mīlitibus cuneīsque datīs, lēgātus nocte
intempestā^[^712]^ ad navem longam clam scaphā vectus est; ubi cuneōs
sīc īnseruit,^[^713]^ ut^[^714]^ gubernācula^[^715]^ nūllam in partem
movērī^[^716]^ possent.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Māne Americānī lacum trānsīre coepērunt. Quō animadversō, Gallī, quī
nihil suspicābantur, vēlās passīs^[^717]^ in hostēs impetum facere
cōnātī sunt; at nāvis, ventīs^[^718]^ statim ad lītus delāta, facile
capta est ā quibusdam Americānīs, quī ad id ipsum^[^719]^ in litore
moratī erant. Nāve longa captā, scaphae Americānōrum sine ūllō incommodō
ad lītus ulterius^[^720]^ pervēnērunt, mīlitēsque rursus ad Canadam per
montēs silvāsque lēniter prōgressī sunt.
:::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
:::

::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt37" lang="la"}
[[]{#c55_A_First_Latin_Reader_55.xhtml_pagename74-n1662}]{#c55_A_First_Latin_Reader_55.xhtml_id-64-n1661
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/74" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 55]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*The Fall of New London*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Cum Britannī Novum Eborācum praesidiō tenērent, colōnī classls onustās
rēbus omnibus, quae ad bellum necessāriae sunt, secundum lītus Novae
Britanniae ad
[[]{#c55_A_First_Latin_Reader_55.xhtml_pagename75}]{#c55_A_First_Latin_Reader_55.xhtml_id-65
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/75"}occidentem
nāvigantēs^[^721]^ interdum^[^722]^ vidēbant;^[^723]^ tum, ē portibus
liburnicīs celerrimē vectī, onerāriās capiēbant,^[^724]^ sī quae^[^725]^
forte, tardius prōgressae, intervāllō^[^726]^ maiōre^[^727]^ sequēbantur
nāvēs longās, quae eīs praesidiō^[^728]^ missae erant. Id^[^729]^
Britannī diū molestē tulerant; cumque īnsula Longa iam tōta
subācta^[^730]^ esset, nē posteā umquam^[^731]^ colōnī in nāvēs suās
impetum facere audērent, Novum Londīnium dēlāre cōnstituērunt.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Itaque ab insulā noctū prōfectī, fretum^[^732]^ clam transiērunt; sed
ventīs adversīs impeditī portum non potuērunt intrāre, dōnec diēs
postera illūxit. Tum celeriter ē castellīs sīgnum colōnīs datum est
hostēs adesse, et agricolae armātī omnibus ex partibus in oppidum
convēnērunt. Quī, cum Britannī ē nāvibus ēgressī essent, ad lītus versus
fēcērunt iter, mūrīsque interpositīs tēla plūrima in hostēs inmīsērunt.
At Britannī, quī numerō^[^733]^ erant multō superiōres, mox inrūperunt
in oppidum atque ignēs^[^734]^ undique aedibus templīsque admōverunt.
Quō vīsū, colōnī, ut uxōres līberōsque in loca tūta dēdūcerent, ex
oppidō in agrōs sē recēpērunt.
:::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}

[]{#c56_A_First_Latin_Reader_56.xhtml}

::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}
::: {.titulusHeaderBox about="#mwt1"}

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}

:::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
::::::: text
::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt41" lang="la"}
[[]{#c56_A_First_Latin_Reader_56.xhtml_pagename75-n1694}]{#c56_A_First_Latin_Reader_56.xhtml_id-65-n1693
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/75" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 56]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*The Fall of New London (Continued}*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Prope oppidum erant castra quaedam, quae Americānī praesidiō baud magnō
tenēbant. Quō cum hostēs
[[]{#c56_A_First_Latin_Reader_56.xhtml_pagename76}]{#c56_A_First_Latin_Reader_56.xhtml_id-66
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/76"}pervēnissent,
colōnōs statim sē dēdere iussērunt. Datō autem respōnsō^[^735]^ minimē
grātō, ācerrimē ibi pugnatum est: sed Britannī, quī, ut^[^736]^ suprā
dīxī, numerō multō erant superiōrēs, postrēmō cōnscendērunt mūnitiōnēs,
castraque expugnāvērunt; quīn etiam virtūte colōnōrum, quī animō
obstinātō restiterant, adeō^[^737]^ exacerbātī sunt,^[^738]^ ut summa
crūdelitāte occīderent dēditōs^[^739]^ quōsdam, qui arma iam
prōiēcerant.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Deinde tamen, castra funditus^[^740]^ dēlenda esse arbitrātī,^[^741]^
vulnerātōs prius efferre coepērunt; sed id^[^742]^ tantā saevitiā, ut
hominēs miseriī in carrum alius super alium abicerentur. Tum ā Britannīs
circiter vīgintī carrus dūcī coeptus est^[^743]^ ad vīllam quandam, ubi
vulnerātī ab amīcis cūrārī possent.^[^744]^ At praeceps^[^745]^ erat
via, ac postrēmō ā mīlitibus carrus diūtius retinērī nōn poterat, sed
per dēclīve^[^746]^ celeriter dēlātus,^[^747]^ in arborem inlīsus est.
Ipsa concussiōne^[^748]^ quīdam ē^[^749]^ vulnerātīs interfectī esse
dīcuntur; ac cēterōrum ululātus etiam trāns portum iaudītus est.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Sed iam undique colōnī plūrimī ad oppidum auxilī^[^750]^ ferendī causā
properābant, hostēsque celeriter ad nāvis sē recipere coactī sunt.
:::::

::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}

:::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
::::::: text
::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt36" lang="la"}
[[]{#c57_A_First_Latin_Reader_57.xhtml_pagename77}]{#c57_A_First_Latin_Reader_57.xhtml_id-67
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/77" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 57]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*Captivity among the Indians*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Priusquam prōvinciae Americānae validae sunt factae, Indī oppida
longinqua saepe adoriēbantur;^[^751]^ miseraque erat fortūna eōrum
colōnōrum, quī ab eīs captī sunt. Ē quibus ūnus haec^[^752]^ ferē dē sē
commemorat:^[^753]^

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

“Ōlim,” inquit,^[^754]^ “cum barbarī subitō in conspectum vēnissent, ego
cum oppidānīs cēterīs fugā^[^755]^ petivī salūtem, et in palūdem
proximam quam^[^756]^ celerrimē contendī. Sed in lutō^[^757]^ prōlapsus,
ā tribus Indīs captus sum, atque ūnā cum reliquīs captīvīs in silvās
longē sum dēductus; ubi diēs multōs per montēs summō cum labōre fēcimus
iter, cum interim contumēliās^[^758]^ acerbissimās cotidiē ferre
cōgēbāmur.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

“Noctū hostēs captīvōs humī supīnōs collocābant, cuneīsque in terrā
dēfixīs, manūs pedēsque artē^[^759]^ religābant, nē quis^[^760]^
nostrum^[^761]^ per tenebrās effugere cōnārētur. Interdum autem^[^762]^
tanta erat inopia cibī, ut barbarī, veritī nē^[^763]^ frūmentum
dēficeret, nōs etiam ignī mandāre^[^764]^ semel iterumque^[^765]^ in
animō habērent. At ego, postquam frīgore fameque sum paene necātus,
paucīs post mēnsibus a dominō novō emptus, postrēmō domum incolumis
pervēnī.”
:::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
:::

1.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c57_A_First_Latin_Reader_57.xhtml_cite_ref-1-n1731){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [[**adoriebantur**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/adorio#Latin "wiktionary:adorio"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"}: cf. capiebant,p. 65, l.
    2..]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c57_A_First_Latin_Reader_57.xhtml_cite_note-1-n1746}
2.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c57_A_First_Latin_Reader_57.xhtml_cite_ref-2-n1732){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [[**haec**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/haec#Latin "wiktionary:haec"){.extiw
    .noteref xmlns:epub="http://www.idpf.org/2007/ops"
    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"}: neut. pl..]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c57_A_First_Latin_Reader_57.xhtml_cite_note-2-n1747}
3.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c57_A_First_Latin_Reader_57.xhtml_cite_ref-3-n1733){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**commemorat**: *i.e.* nārrat. The whole phrase may be rendered
    freely *discourses somewhat as follows*, etc..]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c57_A_First_Latin_Reader_57.xhtml_cite_note-3-n1748}
4.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c57_A_First_Latin_Reader_57.xhtml_cite_ref-4-n1734){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**inquit**: present tense.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c57_A_First_Latin_Reader_57.xhtml_cite_note-4-n1749}
5.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c57_A_First_Latin_Reader_57.xhtml_cite_ref-5-n1735){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**fugă**: abl. of means; we would say, “in flight”; cf. other
    renderings of this abl., p. 57, ll. 6 and 8..]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c57_A_First_Latin_Reader_57.xhtml_cite_note-5-n1750}
6.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c57_A_First_Latin_Reader_57.xhtml_cite_ref-6-n1736){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**quam**: cf. p. 47, l. 14..]{.mw-reference-text

7.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c57_A_First_Latin_Reader_57.xhtml_cite_ref-7-n1737){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}

    -ī**](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/lutum#Latin "wiktionary:lutum"){.extiw

    rel="mw:WikiLink/Interwiki"}: [n]{.smallcaps},
    *mud*.]{.mw-reference-text

[]{#c58_A_First_Latin_Reader_58.xhtml}

::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}
::: {.titulusHeaderBox about="#mwt1"}
:::

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}
:::

:::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
::::::: text
::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt31" lang="la"}
[[]{#c58_A_First_Latin_Reader_58.xhtml_pagename78}]{#c58_A_First_Latin_Reader_58.xhtml_id-68
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/78" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 58]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*A Fresh Supply of Powder*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Ōlim puella, quae Elizabēta appellābātur, oppidānīs suīs ita^[^766]^
salūtī^[^767]^ fuit. Subitō ab Indīs oppidum erat oppugnātum,^[^768]^
colōnīque statim sē recēperant in castellum parvum, quod barbarī diū
expugnāre frūstrā cōnātī sunt. At dēficere iam coeperat pulvis ille
paene magicus, quō^[^769]^ celeritātō exitiālī tēla Americānōrum
aliārumque gentium multārum longissimē feruntur. Quārē colōnī vehementer
erant animō dēmissī;^[^770]^ quamquam enim in villā haud longinquā cōpia
pulveris satis magna relicta erat, nēmō eam putābat ūllō modō^[^771]^ ad
castellum tūtō adferri posse, quod Indī in īnsidiīs undique latēbant.
Multī tamen perīculum subīre^[^772]^ volēbant, sed^[^773]^ Elizabēta:
“Ego ībō,” inquit; “puella enim sum, mēque carēreref\>**mē … carēre**:
*spare me,* lit. *be without me*, mē is abl. case..\</ref\> facilius
potestis.”^[^774]^

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Consiliō ā duce probātō, puella mox ē castellō palam ēgressa est,
lēniterque ad villam versus ambulāvit. Quā rē^[^775]^ novā permōtī, Indī
prīmō ēventum tacitī exspectābant, et Elizabēta nūllō impediente^[^776]^
ad vīllam facillimē pervenit; cum autem, pulvere arreptō, ad castellum
rursus celeriter currere coepisset, tum barbarī, quī iam sē ēlūsōs
sentiēbant, tēla plūrima undique coniēcērunt. Sed puella fortis sine
[[]{#c58_A_First_Latin_Reader_58.xhtml_pagename79}]{#c58_A_First_Latin_Reader_58.xhtml_id-69
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/79"}vulnere intrā portam
castellī recepta est, colōnīque pulvere sublevatī impetūs Indōrum
potuērunt sustinēre, dōnec amīcī auxilī ferendī causā ex oppidīs
fīnitimīs frequentēs convēnērunt.
:::::

[]{#c59_A_First_Latin_Reader_59.xhtml}

::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}
::: {.titulusHeaderBox about="#mwt1"}
:::

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}
:::

:::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
::::::: text
::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt9" lang="la"}
[[]{#c59_A_First_Latin_Reader_59.xhtml_pagename79-n1788}]{#c59_A_First_Latin_Reader_59.xhtml_id-69-n1787
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/79" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 59]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*A Battle against Great Odds*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

In quōdam lacū maximō, cuius in lītore positum est oppidum Taeconderoga,
ācriter quondam ab Americānīs cum Britannis pugnātum est. Americānīs
parvae erant nāvēs et paucae; at dux Britannicus, quī facile ē Canadā
cōpiās adferre poterat, multās nāvēs longās summā diligentiā īnstrūctās
parāverat; sē enim Taeconderōgam brevī expugnātūrum spērābat.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Imperātor tamen colōnōrum, vir maximae virtūtis, etsī numerō erat multō
īnferior, committere proelium minimē dubitāvit; sed cum hōrās multās
esset pugnātum noxque iam adesset, nāvēs vix nābant Americānae, tēlaque
paene dēfēcerant. Quō quidem tempore Britannī, noctem veritī, proeliō
dēstitērunt; sed ad ancoram haud procul cōnsistēbant, nē colōnī per
tenebrās effugere cōnārentur.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

At Americānī nocte intempestā, lucernls extīnctīs, silentiō dedērunt
vēla, et magnō circuitū hostēs vītāvērunt. Itaque māne, cum Britannī
proelium redintegrāre vellent, vix in cōnspectū erat nāvis ūlla; quārē
illī, ancorīs sublātīs, summā celeritāte īnsequī coepērunt. Postquam
autem Americānōs fugientēs paene adsecūtī sunt, cōnstitit ea
[[]{#c59_A_First_Latin_Reader_59.xhtml_pagename80}]{#c59_A_First_Latin_Reader_59.xhtml_id-70
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/80"}nāvis, quā vehēbātur
dux ipse colōnōrum, et sōla hostium sustinuit impetum, dōnec reliqua
classis Americāna in portum mūnītum pervenīre potuit; quīn etiam nē
illam quidem praedam cēpērunt Britannī; nam suō nāvigiō, cum ad lītus
appulsum esset, AmericānI ipsī ignīs admōvērunt.
:::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
:::
:::::::
::::::::
:::::::::::

[]{#c60_A_First_Latin_Reader_60.xhtml}

::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}
::: {.titulusHeaderBox about="#mwt1"}
:::

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}
:::

:::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
::::::: text
::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt9" lang="la"}
[[]{#c60_A_First_Latin_Reader_60.xhtml_pagename80-n1792}]{#c60_A_First_Latin_Reader_60.xhtml_id-70-n1791
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/80" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 60]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*A Night Attack*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Bellō prīmō, quod ā Britannīs cum Americānīs gestum est, in flūmine
quodam Carolaenae Ulteriōris īnsula parva praesidiō Britannicō tenēbātur
interim dominus insulae, vir locuplēs reīque pūblicae amantissimus,
molestē scīlicet ferēbat castra hostium in praediō suō collocāta esse,
eō magis quod mīlitēs interdum sē īnsolenter gerēbant.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Postrēmō Americānī cōnstituērunt adversō flūmine nāvigāre cōpiāsque
Britannicās, sī possent, ex īnsulā expellere. Itaque clam profectī,
nāvibus nocte intempestā ad īnsulam silentiō appulsīs, impetum ācerrimum
subitō fēcērunt. Quā rē novā permōtī Britannī ad arma celeriter
cucurrērunt; et dominus quoque īnsulae, quī nesciēbat amīcōs adesse,
impetum ab hostibus factum arbitrātus, ūnā cum uxōre līberīsque in
silvās tardius sē contulit; ipse enim pedibus
[[]{#c60_A_First_Latin_Reader_60.xhtml_pagename81}]{#c60_A_First_Latin_Reader_60.xhtml_id-71
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/81"}captus ā servīs tum
sellā ferēbātur. Ubi sīc ad casam longinquam perventum est, māter subitō
clāmāvit puerum īnfantem in aedibus relictum esse. Quō audītō, fīlia
fortiter per tenebrās profecta celeriter domum cucurrit; cumque inter
tēla amicōrum et hostium in aedēs pervēnisset, puerum ē cūnīs rapuit
incolumemque ad matrem secum redūxit.
:::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
:::
:::::::
::::::::
:::::::::::

[]{#c61_A_First_Latin_Reader_61.xhtml}

::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}
::: {.titulusHeaderBox about="#mwt1"}
:::

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}
:::

:::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
::::::: text
::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt9" lang="la"}
[[]{#c61_A_First_Latin_Reader_61.xhtml_pagename81-n1796}]{#c61_A_First_Latin_Reader_61.xhtml_id-71-n1795
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/81" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 61]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*A Choice of Evils*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Parvō in oppidō Novae Britanniae habitābat quīdam agricola, cui erant
līberī octō. Is ōlim, cum subitō nuntiātum esset Indōs appropinquāre, ex
agrīs ad bona līberōsque servandos summā celeritāte properāvit; aegra
enim domī uxor iacēbat.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Quō igitur cum pervēnisset, līberīs convocātis atque ad castellum
proximum statim praemissīs, ipse uxōrem ad iter parāre cōnātus est. Sed
iam in cōnspectū erant Indī, neque diūtius ūlla erat salūtis spēs.
Itaque uxōre bonīsque relictīs, agricola, quī iam anteā statuerat cum
līberis sibi vīvendum aut prō eīs moriendum esse, equum cōnscendit,
atque ad castellum versus quam celerrimē contendit. Līberōs mox
adsecūtus est, et omnēs, etsī Indī vestīgiīs sequēbantur, in castellum
incolumēs pervēnērunt; nam
[[]{#c61_A_First_Latin_Reader_61.xhtml_pagename82}]{#c61_A_First_Latin_Reader_61.xhtml_id-72
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/82"}quotiēns propius
accesserant barbarī, pater cōnsistēbat in viā, eōsque armīs terrēbat.
Sed interim uxor aegra, mulier magnae fortitūdinis, ūnā cum captivīs
aliīs ab Indīs in silvās dēdūcēbātur.
:::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
:::
:::::::
::::::::
:::::::::::

[]{#c62_A_First_Latin_Reader_62.xhtml}

::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}
::: {.titulusHeaderBox about="#mwt1"}
:::

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}
:::

:::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
::::::: text
::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt9" lang="la"}
[[]{#c62_A_First_Latin_Reader_62.xhtml_pagename82-n1800}]{#c62_A_First_Latin_Reader_62.xhtml_id-72-n1799
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/82" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 62]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*Lost in the Woods*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Multōs abhinc annōs quīdam puer parvus mātre īnsciente in silvam clam
profectus, diū ibi sēcum sub arboribus lūsit. Quī, cum iam
advesperāsceret, viam reperīre nōn potuit ac brevī intellēxit sub caelō
sibi noctem agendam esse. Itaque ex foliīs lectum fēcit, cumque per
arborēs lūnam stellāsque aliquamdiū suspēxisset, postrēmō somnō
gravissimō quiēvit. Māne iterum viam invenīre frūstrā cōnātus, famem
bācīs sustinuit; quō modō quīnque diēs per silvās errāvit. Deinde noctū
ignem animadvertit, et celeriter prōgressus in vīcum Indōrum subitō
pervēnit. Ā quibus cōmiter acceptus, multōs diēs ibi morātus est.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Dum haec fīunt, lēgātus prōvinciae ūnā cum comitibus paucīs puerī
quaerendī causā in scaphā profectus erat, oppidaque Indōrum finitima
adībat omnia. Quae rēs puerō salūtī fuit; nam postremō repertī sunt
quīdam barbarī, quī nūntiāvērunt ipsum incolumem esse viamque
[[]{#c62_A_First_Latin_Reader_62.xhtml_pagename83}]{#c62_A_First_Latin_Reader_62.xhtml_id-73
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/83"}ostenderunt.Puerō
sīc receptō, lēgātus sīcās dedit eīs Indīs, ā quibus ille servatus erat.
Barbarī scīlicet dōnīs tam grātīs gaudēbant, puer autem domum reductus
est.
:::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
:::
:::::::
::::::::
:::::::::::

[]{#c63_A_First_Latin_Reader_63.xhtml}

::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}
::: {.titulusHeaderBox about="#mwt1"}
:::

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}
:::

:::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
::::::: text
::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt9" lang="la"}
[[]{#c63_A_First_Latin_Reader_63.xhtml_pagename83-n1804}]{#c63_A_First_Latin_Reader_63.xhtml_id-73-n1803
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/83" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 63]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*The Battle of Saratoga*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Saepe prō patriā fortissimē pugnāvit iste Arnoldius, quī posteā
Britannīs prōdere cōnātus est ea castra mūnītissima, quae in rīpā
flūminis Hudsōnis posita sunt: et nōn numquam etiam salūtī cīvibus suīs
fuit; tantopere enim ā mīlitibus amābātur, ut ipsō adventū suō ad
victōriam eōs incitāre posset.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Ōlim Saratōgae, cum eius ōrdinem adēmisset imperātor, quōcum simultātem
gerēbat, ille, sonō proeliī ad aurēs adlātō, “Ego,” inquit, “si dux esse
nōn possum, at saltem manipulāris erō;’ quae cum dīxisset, iniussū
imperātōris equum cōnscendit celerrimēque in proelium vectus est: ubi
mīlitēs, duce vetere cōgnitō, clāmōre sublātō laetī secūtī sunt, atque
impetum ācerrimē fēcērunt in eam partem, ubi aciēs hostium cōnfertissima
vīsa est. Ibi summā virtūte pugnāns Arnoldius est vulnerātus, victōria
autem ab Americānīs parta est.
[[]{#c63_A_First_Latin_Reader_63.xhtml_pagename84}]{#c63_A_First_Latin_Reader_63.xhtml_id-74
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/84"}Etsī vulnera Arnoldī
nōn erant exitiālia, tempus tamen mortī opportūnissimum erat. Odium enim
perfidiae, quā ille posteā ūsus est, glōriam eius rērum gestārum semper
obruet; quīn etiam trāditum est (ut suprā commemorāvī) nē Britannōs
quidem, quī eius perfidiā victōriam sē nactūrōs spērāverant, hominem
ūllō in honōre habuisse, postquam bellum confectum esset.
:::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
:::
:::::::
::::::::
:::::::::::

[]{#c64_A_First_Latin_Reader_64.xhtml}

::::::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}
::: {.titulusHeaderBox about="#mwt1"}
:::

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}
:::

:::::::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
::::::::::: text
::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt9" lang="la"}
[[]{#c64_A_First_Latin_Reader_64.xhtml_pagename84-n1808}]{#c64_A_First_Latin_Reader_64.xhtml_id-74-n1807
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/84" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 64]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*Unwelcome Visitors*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Britannī, cum iam iterum cum Americānīs gererent bellum pugnīsque
nāvālībus saepe victī essent, postrēmō cōnstituērunt usque ad Lovīsiānam
classem mittere, sī ibi fēlīcius rem gerere possent. Quārē appulsīs
nāvibus ad eum locum, ubi in mare fertur flūmen maximum, quem Indī
patrem aquārum vocābant, mīlitēs multī in lītus ēgressī praedia fīnitima
explōrāre coepērunt.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Sīc factum est ut quīdam adulēscēns Americānus, quī in vīllā ōtiōsus
hōrā dīeī ferē quārtā morābātur, mīlitēs complūrīs in hortō latentēs
subitō animadverteret. Quā rē novā graviter commōtus, comitēs ut sine
mora latebrās
[[]{#c64_A_First_Latin_Reader_64.xhtml_pagename86}]{#c64_A_First_Latin_Reader_64.xhtml_id-76
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/86"}quaererent hortātus
est, et ipse prīmō fugā salūtem petīvit; sed ab hostibus statim
circumventus, sē dēdere tum nōn dubitāvit. At paulō post fenestrā
patefactā ērūpit, cumque tēla hostium undique in eum conicerentur,
incolumis pervēnit in palūdem, ubi BritannI armīs impedītī summō labōre
sequēbantur.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Itaque iuvenis, cum dēmum ab hostibus intervallō satis magno abesset,
arborem nactus idōneam in quā latēret, celeriter conscendit. Brevī autem
sonum exiguum sub arbore audīvit; cumque dēspēxisset, ibi vīdit canem,
quam maximē amābat. Quārē perīculum veritus, comitem fidēlem, quae per
palūdem dominum secūta erat, invītus necāvit, multīsque cum lacrimīs sub
foliīs tēxit. Deinde aliquamdiū tacitus in arbore morātus est; postquam
autem Britannī quaerendō dēfessī ad vīllam sē recēpērunt, magnō circuitū
custōdiās hostium vītāvit, eōrumque dē adventū certiōrem fēcit
imperātōrem Americānum, quī oppidum haud longinquum praesidiō tum
tenēbat.
:::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}

.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/85" about="#mwt11"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

[]{.mw-empty-elt about="#mwt12"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt12"}
[Canis]{.smallcaps}
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt12"}

Just inside the street door of a Pompeian house is found worked into the
mosaic of the pavement this representation of a watchdog. The words
*Cavē canem* signify “Beware of the dog.”

[ ]{about="#mwt12"}

[]{.mw-empty-elt about="#mwt12"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt12"}
[Horae]{.smallcaps}
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt12"}

The Romans divided the time between sunrise and sunset into twelve equal
hours[[——]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}long
in summer, and short in winter. Above is shown a sundial to mark the
time in the great used public baths at Pompeii.
:::::

[]{#c65_A_First_Latin_Reader_65.xhtml}

::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}
::: {.titulusHeaderBox about="#mwt1"}
:::

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}
:::

:::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
::::::: text
::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt9" lang="la"}
[[]{#c65_A_First_Latin_Reader_65.xhtml_pagename86-n1814}]{#c65_A_First_Latin_Reader_65.xhtml_id-76-n1813
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/86" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 65]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*The Boyhood of Daniel Boone*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Abhinc annōs circiter ducentōs in Pennsylvēniā nātus est puer, quī
posteā factus est explōrātor clārissimus. Quīn etiam ā prīmā pueritiā
ille arma ferre cōnsuēverat, ac in
[[]{#c65_A_First_Latin_Reader_65.xhtml_pagename87}]{#c65_A_First_Latin_Reader_65.xhtml_id-77
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/87"}silvīs ambulāns
ferās saepe occīdit. Ōlim, cum vespere prīmō domum nōn redīsset, vīcīnī,
veritī nē puer ab Indīs aut ferīs esset interfectus, frequentēs
convēnērunt, complūrīsque diēs errāvērunt per silvās, sī ūllō modō eum
invenīre possent; quī postrēmō pervēnērunt ad casam rāmīs caespitibusque
aedificātam ā puerō ipsō, quī frūstum carnīs in ignem porrigēns humī
sine timōre sōlus sedēbat. Nam ē viā nōn errāverat sed cōnsultō sē
longius contulerat in silvās, quod procul ab oppidīs sine comitibus
etiam tum libenter habitābat.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Paucūs post annīs pater multa mīlia passuum ad loca longinqua cōnstituit
in silvās ēmigrāre, quod ipsī quoque urbēs oppidaque minimē grāta erant.
Quās ad sēdēs novās ubi perventum est, puer, cum pater frātrēsque
arborēs exiscīderent agrōsque ad satūs accipiendōs parārent, ferīs
interfectīs carnem ē silvā cotldiē domum reportābat. Interdum noctū
quoque vēnātus esse dicitur: quō quidem tempore facibus ārdentibus ūtī
solēbat; lūmina enim, ut saepe ab explōrātōribus audīvimus, ad ferās ē
latebrīs ēliciendīs magnō ūsuī sunt.
:::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
:::

:::::::::::

[]{#c66_A_First_Latin_Reader_66.xhtml}

::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}
::: {.titulusHeaderBox about="#mwt1"}
:::

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}
:::

:::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
::::::: text
::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt9" lang="la"}
[[]{#c66_A_First_Latin_Reader_66.xhtml_pagename88}]{#c66_A_First_Latin_Reader_66.xhtml_id-78
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/88" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 66]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*The End of the Pequots*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Nātiō Indōrum crūdēlissima, quae haud procul ā Novō Londīniō habitābat,
quondam īnsidiās collocāre ac colōnōs singulōs undique interficere
subitō coepit. Quibus rēbus nūntiātīs, ē prōvinciā proximā manus exigua
missa est, quae agricolīs auxiliō esset poenāsque ab Indīs repeteret. At
mīlitēs longē ā lītore prōgredī nōn audēbant; quī igitur, parvō frūmentī
numerō dīreptō tabernāculīsque paucīs incēnsis, ē fīnibus hostium brevī
domum sē recēpērunt. Barbarī vērō, hāc iniūriā graviter permōtī,
incendia ac caedēs undique etiam crūdēlius iam miscuērunt.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Tum dēnique ē prōvinciā missa est classis, cuius praefectus iussus erat
mīlitēs expōnere in quōdam portū parvō, quī haud longē ā castrīs Indōrum
aberat. Ille autem, hostēs ita cōnsilium suum facile cōgnōscere posse
arbitrātus, praeter ilium portum nāvigāvit, cumque classis ē cōnspectū
barbarōrum longē discessisset, tum dēmum nāvēs ad lītus appulit. Deinde
in terram ēgressus, sine morā per silvās viā deviā cum exercitū
profectus est, ut ā tergō hostēs adorīrētur. In itinere quāsdam Indōrum
nātiōnēs fīnitimās adiit, ē quibus multī armātī operam suam pollicitī
sunt.
[[]{#c66_A_First_Latin_Reader_66.xhtml_pagename89}]{#c66_A_First_Latin_Reader_66.xhtml_id-79
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/89"}Sīc postrēmō
perventum est ad sēdēs hostium, quī, ratī propter timōrem colōnōs
praetervectōs esse, iam minus dīligenter castra sua custōdiēbant.
:::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
:::
:::::::
::::::::
:::::::::::

[]{#c67_A_First_Latin_Reader_67.xhtml}

::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}
::: {.titulusHeaderBox about="#mwt1"}
:::

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}
:::

:::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
::::::: text
::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt9" lang="la"}
[[]{#c67_A_First_Latin_Reader_67.xhtml_pagename89-n1822}]{#c67_A_First_Latin_Reader_67.xhtml_id-79-n1821
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/89" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 67]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*The End of the Pequots (Continued)*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Noctū castris appropinquāvērunt colōnī. Intus erant uxōrēs quoque
līberīque Indōrum, intusque audīrī poterat cantus barbarōrum, quī,
circum ignīs saltantēs, victōriās superiōrēs celebrābant. Colōnī
aliquamdiū tacitī exspectāvērunt; tum, cum diēs iam illūcēsceret Indīque
saltandō dēfessī somnō quiēscerent gravī, subitō in castrā portīs duābus
inrūpērunt.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Quō impetū repentīnō commōtī, hostēs tamen celeriter ē lectīs
exsiluērunt, tabernāculīsque interpositīs, tēla in mīlitēs conicere
fortiter coepērunt plūrima. Quō animadversō, dux colōnōrum statim
intellēxit cōnsilium sibi mūtandum esse, suōsque tabernāculis ignēs
admovēre iussit, deinde celeriter ēgressōs undique castra circumstāre.
Quō modō Indī miserī, ignl ē castrīs fugere coāctī, ā colōnīs paene ad
ūnum interfectī sunt; et sī quī forte aciem perrūperant, eōs sociī Indī
libenter occīdērunt.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

In proeliō multī quoque ē colōnīs sunt vulnerātī, atque exercitus statim
Novum Londīnium sē recipere coāctus est;
[[]{#c67_A_First_Latin_Reader_67.xhtml_pagename90}]{#c67_A_First_Latin_Reader_67.xhtml_id-80
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/90"}quō, ut iussum erat,
nāvēs iam redierant, ut ibi ducem mīlitēsque exspectārent. Sed hostēs
paucīs post mēnsibus alterā pugnā victī sunt, neque umquam posteā
iniūriam ūllam colōnīs facere potuērunt; quīn etiam brevī in manūs
parvās divīsī, aliī in aliam nātiōnem ascitī sunt.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}
:::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
:::
:::::::
::::::::
:::::::::::

[]{#c68_A_First_Latin_Reader_68.xhtml}

::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}
::: {.titulusHeaderBox about="#mwt1"}
:::

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}
:::

:::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
::::::: text
::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt9" lang="la"}
[[]{#c68_A_First_Latin_Reader_68.xhtml_pagename90-n1826}]{#c68_A_First_Latin_Reader_68.xhtml_id-80-n1825
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/90" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 68]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*A Difficult Escape*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Quondam puerī duo sine timōre in agrīs apertīs cotīdiē laborābant; nam,
etsī colōnī tum bellum cum Gallīs Indīsque gerēbant, in hīs regiōnibus
nēmō barbarōs ūllōs nuper viderat. Sed ōlim duo Indī subitō ex arboribus
ērūperunt proximīs, puerīsque arreptīs sē celerrimē in silvam
recēpērunt. Quā rē novā perterritus puer minor flēre coepit; sed alter,
quī plānē sentiēbat flētum nihil prōfutūrum esse, frātrem hortātus est
ut sē fortiter gereret. Per silvam ūnā cum captīvīs iam properābant
barbarī. Quī, postquam sic diēs multōs iter fecērunt, ad lacum
pervēnērunt longinquum, ubi cum aliīs cīvibus suīs hiemāre
cōnstituerant.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Ibi dum morantur, linguam barbarōrum discere coepērunt puerī. Quō modō
maior prīmā aestāte repperit Indōs in animō habēre in Canadam dūcere
captīvōs, eōsque ibi in
[[]{#c68_A_First_Latin_Reader_68.xhtml_pagename91}]{#c68_A_First_Latin_Reader_68.xhtml_id-81
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/91"}servitūtem Gallīs
vēndere. Quārē, cibō armīsque arreptīs, frātres duo ex hībernīs noctū
clam fūgērunt; ubi autem diēs illūxit, in arbore cavā sē somnō dedērunt.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Interim Indī cum canibus undique puerōs quaerēbant. At frāter maior, cum
canēs propius ad arborem accessissent, ē somnō lātrātū excitātus,
callidō ūsus cōnsiliō frūstum carnis eīs prōiēcit. Quae rēs puerīs
salūtī fuit; cum enim canēs carnem dēvorārent, barbarī nihil suspicantēs
arborem praeteriērunt. Quō vīsō, puerī rursus profectī per silvās
errāvērunt, dōnec fame labōribusque paene cōnfectī sunt; tum in quoddam
oppidum colōnōrum sibi anteā īgnōtum subitō pervēnērunt.
:::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
:::

[]{#c69_A_First_Latin_Reader_69.xhtml}

::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}

:::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
::::::: text
::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt9" lang="la"}
[[]{#c69_A_First_Latin_Reader_69.xhtml_pagename91-n1830}]{#c69_A_First_Latin_Reader_69.xhtml_id-81-n1829
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/91" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 69]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*Stories about Daniel Boone*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Ille explōrātor clārus, cuius dē pueritiā paulō ante dīxī, Indōsque
paene tōtam ēgit aetātem. Ōlim ē inter feras Carolaenā Citeriōre trāns
montēs ūnā cum aliīs explōrātōribus quīnque audācter in vallēs
longinquās contendit; ubi ūnō cum comite ab Indīs captus, postquam ab
eīs septem diēs summā diligentiā custōdītus est, noctū clam surrēxit,
comiteque ē somnō excitātō, incolumis ad casam pervēnit, quam ipse
cēterīque explōrātōrēs paulō ante fēcerant.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Paucīs post annīs eāsdem in regiōnēs colōnōs cum
[[]{#c69_A_First_Latin_Reader_69.xhtml_pagename92}]{#c69_A_First_Latin_Reader_69.xhtml_id-82
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/92"}uxōribus līberīsque
dēdūxit ad locum, quī castellō maximē idōneus vidēbātur. Ubi aliquamdiū
fortūnā prōsperā ūsus est; sed quondam eius fīlia, quae errābat in
agrīs, ut flōrēs carperet, ūnā cum puellīs aliīs ab Indīs capta, in
silvās complūra mīlia passuum ducta est. Dum autem iter faciunt, puellae
prūdentēs omnibus locīs aut rāmōs frēgērunt parvōs aut humī pannōs
rellquērunt quae rēs magnō ūsuī erat patribus īrātīs, quī haud longō
intervāllō vestigiīs īnsequēbantur. Barbarīs victīs, puellae laetae
domum reductae sunt.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Paulō post ille explōrātor ipse iterum captus, diū apud Indōs vīvere
coactus est. Sed postrēmō, cum per aquam prōfluentem cucurrisset, nē
vestigia ūlla faceret, ad amicōs incolumis pervēnit. Multīs autem ante
mēnsibus uxor līberīque, patrem iam prīdem mortuum ratī, ad propinquōs
suōs in Carolaenam Citeriōrem maestī sē recēperant.
:::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
:::

::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}
::: {.titulusHeaderBox about="#mwt1"}
:::

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}
:::

:::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
::::::: text
::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt9" lang="la"}
[[]{#c70_A_First_Latin_Reader_70.xhtml_pagename92-n1834}]{#c70_A_First_Latin_Reader_70.xhtml_id-82-n1833
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/92" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 70]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*An English Privateer*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Abhinc multōs annōs, etsī illō ipsō tempore bellum iūstum cum Hispānīs
non gerēbātur, quīdam praefectus Britannicus per maria nāvigābat omnia,
gazamque ac nāvēs Hispānōrum omnibus locīs spoliābat; itaque accidit ut,
cum
[[]{#c70_A_First_Latin_Reader_70.xhtml_pagename93}]{#c70_A_First_Latin_Reader_70.xhtml_id-83
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/93"}secundum lītus
Americae Ulteriōris navigāret, urbēs illīus regiōnis adīret multās,
incolāsque magnam vim aurī argentīque trādere cogeret.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Līmae duodecim nāvigia in portū ad ancoram consistēbant; quae cum ille
spoliāret, certior factus aliam nāvem gazā onustam haud procul abesse,
praedā ē duodecim nāvigiīs cōnfēstim in suum receptā, ē portū statim
solvit, summāque celeritāte coepit īnsequī; dīvitiās enim etiam maiōrēs
sē iam captūrum spērābat.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Mox in conspectū erat nāvis fugiēns; quae nūllō modō ēvādere potuit, cum
Britannī celeritāte tantopere superābant. Nāve trāditā, dīvitiae maximae
intus repertae sunt; quin etiam gubernātor ipse duo pōcula argentea
habuisse dīcitur. Quae cum praefectus vīdisset, gubernātōrī, “Duo pōcula
tū habēs," inquit; “alterum mihi dandum est." Tum gubernātor miser, quī
omnia trādenda planē intellegēbat, invītus praefectō in manūs pōcula
trādidit ambō.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}
:::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}

[]{#c71_A_First_Latin_Reader_71.xhtml}

:::::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}
::: {.titulusHeaderBox about="#mwt1"}
:::

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}
:::

::::::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
:::::::::: text
::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt12" lang="la"}
[[]{#c71_A_First_Latin_Reader_71.xhtml_pagename93-n1838}]{#c71_A_First_Latin_Reader_71.xhtml_id-83-n1837
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/93" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 71]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*A Roman Vandal*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

\
Quibus rebus admoneor ut dē pessimīs facinoribus Verris, hominis planē
scelerātī, pauca nunc dicam. Nam ille,
[[]{#c71_A_First_Latin_Reader_71.xhtml_pagename95}]{#c71_A_First_Latin_Reader_71.xhtml_id-85
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/95"}cum praetor in
Siciliā esset, omnibus locīs oppida templaque spoliāvit quīn etiam
tantae erat avāritiae, ut nē pauperrimī quidem Siculī bona vidēre
posset, quīn statim ea possidēre vellet. Interdum autem ā suīs comitibus
est ēlūsus.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Sicut memoriae trāditum est eum ōlim certiōrem factum cuidam Siculō esse
duo pōcula argentea; quō audītō, etsī aedēs eiusdem hominis nūper
spoliātae erant, nūntium statim mīsit, quī pōcula ad sē sine morā
dēferrī iubēret. Siculus igitur, veritus nē sibi malum accideret maius,
cōnfestim cum pōculīs ad praetōrem profectus est. Quō ubi pervēnit,
praetor forte iam quiescēbat; sed ante forēs ambulābant quidam ex ipsīus
amīcīs, hominēs improbī, quōrum tamen cōnsiliō ille multum ūtī
cōnsuēverat: quī Siculō statim, “Ubi sunt pōcula?" inquiunt. Tum homō
miser primō querī coepit bona omnia sibi ēripī, deinde eōs vehementer
hortātus est ut sibi auxiliō essent. Quō audītō, illī “Quantum nobis
dabis,” inquiunt, "si pōcula tibi nōn eripientur?" Tum Siculus spē
ērēctus, praemium satis
[[]{#c71_A_First_Latin_Reader_71.xhtml_pagename96}]{#c71_A_First_Latin_Reader_71.xhtml_id-86
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/96"}magnum pollicitus
est, pōculaque brevī domum laetus reportāvit comitēs enim praetōris, cum
ille ē somnō experrectus esset, audācī mendāciō ūsī nōn dubitāvērunt
cōnfīrmāre pōcula sibi nōn digna vidērī, quae in eius mēnsā pōnerentur.
:::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
:::

.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/94" about="#mwt14"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

[]{.mw-empty-elt about="#mwt15"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt15"}
[Forēs]{.smallcaps}
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt15"}

These remnants of a house door serve to show why the word for “door” is
plural in Latin. Roman house doors were arranged almost always to open
inward rather than outward; on the inside there was a more or less
primitive lock or bolt, and sometimes a bar too was used.
::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
