:::::::::::::

[]{#c102_A_First_Latin_Reader_102.xhtml}

::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}
::: {.titulusHeaderBox about="#mwt1"}
:::

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}
:::

:::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
::::::: text
::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt9" lang="la"}
[[]{#c102_A_First_Latin_Reader_102.xhtml_pagename135-n1970}]{#c102_A_First_Latin_Reader_102.xhtml_id-125-n1969
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/135" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 102]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*A Parley with the Enemy*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Ad colloquium missus est C.[ ]{typeof="mw:Entity"}Arpinēius, eques
Rōmānus, et Q.[ ]{typeof="mw:Entity"}Iūnius, Hispāniēnsis, quī iam ante
ā Caesare ipsō saepe dēlēctus erat, ut cum Ambiorīge ageret.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Eīs, cum extrā mūnītiōnēs ēgressī essent, rēx cōnfīrmāvit Gallōs
ūniversōs cōnstituisse eō ipsō diē omnia hīberna Caesaris simul
oppugnāre, nē quā legiō alterī legiōnī
[[]{#c102_A_First_Latin_Reader_102.xhtml_pagename136}]{#c102_A_First_Latin_Reader_102.xhtml_id-126
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/136"}subsidiō venīre
posset; sē tamen invītum castra oppugnāsse, sed voluntātī cēterōrum
Gallōrum cīvitātem suam resistere nōn potuisse. “Nec tamen,” inquit,
“Caesaris in mē beneficiōrum immemor sum; itaque vōs magnopere hortor,
ut quam celerrimē exercitum vestrum ad proxima hīberna dēdūcātis. Magna
enim manus Germānōrum Rhēnum nuper trānsiit, quōrum multitūdinī nūllō
modō resistere poteritis. Quārē salūtī vestrae statim cōnsulite.” Simul
pollicitus est sē Rōmānōs per fīnis suōs incolumēs iter facere passūrum.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Quā ōrātiōne habita, discessit Ambiorīx; nūntiī autem rediērunt in
castra lēgātōsque dē rēgis verbīs cērtiōrēs fēcērunt.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}
:::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
:::
:::::::
::::::::
:::::::::::

[]{#c103_A_First_Latin_Reader_103.xhtml}

::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}
::: {.titulusHeaderBox about="#mwt1"}
:::

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}
:::

:::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
::::::: text
::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt9" lang="la"}
[[]{#c103_A_First_Latin_Reader_103.xhtml_pagename136-n1974}]{#c103_A_First_Latin_Reader_103.xhtml_id-126-n1973
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/136" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 103]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*Division of Opinion in the Roman Camp*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Q. Sabinus et L. Cotta lēgātī, rē repentīnā permōtī, ea verba, etsī ab
hoste dicta erant, tamen nōn neglegenda esse exīstimābant itaque,
cōnsiliō convocātō, quid optimum factū esset diū disputātum est.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Tribūnī centuriōnēsque complūrēs nihil sibi temerē
[[]{#c103_A_First_Latin_Reader_103.xhtml_pagename137}]{#c103_A_First_Latin_Reader_103.xhtml_id-127
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/137"}agendum, neque ex
hībernīs iniussū Caesaris discēdendum iūdicābant; cum enim castra
mūnitissima essent, crēdēbant sē Germānīs facīle resistere posse, dōnec
Caesar cum legiōnibus subsidiō veniret. Sabīnus autem, veritus nē Gallī
cum Germānīs sē coniungerent, statim discēdendum cēnsuit; aciēbat enim
Germānīs magnō dolōrī fuisse victōriās superiōrēs Rōmānōrum, neque
arbitrābātur Gallōs, quī tot contumēliās ā Rōmānīs accēperant, sē cum
hoste quōvīs coniungere dubitātūrōs.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Ōrātiōne in utramque partem habitā, cum Cotta sententiae collēgae suī
ācriter resisteret, Sabīnus postrēmō īratus “Fīat,” inquit, “ut vōbīs
vidētur; ego nōn is sum, quī mortis perīculō magnopere terrear.”
:::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
:::
:::::::
::::::::
:::::::::::

[]{#c104_A_First_Latin_Reader_104.xhtml}

::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}
::: {.titulusHeaderBox about="#mwt1"}
:::

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}
:::

:::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
::::::: text
::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt9" lang="la"}
[[]{#c104_A_First_Latin_Reader_104.xhtml_pagename137-n1978}]{#c104_A_First_Latin_Reader_104.xhtml_id-127-n1977
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/137" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 104]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*The Advice of the Enemy is Taken*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Quibus verbīs commōtī, omnēs statim ē consiliō surrēxērunt, lēgātōsque
vehementer hortātī sunt nē suā pertināciā rem in summum perīculum
dēdēcerent: neque enim ūllum
[[]{#c104_A_First_Latin_Reader_104.xhtml_pagename138}]{#c104_A_First_Latin_Reader_104.xhtml_id-128
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/138"}hostem sibi
timendum esse, sī modō omnēs idem probārent; in dissēnsiōne autem nūllam
esse spem.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Cum iam ad mediam noctem disputātum esset, tum dēmum Sabīnī sententia
superāvit, ac māne castra mōtum īrō mōlitibus prōnūntiātum est.
Cōnsūmpta est vigiliīs reliqua pars noctis, cum mīlitēs bona colligerent
sua, nec satis scīrent quid in hībernīs relinquendum, aut quid sēcum
portandum esset. Deinde prīmā lūce ē castrīs longissimō agmine
maximīsque impedimentīs profectī sunt; plērīque enim nōn suspicābantur
Ambiorīgem omnia ea, quae dē Germānōrum adventū dīxerat, mentītum esse,
cum spērāret ita sē Rōmānōs ex hībernīs ēlicere posse.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

At interim hostēs, quī ex nocturnō strepitū intellēxerant lēgātōs
cōnstituisse cōnfēstim castra movēre, in silvās paulum sē recēperant
īnsidiīsque locō idōneō collocātīs adventum Rōmānōrum cupidē
exspectābant.
:::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
:::
:::::::
::::::::
:::::::::::

[]{#c105_A_First_Latin_Reader_105.xhtml}

::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}
::: {.titulusHeaderBox about="#mwt1"}
:::

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}
:::

:::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
::::::: text
::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt9" lang="la"}
[[]{#c105_A_First_Latin_Reader_105.xhtml_pagename138-n1982}]{#c105_A_First_Latin_Reader_105.xhtml_id-128-n1981
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/138" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 105]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*The Romans are Ambushed*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Ita factum est ut, cum maior pars agminis Rōmānōrum in magnam vallem
dēscendisset, Gallī subitō ē latebrīs
[[]{#c105_A_First_Latin_Reader_105.xhtml_pagename139}]{#c105_A_First_Latin_Reader_105.xhtml_id-129
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/139"}âerumperent, atque
inīquissimō nostrīs locō proelium committerētur. Sabīnus, quī adhuc
nihil suspicātus erat, ācerrimō hostium impetū vehementer commōtus, in
omnīs partēs properāvit ac cohortēs disponere cōnātus est: Cotta vērō,
quiī cōgitāverat haec posse in itinere accidere, ob eamque causam
cēnsuerat ex hībernīs nōn discēdendum esse, virum magnum interim sē
praebēbat; omnibus enim modīs commūnī cōnsulēbat salūtī, ac fortissimē
officia et imperātōris et mīlitis simul praestābat.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Tum, quod propter longitūdinem agminis nōn facile providērī poterat quid
quōque locō faciendum esset, lēgātī suīs imperāvērunt ut, impedīments
relictīs, in orbem cōnsisterent. Quod consilium (etsī eōdem imperātōrēs
summī in eius modī cāsū ūtī solent) tum haud fēlīciter accidit; nam
hostēs, nōn sine maximō timōre impedīmenta ā Rōmānīs relicta esse ratī,
etiam ācrius iam dīmicāvērunt.
:::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
:::
:::::::
::::::::
:::::::::::

[]{#c106_A_First_Latin_Reader_106.xhtml}

::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}
::: {.titulusHeaderBox about="#mwt1"}
:::

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}
:::

:::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
::::::: text
::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt9" lang="la"}
[[]{#c106_A_First_Latin_Reader_106.xhtml_pagename140}]{#c106_A_First_Latin_Reader_106.xhtml_id-130
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/140" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 106]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*The Enemy Prevail*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Accēdēbat ut mīlitēs multī ab sīgnīs discēderent et bona sua cārissima
ab impedīmentīs arripere cōnārentur: cēterī autem, quamquam ā Fortunā
dēserēbantur, tamen omnem spem salūtis in virtūte pōnēbant, et quotiēns
quaeque cohors prōcurrerat, ab eā parte magnus numerus hostium cadēbat.
Quā rē animadversā, Ambiorīx suōs procul tēla conicere iussit nec
propius accēdere. Quam ob rem, cum iam aliqua cohors excesserat ex orbe
atque impetum fēcerat, summā celeritāte fugiēbant hostēs; cum autem
cohors rursus ad aciem sē recipere coeperat, tum Gallī, undīque coortī,
nostrōs ācerrimē premēbant.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Cum sīc ā prīmā lūce ad hōram octāvam pugnātum esset, T. Balventius, vir
fortis et magnae auctōritātis, trāgulā graviter vulnerātus est; Q.
Lūcānius, fortissimē pugnāns, dum circumventō fīliō subsidiō venit, est
interfectus; ac L. Cotta lēgātus, cum mīlitēs hortārētur, fundā
percussus est. Quibus rēbus permōtus Sabīnus, cum procul Ambiorīgem suōs
cohortantem cōnspēxīsset, interpretem suum
[[]{#c106_A_First_Latin_Reader_106.xhtml_pagename141}]{#c106_A_First_Latin_Reader_106.xhtml_id-131
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/141"}Cn. Pompēium ad eum
mīsit rogātum, ut sibi mīlitibusque parceret.
:::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
:::
:::::::
::::::::
:::::::::::

[]{#c107_A_First_Latin_Reader_107.xhtml}

:::::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}
::: {.titulusHeaderBox about="#mwt1"}
:::

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}
:::

::::::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
:::::::::: text
::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt9" lang="la"}
[[]{#c107_A_First_Latin_Reader_107.xhtml_pagename141-n1990}]{#c107_A_First_Latin_Reader_107.xhtml_id-131-n1989
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/141" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 107]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*Annihilation of the Roman Force*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Rēx respondit nihil Rōmānīs timendum esse, sēque Sabīnī ipsīus salūtem
praestāre, sī ille ad colloquium venīre vellet. Quō audītō, Cotta tamen
negāvit ad armātum hostem sē itūrum, atque in eō persevērāvit. Sabīnus
autem tribūnōs mīlitum centuriōnēsque quī adstābant se sequī iussit;
cumque propius Ambiorīgem accessisset, iussus arma abicere, pāruit, ac
suīs ut idem facerent imperāvit. Dum autem ibi dē condiciōnibus inter sē
agunt, Sabīnus paulātim circumventus ā Gallīs occīsus est.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Tum vērō hostēs sustulērunt ululātum, impetūque in nostrōs factō ōrdinēs
perturbāvērunt. Ibi L. Cotta pugnāns periit cum maximā parte mīlitum.
Reliquī sē in hīberna recēpērunt, unde erant nūper ēgressī. Ē quibus L.
Petrosidius aquilifer, homō magnārum vīrium, cum cōnfertissimā
multitūdine hostium premerētur, aquilam intrā vāllum prōiēcit, ipse prō
castrīs fortissimē pugnāns interfectus est.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Rōmānī aegrē ad noctem oppugnātiōnem sustinuerunt;
[[]{#c107_A_First_Latin_Reader_107.xhtml_pagename143}]{#c107_A_First_Latin_Reader_107.xhtml_id-133
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/143"}tum, dēspērātā
salūte, ad ūnum omnēs sē ipsī interfēcērunt. Paucī, quī paulō ante ē
proeliō effūgerant, per silvās incertīs itineribus ad T. Labiēnum
lēgātum in hīberna pervēnērunt, atque eum dē rēbus gestīs fēcērunt
certiōrem.
:::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
:::

[[]{#c107_A_First_Latin_Reader_107.xhtml_pagename142}]{#c107_A_First_Latin_Reader_107.xhtml_id-132
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/142" about="#mwt11"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

[]{.mw-empty-elt about="#mwt12"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt12"}
[Standard Bearers]{.smallcaps}
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt12"}

The standards carried in the Roman army were numerous and rather diverse
(see also the illustration on page 162). As the eagle was the chief
standard of the legion, upon it was lavished all the enthusiastic
devotion which modern soldiers feel for their flag. No disgrace was so
deep and terrible as to have the eagle fall into the hands of the enemy.
::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}

[]{#c108_A_First_Latin_Reader_108.xhtml}

::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}
::: {.titulusHeaderBox about="#mwt1"}
:::

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}
:::

:::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
::::::: text
::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt9" lang="la"}
[[]{#c108_A_First_Latin_Reader_108.xhtml_pagename143-n1996}]{#c108_A_First_Latin_Reader_108.xhtml_id-133-n1995
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/143" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 108]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*The Gauls attack a Second Camp*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Hāc victōriā sublātus, Ambiorīx statim cum equitātū in Aduātucōs, quī
erant eius rēgnō fīnitimī, profectus est; neque noctem neque diem
intermīsit, peditātumque sē iussit subsequī.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Rē dēmōnstrātā Aduātucīsque concitātīs, posterō diē in Nerviōs pervēnit,
eōsque hortātus est, nē suī in perpetuum līberandī occāsiōnem
dīmitterent. Interfectōs esse lēgātōs duo Rōmānōs magnamque partem
exercitūs interīsse docuit; facillimēque opprimī posse earn quoque
legiōnem, quae cum Q.[ ]{typeof="mw:Entity"}Cicerōne in fīnibus eōrum
hiemāret. Quaa ōrātiōne facile Nerviīs persuāsit.
[[]{#c108_A_First_Latin_Reader_108.xhtml_pagename144}]{#c108_A_First_Latin_Reader_108.xhtml_id-134
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/144"}Itaque cōnfēstim
dīmissīs nūntiīs ad Ceutronēs, Grudiōs, nātiōnēsque aliās, ut quam
maximīs cōpiīs auxiliō statim venīrent, repente ad Cicerōnis hīberna
hostēs sē ostendērunt; ubi nōnnūllī mīlitēs, morte Sabīnī Cottaeque
nōndum nūntiātā, sine timōre extrā mūnītiōnēs officiīs variīs operam
dabant. Ex hīs quīdam, quī līgnātiōnis causā in silvās discesserant,
repentīnō equitum adventū interceptī sunt. Cēterī autem celeriter
concurrērunt ad arma, vāllumque cōnscendērunt.
:::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
:::
:::::::
::::::::
:::::::::::

[]{#c109_A_First_Latin_Reader_109.xhtml}

::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}
::: {.titulusHeaderBox about="#mwt1"}
:::

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}
:::

:::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
::::::: text
::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt9" lang="la"}
[[]{#c109_A_First_Latin_Reader_109.xhtml_pagename144-n2000}]{#c109_A_First_Latin_Reader_109.xhtml_id-134-n1999
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/144" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 109]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*The Besieged attempt to Communicate with Caesar*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Missae sunt ad Caesarem cōnfēstim ā Cicerōne litterae; obsessīs autem
omnibus viīs, ab hostibus missī interceptī sunt. Noctū ex materiā, quam
mūnitiōnis causā comportāvērant, nostrī turrēs circiter CXX incrēdibilī
celeritāte exstrūxērunt.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Posterō diē hostēs, multō maiōribus coāctīs cōpiīs, castra iterum
oppugnāvērunt, fossamque complēre cōnātī sunt. Eādem ratiōne, quā
prīdiē, nostrī restitērunt. Hoc idem reliquīs deinceps diēbus factum
est. Nūlla pars noctis labōribus mīlitum carēbat: nōn aegrīs, nōn
vulnerātīs
[[]{#c109_A_First_Latin_Reader_109.xhtml_pagename145}]{#c109_A_First_Latin_Reader_109.xhtml_id-135
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/145"}facultās quiētis
dabātur: nec Cicerō ipse, etsī tēnuissimā erat valētūdine, nocturnō
tempore ad quiētem ūtēbātur, priusquam mīlitum vōcibus sibi parcere
coāctus est.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Tum ducēs Nerviōrum, quī aliquam causam amīcitiae cum Cicerōne habēbant,
colloquī sēsē velle nūntiāvērunt. Factā potestāte, eādem commemorant,
quae paulō ante Ambiorīx cum Sabīnō ēgerat. Addunt etiam dē Sabīnī
morte, et cōnfīrmant sē nihil recūsāre nisi hīberna, atque hanc
inveterāscere cōnsuētūdinem nōlle; quam ob rem Rōmānīs licēre
incolumibus ex castrīs discēdere et quāscumque in partēs velint sine
timōre proficīscī.
:::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
:::
:::::::
::::::::
:::::::::::

[]{#c110_A_First_Latin_Reader_110.xhtml}

::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}
::: {.titulusHeaderBox about="#mwt1"}
:::

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}
:::

:::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
::::::: text
::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt12" lang="la"}
[[]{#c110_A_First_Latin_Reader_110.xhtml_pagename145-n2004}]{#c110_A_First_Latin_Reader_110.xhtml_id-135-n2003
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/145" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 110]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*Heroic Defense of their Camp*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

At Cicerō, quī iniussū Caesaris castra movēre nōlēbat, Gallīs respondit
nōn esse cōnsuētūdinem populī Rōmānī ūllam accipere ab hoste armātō
condiciōnem; sī ab armīs discēdere atque lēgātōs ad Caesarem mittere
vellent, spērāre sē eōs, quae petīssent, impetrātūrōs.
[[]{#c110_A_First_Latin_Reader_110.xhtml_pagename146}]{#c110_A_First_Latin_Reader_110.xhtml_id-136
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/146"}Hāc spē dēiectī
Nerviī vāllō pedum decem et fossā pedum quīndecim hīberna circumdant.
Eīs autem nūlla erat ferramentōrum cōpia, quae ad eam rem ūsuī sunt;
gladiīs igitur caespitēs circumcīdere et manibus sagīsque terram
exhaurīre cōgēbantur. Quā ex rē hominum multitūdō cōgnōscī potest; nam
hōrīs ferē tribus decem mīlium passuum in circuitū mūnītiōnem pedum
quīndecim perfēcērunt.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Septimō oppugnātiōnis diē, maximō coortō ventō, hostēs tēla fervefacta
in casās iēcērunt; quae celeriter comprehendērunt ignem, et ventī
magnitūdine in omnem locum castrōrum distulērunt. Tum Gallī, victōriam
ratī iam dēmum esse partam, maximō clāmōre vāllum scālīs ascendere
coepērunt. At tanta erat virtūs nostrōrum, ut, cum maximā tēlōrum
multitūdine premerentur, suaque impedimenta omnia igni cōnsūmī
intellegerent, dē vāllō dēcēderet nēmō. Hīc diēs nostrīs longē
gravissimus fuit; sed tamen
[[]{#c110_A_First_Latin_Reader_110.xhtml_pagename147}]{#c110_A_First_Latin_Reader_110.xhtml_id-137
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/147"}hunc habuit
ēventum, ut eō diē maximus numerus hostium interīret aut vulnerārētur.
:::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
:::
:::::::
::::::::
:::::::::::

[]{#c111_A_First_Latin_Reader_111.xhtml}

::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}
::: {.titulusHeaderBox about="#mwt1"}
:::

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}
:::

:::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
::::::: text
::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt9" lang="la"}
[[]{#c111_A_First_Latin_Reader_111.xhtml_pagename147-n2010}]{#c111_A_First_Latin_Reader_111.xhtml_id-137-n2009
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/147" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 111]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*A Messenger eludes the Enemy*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Quantō erat in diēs gravior oppugnātiō, tantō crēbriōrēs litterae
nūntiīque ad Caesarem mittēbantur; ē quibus nōnnūllī, in cōnspectū
nostrōrum mīlitum interceptī, cum cruciātū necātī sunt. Intrā hīberna
autem erat Nervius quidam, nōmine Verticō, quī ad Cicerōnem perfūgerat,
cum prīmum castra oppugnāta sunt. Hīc servō spē lībertātis magnīsque
persuāsit praemiīs, ut litterās ad Caesarem dēferret. Ille celeriter
profectus, et Gallus inter Gallōs sine ūllā suspiciōne versātus, ad
Caesarem incolumis pervēnit. Ab eō dē perīculīs Cicerōnis legiōnisque
cōgnitum est.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Caesar, acceptīs litterīs horā ferē ūndecimā diēī, nūntium cōnfēstim in
Bellovacōs mittit ad M. Crassum, cuius hīberna aberant ab eō mīlia
passuum quīnque et vīgintī; iubet mediā nocte legiōnem proficīscī
celeriterque ad sē venīre. Alterum ad C. Fabium lēgātum mittit, quī eī
[[]{#c111_A_First_Latin_Reader_111.xhtml_pagename148}]{#c111_A_First_Latin_Reader_111.xhtml_id-138
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/148"}nūntiet, ut
legiōnem in Atrebatēs addūcat, quōrum per fīnēs sibi iter faciendum
sciēbat. Scrībit Labiēnō ut, sī reī pūblicae commodō fierī possit, cum
legiōne ad fines Nerviōrum veniat. Reliquam partem exercitūs, quae paulō
aberat longius, nōn arbitrātur exspectandam; equitēs circiter CCCC ex
proximīs hībernīs cōgit.
:::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
:::
:::::::
::::::::
:::::::::::

[]{#c112_A_First_Latin_Reader_112.xhtml}

::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}
::: {.titulusHeaderBox about="#mwt1"}
:::

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}
:::

:::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
::::::: text
::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt9" lang="la"}
[[]{#c112_A_First_Latin_Reader_112.xhtml_pagename148-n2014}]{#c112_A_First_Latin_Reader_112.xhtml_id-138-n2013
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/148" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 112]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*Caesar heads a Relief Force*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Hōrā ferē tertiā ab antecursōribus dē Crassī adventū Caesar certior est
factus. Eō diē mīlia passuum vīgintī prōgressus est. Crassum
Samarobrīvae praeposuit, legiōnemque eī trādidit, quod ibi relinquēbat
impedimenta exercitūs, obsidēs cīvitātum, litterās pūblicās,
frūmentumque omne, quod eō tolerandae hiemis causā comportāverat. Paulō
post Fabius, ut imperātum erat, in itinere cum legiōne occurrit. At
Labiēnus, morte Sabīnī et clāde cohortium cōgnitā, cum omnēs ad eum
Trēverōrum cōpiae vēnissent, veritus nē, sī ex hībernīs fugae similem
[[]{#c112_A_First_Latin_Reader_112.xhtml_pagename149}]{#c112_A_First_Latin_Reader_112.xhtml_id-139
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/149"}prōfectiōnem
fēcisset, hostium impetus sustinērī nōn posset, litterās Caesarī
remīsit, quibus ostendit quantum esset perīculum docuitque omnēs
peditātūs equitātūsque cōpiās Trēverōrum tria mīlia passuum ab suīs
castrīs cōnsēdisse.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Caesar, cōnsiliō eius probātō, etsī opīniōne trium legiōnum dēiectus ad
duās redierat, omnem tamen commūnis salūtis spem in celeritāte pōnēbat.
Venit igitur magnīs itineribus in Nerviōrum fīnēs. Ibi ex captīvīs
cōgnōscit quae in Cicerōnīs hībernis gerantur, quantōque in perīculo rēs
sit.
:::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
:::
:::::::
::::::::
:::::::::::

[]{#c113_A_First_Latin_Reader_113.xhtml}

:::::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}
::: {.titulusHeaderBox about="#mwt1"}
:::

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}
:::

::::::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
:::::::::: text
::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt9" lang="la"}
[[]{#c113_A_First_Latin_Reader_113.xhtml_pagename149-n2018}]{#c113_A_First_Latin_Reader_113.xhtml_id-139-n2017
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/149" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 113]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*The Besieged learn of Caesar’s Approach*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Itaque cuidam ex equitibus Gallīs Caesar magnls praemiīs persuāsit, ut
ad Cicerōnem epistulam dēferret. Hanc Graecīs litterīs scrīptam mīsit,
nē Gallō interceptō nostra cōnsilia ab hostibus cōgnōscerentur. Hominī
imperāvit ut, sī hīberna intrāre nōn posset, trāgulam cum epistulā ad
āmentum dēligātā intrā mūnītiōnēs abiceret. In epistulā scrīpsit sē cum
legiōnibus profectum celeriter adfore; Cicerōnem hortātus est ut
prīstinam virtūtem retinēret.
[[]{#c113_A_First_Latin_Reader_113.xhtml_pagename151}]{#c113_A_First_Latin_Reader_113.xhtml_id-141
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/151"}Gallus, cum ad
hīberna vēnisset, perīculum veritus, ut erat imperātum, trāgulam cum
litterīs mittit. Haec cāsū ad turrim adhaesit, neque ā nostrīs statim
animadversa, tertiō diē ā mīlite quōdam cōnspicitur; quī eam sine morā
ad Cicerōnem dēfert. Ille, epistulā perlēctā, mīlitēs laetus docet
Caesarem iam subsidiō venīre. Tum fūmī incendiōrum procul cernēbantur;
quae rēs omnem dubitātiōnem adventūs legiōnum expulit.
:::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
:::

.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/150" about="#mwt11"

[]{.mw-empty-elt about="#mwt12"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt12"}
[Arma]{.smallcaps}
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt12"}

The upper illustration is interesting as showing the very primitive
equipment of some of the light-armed troops. In the lower picture may be
seen on the spears of the warrior the strap (*āmentum*) which was used
to assist the hand when the weapons were hurled.
::::

[]{#c114_A_First_Latin_Reader_114.xhtml}

::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}
::: {.titulusHeaderBox about="#mwt1"}
:::

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}
:::

:::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
::::::: text
::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt9" lang="la"}
[[]{#c114_A_First_Latin_Reader_114.xhtml_pagename151-n2024}]{#c114_A_First_Latin_Reader_114.xhtml_id-141-n2023
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/151" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 114]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*The Enemy raise the Siege*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Gallī rē cōgnitā per explōrātōrēs, obsidiōne statim relictā, ad Caesarem
omnibus cōpiīs contendunt. Quō animadversō, Cicerō Gallum quendam
celeriter cum litteris mittit, in quibus scrībit hostēs ab sē
dīscessisse omnemque multitudinem ad Caesarem convertisse. Quibus
litterīs circiter mediā nocte adlātīs, Caesar suōs facit certiōrēs,
eōsque ad pugnandum animō cōnfīrmat.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Posterō diē, cum lūce prīmā mōvisset castra et circiter mīlia passuum
quattuor prōgressus esset, trāns vallem
[[]{#c114_A_First_Latin_Reader_114.xhtml_pagename152}]{#c114_A_First_Latin_Reader_114.xhtml_id-142
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/152"}magnam et rīvum
hostium multitūdinem vīdit. Erat magnī perīculī rēs cum tantīs cōpiīs
inīquō locō dīmicāre; tum, quoniam obsidiōne līberātum esse Cicerōnem
sciēbat, dē celeritāte aliquid sibi remittendum existimābat: quārē
cōnsēdit, et, quam aequissimō locō poterat, castra mūnivit.
:::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
:::
:::::::
::::::::
:::::::::::

[]{#c115_A_First_Latin_Reader_115.xhtml}

::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}
::: {.titulusHeaderBox about="#mwt1"}
:::

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}
:::

:::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
::::::: text
::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt9" lang="la"}
[[]{#c115_A_First_Latin_Reader_115.xhtml_pagename152-n2028}]{#c115_A_First_Latin_Reader_115.xhtml_id-142-n2027
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/152" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 115]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*They are Outgeneraled by Caesar*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Postrīdie hostium equitātus prīma lūce ad castra accessit, proeliumque
cum nostrīs equitibus commīsit. Caesar autem suīs imperāvit ut cēderent
cōnsultō sēque in castra reciperent; simul ex omnibus partibus castra
altiōre vāllō munīrī, portās obstruī, omniaque cum simulātiōne timōris
agī iussit.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Quibus rēbus invītātī, hostēs cōpiās rīvum trādūxērunt omnīs, aciemque
inīquō locō cōnstituērunt; tum Caesar, omnibus portīs ēruptiōne factā
equitātūque ēmissō, eōs
[[]{#c115_A_First_Latin_Reader_115.xhtml_pagename153}]{#c115_A_First_Latin_Reader_115.xhtml_id-143
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/153"}celeriter in fugam
dedit. Longius autem īnsequī veritus, quod silvae palūdēsque
intercēdēbant, omnibus suīs incolumibus eōdem diē ad Cicerōnem pervēnit.
Turrēs mūnitiōnēsque hostium admīratur. Legiōne prōducta, cōgnōscit nōn
decimum quemque esse reliquum mīlitem sine vulnere; quā ex rē iūdicat
quantō in perīculo rēs fuerit. Cicerōne mīlitibusque laudātīs,
centuriōnēs trībūnōsque singulōs appellat, quōrum ēgregiam fuisse
virtūtem testimōniō Cicerōnis cōgnōverat. Dē cāsū Sabīnī et Cottae
certius ex captīvīs cōgnōscit.
:::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
:::

[]{#c116_A_First_Latin_Reader_116.xhtml}

::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}
::: {.titulusHeaderBox about="#mwt1"}
:::

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}
:::

:::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
::::::: text
::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt9" lang="la"}
[[]{#c116_A_First_Latin_Reader_116.xhtml_pagename153-n2032}]{#c116_A_First_Latin_Reader_116.xhtml_id-143-n2031
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/153" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 116]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*Arrangements for the Rest of the Winter*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Dum haec fīunt, ad Labiēnum incrēdibilī celeritāte dē victōriā Caesaris
fāma dēfertur; quīn etiam, cum ab hībernis Cicerōnīs mīlia passuum
Labiēnus abesset circiter sexāginta, atque ad Cicerōnem post hōram nōnam
diēī Caesar pervēnisset, ante mediam noctem subitō ad portās Labiēnī
castrōrum audītus est eōrum clāmor, quī lēgatō grātulārī
[[]{#c116_A_First_Latin_Reader_116.xhtml_pagename154}]{#c116_A_First_Latin_Reader_116.xhtml_id-144
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/154"}volēbant, quod
hostīs Caesar superāvisset. At Trēverī, quī posterō diē hīberna Labiēnī
oppugnāre cōnstituerant, repentīnā rē perterritī noctū domum celeriter
sē recēpērunt.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Postrīdiē Caesar cōntiōne habitā mīlitēs cōnfirmāvit, eōsque docuit
dētrīmentum, quod temeritāte lēgātī esset acceptum, aequiōre animō esse
ferendum, quod beneficiō deōrum immortālium et virtūte eōrum legiōnēs
cēterae cōnservātae essent neque hostibus diūtinum gaudium
relinquerētur. Fabium cum legiōne remīsit in hīberna; ipse cum tribus
legiōnibus circum Samarobrīvam hiemāre cōnstituit: nam cum animī omnium
Gallōrum ad bellum incitātī vidērentur, tōtam hiemem sibi apud exercitum
manendum arbitrābātur.
:::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
:::

[]{#c117_A_First_Latin_Reader_117.xhtml}

:::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}
::: {.titulusHeaderBox about="#mwt1"}
:::

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}
:::

::::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
:::::::: text
:::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt24" lang="la"}
[[]{#c117_A_First_Latin_Reader_117.xhtml_pagename155}]{#c117_A_First_Latin_Reader_117.xhtml_id-145
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/155" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[**AN AFRICAN
CAMPAIGN**]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
[[LESSON 117]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

[During the civil war which broke out between Caesar and Pompey four or
five years after the events above narrated, there was fighting in all
parts of the civilized world, and more than once Africa was the
battleground.]{style="font-size: 83%;"}

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*Caesar lands a Force in Africa*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Interim C. Cūriō^[^777]^ duās legiōnēs, D^[^778]^ equitēs, ex Siciliā in
Āfricam trānsportāvit. Ubi eius adventum L. Caesar^[^779]^ cum decem
longīs nāvibus exspectābat; quī autem, cum classis Cūriōnis in
cōnspectum vēnisset, nāvium multitūdinem veritus,^[^780]^ appulsā ad
proximum lītus trirēme,^[^781]^ pedibus^[^782]^ Hadrūmētum^[^783]^
fūgit: quō^[^784]^ nāvēs quoque eius reliquae, fugā^[^785]^ ducis
cōgnitā, statim sē recēpērunt.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Curiō Mārcium Rūfum cum classe Uticam^[^786]^ praemittit. Ipse eōdem cum
exercitū proficīscitur^[^787]^ trīduīque iter prōgressus, ad flūmen
Bagradam pervēnit. Ibi C. Canīnium Rebilum lēgātum legiōnēsque
relinquit; ipse cum equitātū antecēdit^[^788]^ ad Castra Cornēlia
explōranda, quī locus^[^789]^ peridōneus^[^790]^ castrīs existimābātur.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

\
[[]{#c117_A_First_Latin_Reader_117.xhtml_pagename157}]{#c117_A_First_Latin_Reader_117.xhtml_id-147
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/157"}Hāc explōrātā
regiōne, Curiō Uticae quoque mūnitiōnēs speculātus est; cumque
animadvertisset plēnissimīs viīs undique portārī agīque multa, quae
repentīnī tumultūs timōre ex agrīs in urbem cōnferēbantur, equitātum
mīsit, ut praeda īnspērātā potīrētur. Simul ex urbe ēmissī sunt DC
equitēs Numidae, quī agricolīs fugientibus auxiliō essent. Concurrunt
equitēs inter sē; neque vērō prīmum impetum nostrōrum Numidae ferre
poterant, sed interfectīs circiter CXX reliquī sē in urbem contulērunt.
::::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
:::

    [**trirēme**: sc. **suā** (*trirēmis, -is*, [f]{.smallcaps}.,
    *galley*)]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c117_A_First_Latin_Reader_117.xhtml_cite_note-5-n2057}
6.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c117_A_First_Latin_Reader_117.xhtml_cite_ref-6-n2042){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**pedibus**: we would say "on foot"; cf. **manibus genibusque**, p.
    59, 1. 8.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c117_A_First_Latin_Reader_117.xhtml_cite_note-6-n2058}
7.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c117_A_First_Latin_Reader_117.xhtml_cite_ref-7-n2043){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**Hadrumētum**: consult the map on p. 146; for syntax, see the note
    on p. 79, 1. 21.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c117_A_First_Latin_Reader_117.xhtml_cite_note-7-n2059}
8.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c117_A_First_Latin_Reader_117.xhtml_cite_ref-8-n2044){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**quo**: the adv.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c117_A_First_Latin_Reader_117.xhtml_cite_note-8-n2060}
9.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c117_A_First_Latin_Reader_117.xhtml_cite_ref-9-n2045){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**fugă**: *defection*.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c117_A_First_Latin_Reader_117.xhtml_cite_note-9-n2061}
10. [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c117_A_First_Latin_Reader_117.xhtml_cite_ref-10-n2046){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**Uticam**: the base of operations of Pompey's forces in
    Africa.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c117_A_First_Latin_Reader_117.xhtml_cite_note-10-n2062}
11. [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c117_A_First_Latin_Reader_117.xhtml_cite_ref-11-n2047){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**proficīscitur**: from Anquillaria.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c117_A_First_Latin_Reader_117.xhtml_cite_note-11-n2063}
12. [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c117_A_First_Latin_Reader_117.xhtml_cite_ref-12-n2048){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**antecedit**: **antecēdō**, 3, **-cessi, -cessum est**, *push
    ahead*, lit. *go on ahead*.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c117_A_First_Latin_Reader_117.xhtml_cite_note-12-n2064}
13. [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c117_A_First_Latin_Reader_117.xhtml_cite_ref-13-n2049){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [*quī locus*: cf. *quae urbs*, p. 44, 1. 13.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c117_A_First_Latin_Reader_117.xhtml_cite_note-13-n2065}
14. [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c117_A_First_Latin_Reader_117.xhtml_cite_ref-14-n2050){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**peridōneus** (**-a, -um**): particularly suitable; cf. the note
    on perpaucos, p. 25, 1. 10.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c117_A_First_Latin_Reader_117.xhtml_cite_note-14-n2066}

[]{#c118_A_First_Latin_Reader_118.xhtml}

::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}
::: {.titulusHeaderBox about="#mwt1"}
:::

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}
:::

:::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
::::::: text
::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt9" lang="la"}
[[]{#c118_A_First_Latin_Reader_118.xhtml_pagename157-n2068}]{#c118_A_First_Latin_Reader_118.xhtml_id-147-n2067
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/157" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 118]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*Operations about Utica*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Interim Mārcius nāvēs longās Uticam dēdūxerat; cuius adventū cōgnitō,
Cūriō prōnūntiārī iussit onerāriīs, quae in portū ad ancoram stābant
numerō circiter CC, sē in hostium locō habitūrum omnēs, quī nōn statim
ad Castra Cornēlia nāvis trādūxissent. Quā prōnūntiātiōne factā, sine
morā sublātīs ancorīs omnēs reliquērunt Uticam et, quō imperātum erat,
trānsiērunt. Quae rēs omnium rērum cōpiā exercitum nostrum complēvit.
[[]{#c118_A_First_Latin_Reader_118.xhtml_pagename158}]{#c118_A_First_Latin_Reader_118.xhtml_id-148
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/158"}Hīs rēbus gestīs,
Cūriō sē in castra ad Bagradam recipit, posterōque diē exercitum Uticam
dūcit et prope oppidum castra ponit. Nōndum opere castrōrum perfectō,
equitēs ex statiōne nūntiant magna auxilia equitum peditumque ā rēge
Iubā missa Uticam venīre; eōdemque tempore vīs magna pulveris
cernēbātur, et temporis pūnctō prīmum agmen erat in cōnspectū. Quā rē
nova Cūriō permōtus equitēs suōs praemittit, quī prīmum impetum
sustineant; ipse, celeriter ab opere dēductis legiōnibus, aciem
īnstruit.
:::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
:::
:::::::

:::::::::::

[]{#c119_A_First_Latin_Reader_119.xhtml}

::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}
::: {.titulusHeaderBox about="#mwt1"}
:::

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}
:::

:::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
::::::: text
::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt9" lang="la"}
[[]{#c119_A_First_Latin_Reader_119.xhtml_pagename158-n2072}]{#c119_A_First_Latin_Reader_119.xhtml_id-148-n2071
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/158" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 119]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*Curio gains an Initial Advantage*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Interim equitēs cum hostibus proelium commisērunt et, priusquam legiōnēs
plānē explicārī possent, tōta auxilia rēgis, quae nūllō ordine et sine
metū iter faciēbant, in fugam coniecta sunt. Equitēs hostium per lītus
in oppidum properāvērunt, peditum autem magnus numerus interfectus est.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Proximā nocte centuriōnēs du ex castrīs Cūriōnis cum manipulāribus suīs
duōbus et vīgintī ad Attium Vārum perfugiunt; cuī cōnfīrmant tōtīus
exercitūs animōs alienōs esse
[[]{#c119_A_First_Latin_Reader_119.xhtml_pagename159}]{#c119_A_First_Latin_Reader_119.xhtml_id-149
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/159"}ā Cūriōne,
multōsque facultāte datā libenter esse trānsitūrōs. Qua ōrātiōne
adductus Vārus posterō diē māne legiōnēs ex castrīs ēdūcit. Facit idem
Cūriō, atque ūnā valle nōn magnā interpositā suās uterque cōpiās
īnstruit.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Erat in exercitū Vārī lēgātus quīdam, cuī nōtī erant multī Cūriōnis
mīlitēs. Hanc ille nactus appellātiōnis causam, circumīre aciem Cūriōnis
atque omnēs hortārī coepit, ut Vārum sequerentur; quīn etiam praemium
pollicitus est, sī quī ad eum trānsīre voluissent. Hīs verbīs audītīs,
nūllam in partem ab exercitū Cūriōnis fit sīgnificātiō, atque ita suas
uterque cōpiās redūcit.
:::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
:::
:::::::
::::::::
:::::::::::

[]{#c120_A_First_Latin_Reader_120.xhtml}

::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}
::: {.titulusHeaderBox about="#mwt1"}
:::

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}
:::

:::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
::::::: text
::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt9" lang="la"}
[[]{#c120_A_First_Latin_Reader_120.xhtml_pagename159-n2076}]{#c120_A_First_Latin_Reader_120.xhtml_id-149-n2075
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/159" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 120]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*He maintains his Army’s Loyalty to Caesar*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

At in castrīs Cūriōnis animī omnium sollicitī erant; quisque enim ad id,
quod ab aliō audierat, aliquid suī timoris addēbat.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Cōnsiliō convocātō, duae sententiae dictae sunt. Erant quī castra Vārī
statim oppugnanda cēnsērent; alterī autem
[[]{#c120_A_First_Latin_Reader_120.xhtml_pagename160}]{#c120_A_First_Latin_Reader_120.xhtml_id-150
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/160"}optimum factū
existimābant in Castra Cornēlia legiōnēs redūcere, ut maiōre spatiō
temporis interpositō mīlitum mentēs sānārentur, simul ut exercitus, sī
proeliō victus esset, in Siciliam facile trānsportārī posset. Cūriō
tamen “Neutrum cōnsilium,” inquit, “probō; neque enim tantī sum animī,
ut castra tam mūnita temerē oppugnanda cēnseam, neque tantī timōris, ut
spem statim dīmittam, atque omnia prius experienda arbitror.”

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Quārē, dīmissō cōnsiliō, cōntiōnem advocat mīlitum; quōrum animōs verbis
cōnfīrmat, docetque quid sit causae, cūr sibi Caesarīque fidēlēs sint.
Quā ōratiōne permōtī mīlitēs eum etiam dīcentem interpellābant,
discēdentem vērō ex cōntiōne ūniversī cohortantur ut magnō sit animō
neve dubitet proelium committere et suam fidem virtūtemque experīrī.
:::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
:::
:::::::
::::::::
:::::::::::

[]{#c121_A_First_Latin_Reader_121.xhtml}

::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}
::: {.titulusHeaderBox about="#mwt1"}
:::

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}
:::

:::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
::::::: text
::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt6" lang="la"}
[[]{#c121_A_First_Latin_Reader_121.xhtml_pagename161}]{#c121_A_First_Latin_Reader_121.xhtml_id-151
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/161" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 121]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*The Pompeians suffer a Second Reverse*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Quibus rēbus cōnfīrmātus Cūriō cōnstituit, cum prīmum esset data
potestās, proeliō rem committere; postrīdiēque mīlitēs prōductōs eōdem
locō, quō ante cōnstiterant, in aciē collocāvit. Quō animadversō, Vārus
quoque cōpiās prodūxit, nē, sī aequo locō darētur occāsiō, dīmicandī
facultātem dīmitteret.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Erat vallēs inter duās aciēs, ut suprā dēmōnstrātum est, nōn ita magna,
at difficilī et arduō ascēnsū. Hanc uterque sī adversāriōrum cōpiae
trānsīre cōnārentur, exspectābat, quō aequiōre locō proelium ipse
committeret. Postrēmō Vārī equitēs in vallem dēscendere coepērunt. Ad
eōs Cūriō equitātum et duās cohortēs mittit; quōrum prīmum impetum
equitēs hostium nōn ferunt, sed admissīs equīs ad suōs refugiunt.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Quā rē animadversā, legiōnēs sē sequī iubet Cūriō, et omnibus cum cōpiīs
in vallem cōnfēstim dēscendit; interim autem hostēs, veritī nē ab
equitātū circumvenīrentur, terga vertunt ūniversī, ac summā celeritāte
sē in castra recipiunt.
:::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
:::
:::::::
::::::::
:::::::::::

[]{#c122_A_First_Latin_Reader_122.xhtml}

:::::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}
::: {.titulusHeaderBox about="#mwt1"}
:::

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}
:::

::::::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
:::::::::: text
::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt9" lang="la"}
[[]{#c122_A_First_Latin_Reader_122.xhtml_pagename162}]{#c122_A_First_Latin_Reader_122.xhtml_id-152
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/162" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 122]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*Narrow Escape of their Commander*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Quā in fugā Fabius Paelignus, mīles quīdam ex Cūriōnis exercitū, agmen
fugientium cōnsecūtus, magnā vōce Vārum ita nōmine appellavit, ut ūnus
esse ex eius mīlitibus et velle aliquid dicere vidērētur. Ubi autem
Vārus saepius appellātus cōnstitit, et quis esset aut quid vellet
quaesīvit, tum Fabius eius umerum apertum gladiō appetiit. Quod ille
perīculum sublātō scūtō vītāvit; Fabius autem ā proximis mīlitibus
circumventus interficitur.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Interim fugientium multitūdine portae castrōrum complētae sunt, atque
iter erat ita impeditum, ut plūrēs in eō locō sine vulnere quam in
proeliō aut fugā interīrent; nōnnūlli vērō erant adeō perterritī, ut
prōtinus eōdem cursū per castra in oppidum ipsum contenderent. At
Cūriōnis mīlitēs, ad proelium ēgressī, sēcum nūllam cōpiam portaverant
eārum rērum, quae ad oppugnātiōnem castrōrum erant ūsuī. Itaque Cūriō
exercitum turn in castra redūcit. Cuius discessu vulnerati e castris
hostium in oppidum redūcuntur; quō quidem tempore multī praetereā per
simulātiōnem vulnerum propter metum eōdem sese
[[]{#c122_A_First_Latin_Reader_122.xhtml_pagename164}]{#c122_A_First_Latin_Reader_122.xhtml_id-154
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/164"}recipiunt. Quā rē
animadversā exercitūsque timōre cōgnitō, Varus, būcinātōre
tabernāculīsque paucīs in castrīs ad speciem relictīs, tertiā vigiliā
reliquum quoque exercitum silentiō in oppidum redūcit.
:::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
:::

[[]{#c122_A_First_Latin_Reader_122.xhtml_pagename163}]{#c122_A_First_Latin_Reader_122.xhtml_id-153
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/163" about="#mwt11"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

[]{.mw-empty-elt about="#mwt12"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt12"}
[Scūta]{.smallcaps}
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt12"}

This illustration, taken from the carvings on the column of Trajan (see
page 40), shows how Roman soldiers, by locking their shields (scuta),
formed a solid roof over their heads as they came up under a wall from
which the enemy were sending down a shower of missiles.
::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
:::

::::::::::::::

[]{#c123_A_First_Latin_Reader_123.xhtml}

::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}
::: {.titulusHeaderBox about="#mwt1"}
:::

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}
:::

:::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
::::::: text
::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt9" lang="la"}
[[]{#c123_A_First_Latin_Reader_123.xhtml_pagename164-n2088}]{#c123_A_First_Latin_Reader_123.xhtml_id-154-n2087
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/164" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 123]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*King Juba marches to the Relief of Varus*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Postridiē eius diēī Cūriō obsidēre Uticam coepit. Sed iam ad urbem
perveniunt ā rēge Iubā nūntiī, quī illum adesse magnīs cum copiīs dīcant
oppidānōsque dē dēfēnsiōne urbis hortentur. Nūntiābantur haec eādem
Cūriōnī. Ille tamen prīmō rēgem nihil contrā sē ausurum existimābat; sed
ubi certior est factus cōpiās Iubae ab Utiāa minus quīnque et vīgintī
mīlia passuum abesse, relictīs mūnītiōnibus sēsē in Castra Cornēlia
recēpit. Hūc comportāre coepit omnia, quae ad obsidiōnem sustinendam
ūsuī erant.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Dum haec fīunt, ex oppidānīs perfugīs audīvit Iubam aliō bellō esse
revocātum, et Saburram, eius praefectum, parvīs cum cōpiīs Uticae
appropinquāre. Quō audītō, cōnsilium temerē mūtāvit, proeliōque rem
committere
[[]{#c123_A_First_Latin_Reader_123.xhtml_pagename165}]{#c123_A_First_Latin_Reader_123.xhtml_id-155
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/165"}constituit. Quārē
equitātum omnem prīma nocte ad castra Saburrae praemittit; quī hostīs
necopīnantēs adortus, magnum numerum eōrum occīdit. Quō factō, ad
Curiōnem equitēs redeunt captīvōsque ad eum reducunt.
:::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
:::
:::::::
::::::::
:::::::::::

[]{#c124_A_First_Latin_Reader_124.xhtml}

::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}
::: {.titulusHeaderBox about="#mwt1"}
:::

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}
:::

:::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
::::::: text
::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt9" lang="la"}
[[]{#c124_A_First_Latin_Reader_124.xhtml_pagename165-n2092}]{#c124_A_First_Latin_Reader_124.xhtml_id-155-n2091
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/165" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 124]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*The Numidians resort to Strategy*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Cūriō, cohortibus quīnque castrīs praesidiō relictīs, omnibus cum copiīs
quārtā vigiliā profectus, sex mīlia passuum iam ipse prōgressus erat.
Quī, victōriā equitātūs cōgnitā, etiam celerius iter fecit; Iubam enim
crēdēbat longē abesse, exiguāsque Saburrae cōpiās facile sē opprimere
posse exīstimābat.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Interim autem Iuba (cuius dē discessū falsā erat nūntiātum, quīque iam
haud longē aberat), dē nocturnō proeliō certior factus, duo mīlia
equitum eamque peditum partem, cui maximē confīdebat, Saburrae subsidiō
mittit, ipseque cum reliquīs cōpiīs elepbantīsque sexāgintā lēnius
subsequitur. Suspicātus brevī Cūriōnem ipsum adfore, Saburra cōpiās
equitum peditumque statim īnstrūxit atque eīs imperāvit ut simul atque
nostrī in cōnspectum vēnissent, simulātiōne timōris paulātim cēderent.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Quō factō, hostēs fugere Cūriō ratus legiōnēs dē collibus
[[]{#c124_A_First_Latin_Reader_124.xhtml_pagename166}]{#c124_A_First_Latin_Reader_124.xhtml_id-156
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/166"}in plānitiem
dēdūxit; cumque longius esset inde prōgressus, cōnfectō iam labōre
exercitū, locō inīquō cōnstitit. Tum suīs signum subitō dat Saburra
aciemque explicat. Peditātū prīmao ad speciem tantum ūtitur, equitēs in
aciem nostram inmittit.
:::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
:::
:::::::
::::::::
:::::::::::

[]{#c125_A_First_Latin_Reader_125.xhtml}

::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}
::: {.titulusHeaderBox about="#mwt1"}
:::

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}
:::

:::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
::::::: text
::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt11" lang="la"}
[[]{#c125_A_First_Latin_Reader_125.xhtml_pagename166-n2096}]{#c125_A_First_Latin_Reader_125.xhtml_id-156-n2095
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/166" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 125]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*Curio's Army is Annihilated*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Repentīnā rē minimē permōtus Cūriō ōrdinēs circumiit mīlitēsque hortātus
est ut spem omnem in virtūte pōnerent. Hī prīmō fortissimē dīmicābant
sed hostēs, quī numerō longē erant superiōrēs, mox aciem nostram
circumventam ā tergō adorīrī coepērunt. Tum Cūriō, ubi perterritīs
omnibus cohortātiōnēs suās nōn audīrī intellēxit, ūnam salūtis esse spem
reliquam arbitrātus, proximōs collēs capere atque eō sīgna ferre iussit.
Sed hōs quoque praeoccupat missus ā Saburrā equitātus.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Tum vērō ad summam dēspērātiōnem nostrī perveniunt, et Cn. Domitius,
praefectus equitum, cum paucīs equitibus circumsistēns, Cūriōnem ōrat ut
fugā petat salūtem, et sē ab eō nōn discessūrum pollicētur. At Cūriō
numquam sē,
[[]{#c125_A_First_Latin_Reader_125.xhtml_pagename167}]{#c125_A_First_Latin_Reader_125.xhtml_id-157
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/167"}āmissō exercitū
quem ā Caesare accēpisset, in eius cōnspectum reditūrum coōnfirmat,
atque ita pugnāns interficitur.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Ē proeliō equitēs nostrī perpaucī ēffūgērunt; quibuscum nōnnūllī, quī
equōrum reficiendōrum^[^791]^ causā in itinere paulum morātī erant, fugā
tōtīus exercitūs procul animadversā, incolumēs in castra^[^792]^ sē
contulērunt. Peditēs ad ūnum omnēs interfectī sunt.
:::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
:::

1.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c125_A_First_Latin_Reader_125.xhtml_cite_ref-1-n2099){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**reficiendōrum: reficiō, fēcī, -fectus,**
    *refresh.*]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c125_A_First_Latin_Reader_125.xhtml_cite_note-1-n2101}
2.  [[[[↑]{.mw-linkback-text}](#c125_A_First_Latin_Reader_125.xhtml_cite_ref-2-n2100){rel="mw:referencedBy"}]{.mw-cite-backlink}
    [**castra**: *i.e.* the camp at Castra Cornēlia.]{.mw-reference-text
    .reference-text}]{#c125_A_First_Latin_Reader_125.xhtml_cite_note-2-n2102}
:::::::

:::::::::::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}
::: {.titulusHeaderBox about="#mwt1"}
:::

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}
:::

::::::::::::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
:::::::::::::::: text
::::::::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt19" lang="la"}
[[]{#c126_A_First_Latin_Reader_126_128.xhtml_pagename168}]{#c126_A_First_Latin_Reader_126_128.xhtml_id-158
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/168" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[[SELECTED PASSAGES FROM LATIN\
PROSE
AUTHORS]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

\

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
[[**AN EPISODE FROM THE GALLIC
WAR**]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
[Caesar](https://la.wikisource.org/wiki/Scriptor:Gaius_Iulius_Caesar "Scriptor:Gaius Iulius Caesar"){rel="mw:WikiLink"},
*[Dē Bellō
Gallicō](https://la.wikisource.org/wiki/Commentarii_de_bello_Gallico "Commentarii de bello Gallico"){rel="mw:WikiLink"}*,
[VI](https://la.wikisource.org/wiki/Commentarii_de_bello_Gallico/Liber_VI "Commentarii de bello Gallico/Liber VI"){rel="mw:WikiLink"},
[7,
8](https://la.wikisource.org/wiki/Commentarii_de_bello_Gallico/Liber_VI#7 "Commentarii de bello Gallico/Liber VI"){rel="mw:WikiLink"}.
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

\

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
[[LESSON 126]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

[Though disconcerted for the time being by Caesar's decisive victory
over the Nervii (Lesson 115), the Treveri subsequently more than once
threatened the winter camp of Labienus (cf. Lessons 112 and 116, and see
the map on page 124).]{style="font-size: 83%;"}

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Dum haec ā Caesare geruntur, Trēverī magnīs coāctīs peditātūs
equitātūsque cōpiīs Labiēnum cum ūnā legiōne, quae in eoōrum fīnibus
hiemābat, adorīrī parābant; iamque ab eō nōn longius bīdui viā aberant,
cum duās vēnisse legiōnēs missū Caesaris cōgnōscunt. Positis castrīs ā
mīlibus passuum xv, auxilia Germānōrum exspectāre constituunt.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Labiēnus, hostium cōgnitō cōnsiliō, spērāns temeritāte eorum fore
aliquam dīmicandī facultātem, praesidiō quīnque
[[]{#c126_A_First_Latin_Reader_126_128.xhtml_pagename169}]{#c126_A_First_Latin_Reader_126_128.xhtml_id-159
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/169"}cohortium
impedīmentīs relictō, cum xxv cohortibus magnōque equitātū contrā hostem
proficīscitur, et mīlle passuum intermissō spatiō castra commūnit. Erat
inter Labiēnum atque hostem difficilī trānsitū flūmen rīpīsque
praeruptīs. Hoc neque ipse trānsīre habēbat in animō neque hostēs
trānsitūrōs existimābat. Augebātur auxiliōrum cotīdiē spēs. Loquitur in
cōnsiliō palam, quoniam Germānī appropinquāre dīcantur, sēsē suās
exercitūsque fortūnās in dubium nōn dēvocātūrum, et posterō diē prīmā
lūce castra mōtūrum. Celeriter haec ad hostēs dēferuntur, ut ex magnō
Gallōrum equitātūs numerō nōnnūllōs Gallicīs rēbus favēre nātūra
cōgēbat.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
[[LESSON 127]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*The Enemy are Deceived and become Overconfident*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Labiēnus noctū tribūnīs mīlitum prīmīsque ōrdinibus convocātīs, quid suī
sit cōnsilī, prōpōnit et, quō facilius
[[]{#c126_A_First_Latin_Reader_126_128.xhtml_pagename170}]{#c126_A_First_Latin_Reader_126_128.xhtml_id-160
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/170"}hostibus timōris
det susplciōnem, maiōre strepitū et tumultū, quam populī Rōmānī fert
cōnsuētūdō, castra movērī iubet. Hīs rēbus fugae similem profectiōnem
efficit. Haec quoque per explōrātōrēs ante lūcem in tantā propinquitāte
castrōrum ad hostēs dēferuntur.

Vix agmen novissimum extrā mūnītiōnēs prōcesserat, cum Gallī cohortātī
inter sē, nē spērātam praedam ex manibus dīmitterent
[[——]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
longum esse, perterritīs Rōmānīs, Germānōrum auxilium exspectāre, neque
suam patī dignitātem ut tantīs cōpiīs tam exiguam manum, praesertim
fugientem atque impeditam, adorīrī nōn audeant
[[——]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
flūmen transīre et inīquō locō committere proelium non dubitant. Quae
fore suspicātus Labiēnus, ut omnēs citrā flūmen ēliceret, eādem ūsus
simulātiōne itineris placidē prōgrediēbātur.
[[]{#c126_A_First_Latin_Reader_126_128.xhtml_pagename171}]{#c126_A_First_Latin_Reader_126_128.xhtml_id-161
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/171"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt14" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[LESSON 128]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt14"}
*They are Decisively Beaten*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt14"}

Tum praemissīs paulum impedīments atque in tumulō quōdam collocātis,
“Habētis,” inquit, “mīlitēs, quam petīstis facultātem; hostem impedītō
atque inīquō locō tenētis; praestāte eandem nōbīs ducibus virtūtem, quam
saepenumerō imperātōrī praestitistis, atque illum adesse et haec cōram
cernere existimāte." Simul signa ad hostem convertī aciemque dērigī
iubet; paucīs turmīs praesidiō ad impedīmenta dīmissīs reliquōs equitēs
ad latera dispōnit.

[ ]{about="#mwt14"}

Celeriter nostrī clāmōre sublātō pīla in hostēs inmittunt. Illī ubi
praeter spem, quōs modō fugere crēdēbant, īnfestīs sīgnīs ad sē ire
vidērunt, impetum ferre nōn potuērunt, ac prīmō concursū in fugam
coniectī proximās silvās petivērunt. Quōs Labiēnus equitātū cōnsectātus,
magnō numerō interfectō, complūribus captīs, paucīs post diebus
civitātem recēpit. Nam Germānī, quī auxiliō veniēbant, perceptā
Trēverōrum fugā, sēsē domum receperunt.
:::::::::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
:::

.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/172" about="#mwt21"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

[]{.mw-empty-elt about="#mwt22"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt22"}
[Signa]{.smallcaps}
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt22"}

With these standards compare those shown in the illustrations on page
132. Flags (*vēxilla*) were used for giving signals, and to
differentiate small bodies of troops. In the matter of inspiring loyalty
among the men, their effect was in general very slight as compared with
that of the flag in modern armies.
::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
:::

::::::::::::::::::::

[]{#c127_A_First_Latin_Reader_129_130.xhtml}

:::::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}
::: {.titulusHeaderBox about="#mwt1"}
:::

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}
:::

::::::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
:::::::::: text
:::::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt12" lang="la"}
[[]{#c127_A_First_Latin_Reader_129_130.xhtml_pagename173}]{#c127_A_First_Latin_Reader_129_130.xhtml_id-163
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/173" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[**AN EPISODE FROM THE CIVIL
WAR**]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
[Caesar](https://la.wikisource.org/wiki/Scriptor:Gaius_Iulius_Caesar "Scriptor:Gaius Iulius Caesar"){rel="mw:WikiLink"},
*[Dē Bellō
Cīvīllī](https://la.wikisource.org/wiki/Commentarii_de_bello_civili "Commentarii de bello civili"){rel="mw:WikiLink"}*,
[III](https://la.wikisource.org/wiki/Commentarii_de_bello_civili/Liber_III "Commentarii de bello civili/Liber III"){rel="mw:WikiLink"},
[95-98](https://la.wikisource.org/wiki/Commentarii_de_bello_civili/Liber_III#95 "Commentarii de bello civili/Liber III"){rel="mw:WikiLink"}
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

\

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
[[LESSON 129]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

[When, in 49 [b.c.]{.smallcaps}, Caesar marched some of his troops south
into Italy, and thus precipitated the civil war between himself and
Pompey (cf. the episode in Lessons 117-125), Pompey was taken by
surprise, and retired into Greece. In the decisive battle of Pharsalus,
fought there in the following year, Caesar gained the first advantage,
driving the Pompeians back to the shelter of their
ramparts.]{style="font-size: 83%;"}

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Caesar, Pompēiānīs ex fugā intrā vāllum compulsīs, nūllum spatium
perterritīs darī oportēre existimāns, mīlitēs cohortātus est ut
beneficiō Fortūnae ūterentur castraque oppugnārent. Quī, etsī magnō
aestū fatlgātī
[[——]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
nam ad merīdiem rēs erat perducta
[[——]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
tamen ad omnem labōrem animō parātī, imperiō paruērunt.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Castra ā cohortibus, quae ibi praesidiō erant relictae, īndustriē
dēfendēbantur, multō etiam ācrius ā Thrācibus barbarīsque auxiliīs. Nam
quī ex aciē refūgerant mīlitēs, et animō perterritī et lassitūdine
cōnfectī, missīs plērīque
[[]{#c127_A_First_Latin_Reader_129_130.xhtml_pagename174}]{#c127_A_First_Latin_Reader_129_130.xhtml_id-164
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/174"}armīs sīgnīsque
mīlitāribus, magis dē reliquā fugā quam dē castrōrum dēfensiōne
cōgitābant. Neque vērō diūtius, quī in vāllō cōnstiterant, multitūdinem
tēlōrum sustinēre potuērunt, sed cōnfectī vulneribus locum rellquērunt,
prōtinusque omnēs, ducibus ūsī centuriōnibus tribūnīsque mīlitum, in
altissimōs montēs, quī ad castra pertinēbant, cōnfūgērunt.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Caesar, castrīs potitus, ā mīlitibus contendit nē, in praedā occupātī,
reliquī negōtī gerendī facultātem dīmitterent. Quā rē impetrātā, montem
opere circummūnīre instituit.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
[[LESSON 130]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
*Unconditional Surrender of the Pompeians*
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Pompēiānī, quod is mōns erat sine aquā, diffīsī el locō, relictō monte,
ūniversī iugīs eius Lārīsam versus sē recipere coepērunt. Quā rē
animadversā, Caesar cōpiās suās dīvīsit,
[[]{#c127_A_First_Latin_Reader_129_130.xhtml_pagename175}]{#c127_A_First_Latin_Reader_129_130.xhtml_id-165
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/175"}partemque legiōnum
in castrīs Pompēī remanēre iussit, partem in sua castra remīsit, IV
sēcum legiōnēs dūxit, commodiōreque itinere Pompēiānīs occurrere coepit,
et progressus mīlia passuum VI, aciem īnstrūxit. Quā rē animadversā,
Pompēiānī in quōdam monte constitērunt. Hunc montem flūmen subluēbat.
Caesar mīlitēs cohortātus, etsī tōtius diēī continentī labōre erant
cōnfectī noxque iam suberat, tamen mūnitiōne flūmen ā monte sēclūsit, nē
noctū aquārī Pompēiānī possent.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Quō perfectō opere, illī dē dēditiōne missīs lēgātīs agere coepērunt.
Paucī ōrdinis senātōriī, quī sē cum hīs coniūnxerant, nocte fugā salūtem
petīvērunt. Caesar prīmā lūce omnēs eōs, quī in monte cōnsēderant, ex
superiōribus locīs in plānitiem dēscendere atque arma prōicere iussit.
Quod ubi sine recūsātiōne fēcērunt, passīsque palmīs proiectī ad terram
flentēs ab eō salūtem petīvērunt, cōnsolātus cōnsurgere iussit et pauca
apud eōs dē lēnitāte suā locūtus, quō minōre essent timōre, omnēs
cōnservāvit.
::::::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
:::
::::::::::
:::::::::::
::::::::::::::

[]{#c128_A_First_Latin_Reader_131.xhtml}

::::::::::::::: {.section mw-section-id="0"}
::: {.titulusHeaderBox about="#mwt1"}
:::

::: {title="beginning" about="#mwt1"}
:::

:::::::::::: {.text about="#mwt1"}
::::::::::: text
:::::: {.prp-pages-output typeof="mw:Extension/pages" about="#mwt12" lang="la"}
[[]{#c128_A_First_Latin_Reader_131.xhtml_pagename176}]{#c128_A_First_Latin_Reader_131.xhtml_id-166
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/176" about="#mwt3"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4" typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
[[**THE DEATH OF
CAESAR**]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
([Suetonius](https://la.wikisource.org/wiki/Scriptor:Gaius_Suetonius_Tranquillus "Scriptor:Gaius Suetonius Tranquillus"){rel="mw:WikiLink"},
*[Iūlius](https://la.wikisource.org/wiki/De_vita_Caesarum_libri_VIII/Vita_divi_Iuli "De vita Caesarum libri VIII/Vita divi Iuli"){rel="mw:WikiLink"}*,
[81](https://la.wikisource.org/wiki/De_vita_Caesarum_libri_VIII/Vita_divi_Iuli#%5B81%5D "De vita Caesarum libri VIII/Vita divi Iuli"){rel="mw:WikiLink"},
[82](https://la.wikisource.org/wiki/De_vita_Caesarum_libri_VIII/Vita_divi_Iuli#%5B82%5D "De vita Caesarum libri VIII/Vita divi Iuli"){rel="mw:WikiLink"})
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

\

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  " about="#mwt4"}
[[LESSON 131]{style="font-size:larger"}]{style="font-size:larger"}
:::

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

[As a result of the civil war, Caesar became master of the Roman world.
Many did not approve of his absolute power, and a plot was formed to
take his life. As he left home for the senate house on the fatal day,
some one pushed into his hand a document telling of the conspiracy; but
he did not stop to examine it.]{style="font-size: 83%;"}

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Plūribus hostiīs caesīs, cum litāre nōn posset, introiit cūriam sprētā
religiōne Spurinnamque irrīdēns et ut falsum arguēns, quod sine ūllā suā
noxā Īdus Mārtiae adessent: quamquam is vēnisse quidem eās dīceret, sed
nōn praeterisse. Assidentem cōnspīrātī speciē officiī circumstetērunt;
īlicōque Cimber Tillius, quī prīmās partēs suscēperat, quasi
[[]{#c128_A_First_Latin_Reader_131.xhtml_pagename178}]{#c128_A_First_Latin_Reader_131.xhtml_id-168
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/178"}aliquid rogātūrus
propius accessit, renuentīque et gestū in aliud tempus differentī ab
utrōque umerō togam apprehendedit; deinde clāmantem, “Ista quidem vīs
est,” alter ē Cascīs āversum vulnerat, paulum īnfrā iugulum.

[ ]{about="#mwt4"}

Caesar Cascae bracchium arreptum graphiō trāiēcit, cōnātusque prōsilīre
aliō vulnere tardātus est; utque animadvertit undique sē strīctīs
pūgiōnibus petī, toga caput obvolvit, simul sinistrā manū sīnum ad īma
crūra dēduxit, quō honestius caderet, etiam īnferiōre corporis parte
vēlātā. Atque ita tribus et vigintī plāgīs cōnfossus est, ūnō modō ad
prīmum īctum gemitū sine vōce ēditō; etsī trādidērunt quīdam Mārcō Brūtō
inruentī dīxisse,
“[καὶ]{style="font-family: 'SBL BibLit', 'SBL Greek', Athena, 'EB Garamond 12', 'Foulis Greek', 'Gentium Plus', Cardo, Gentium, Garamond, 'Palatino Linotype', 'Arial Unicode MS', 'Lucida Sans Unicode', 'Lucida Grande', Code2000, sans-serif;"
lang="grc"}
[[]{#c128_A_First_Latin_Reader_131.xhtml_pagename179}]{#c128_A_First_Latin_Reader_131.xhtml_id-169
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/179"}[σύ,
τέκνον]{style="font-family: 'SBL BibLit', 'SBL Greek', Athena, 'EB Garamond 12', 'Foulis Greek', 'Gentium Plus', Cardo, Gentium, Garamond, 'Palatino Linotype', 'Arial Unicode MS', 'Lucida Sans Unicode', 'Lucida Grande', Code2000, sans-serif;"
lang="grc"};” Exanimis, diffugientibus cūnctīs, aliquamdiū iacuit, dōnec
lectīcae impositum, dēpendente bracchiō, trēs servolī domum rettulērunt.
Nec in tot vulneribus, ut Antistius medicus exīstimābat, lētāle ūllum
repertum est, nisi quod secundō locō in pectore accēperat.
::::::

::: {.centertext style="margin-left:0pt; text-align:center; width:100%;  "}
[[————————]{style="color:transparent !important;"}]{style="text-decoration:line-through;"}
:::

[[]{#c128_A_First_Latin_Reader_131.xhtml_pagename177}]{#c128_A_First_Latin_Reader_131.xhtml_id-167
.pagenum title="Pagina:A First Latin Reader.pdf/177" about="#mwt14"
typeof="mw:Transclusion"}
